sn12.1:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.1
sn12.1:0.2 1. Buddhavagga
sn12.1:0.3 Paṭiccasamuppādasutta
sn12.1:1.1 Evaṁ me sutaṁ—
sn12.1:1.2 ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.
sn12.1:1.3 Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi:
sn12.1:1.4 “bhikkhavo”ti.
sn12.1:1.5 “Bhadante”ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.
sn12.1:1.6 Bhagavā etadavoca:
sn12.1:1.7 “paṭiccasamuppādaṁ vo, bhikkhave, desessāmi.
sn12.1:1.8 Taṁ suṇātha, sādhukaṁ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmī”ti.
sn12.1:1.9 “Evaṁ, bhante”ti kho te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.
sn12.1:1.10 Bhagavā etadavoca:
sn12.1:2.1 “Katamo ca, bhikkhave, paṭiccasamuppādo?
sn12.1:2.2 Avijjāpaccayā, bhikkhave, saṅkhārā;
sn12.1:2.3 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ;
sn12.1:2.4 viññāṇapaccayā nāmarūpaṁ;
sn12.1:2.5 nāmarūpapaccayā saḷāyatanaṁ;
sn12.1:2.6 saḷāyatanapaccayā phasso;
sn12.1:2.7 phassapaccayā vedanā;
sn12.1:2.8 vedanāpaccayā taṇhā;
sn12.1:2.9 taṇhāpaccayā upādānaṁ;
sn12.1:2.10 upādānapaccayā bhavo;
sn12.1:2.11 bhavapaccayā jāti;
sn12.1:2.12 jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇaṁ sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsā sambhavanti.
sn12.1:2.13 Evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.1:2.14 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, paṭiccasamuppādo.
sn12.1:3.1 Avijjāya tveva asesavirāganirodhā saṅkhāranirodho;
sn12.1:3.2 saṅkhāranirodhā viññāṇanirodho;
sn12.1:3.3 viññāṇanirodhā nāmarūpanirodho;
sn12.1:3.4 nāmarūpanirodhā saḷāyatananirodho;
sn12.1:3.5 saḷāyatananirodhā phassanirodho;
sn12.1:3.6 phassanirodhā vedanānirodho;
sn12.1:3.7 vedanānirodhā taṇhānirodho;
sn12.1:3.8 taṇhānirodhā upādānanirodho;
sn12.1:3.9 upādānanirodhā bhavanirodho;
sn12.1:3.10 bhavanirodhā jātinirodho;
sn12.1:3.11 jātinirodhā jarāmaraṇaṁ sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsā nirujjhanti.
sn12.1:3.12 Evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hotī”ti.
sn12.1:3.13 Idamavoca bhagavā.
sn12.1:3.14 Attamanā te bhikkhū bhagavato bhāsitaṁ abhinandunti.
sn12.1:3.15 Paṭhamaṁ. "
sn12.2:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.2
sn12.2:0.2 1. Buddhavagga
sn12.2:0.3 Vibhaṅgasutta
sn12.2:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.2:1.2 “Paṭiccasamuppādaṁ vo, bhikkhave, desessāmi vibhajissāmi.
sn12.2:1.3 Taṁ suṇātha, sādhukaṁ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmī”ti.
sn12.2:1.4 “Evaṁ, bhante”ti kho te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.
sn12.2:1.5 Bhagavā etadavoca:
sn12.2:2.1 “Katamo ca, bhikkhave, paṭiccasamuppādo?
sn12.2:2.2 Avijjāpaccayā, bhikkhave, saṅkhārā;
sn12.2:2.3 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ;
sn12.2:2.4 viññāṇapaccayā nāmarūpaṁ;
sn12.2:2.5 nāmarūpapaccayā saḷāyatanaṁ;
sn12.2:2.6 saḷāyatanapaccayā phasso;
sn12.2:2.7 phassapaccayā vedanā;
sn12.2:2.8 vedanāpaccayā taṇhā;
sn12.2:2.9 taṇhāpaccayā upādānaṁ;
sn12.2:2.10 upādānapaccayā bhavo;
sn12.2:2.11 bhavapaccayā jāti;
sn12.2:2.12 jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇaṁ sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsā sambhavanti.
sn12.2:2.13 Evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.2:3.1 Katamañca, bhikkhave, jarāmaraṇaṁ?
sn12.2:3.2 Yā tesaṁ tesaṁ sattānaṁ tamhi tamhi sattanikāye jarā jīraṇatā khaṇḍiccaṁ pāliccaṁ valittacatā āyuno saṁhāni indriyānaṁ paripāko;
sn12.2:3.3 ayaṁ vuccati jarā.
sn12.2:3.4 Yā tesaṁ tesaṁ sattānaṁ tamhā tamhā sattanikāyā cuti cavanatā bhedo antaradhānaṁ maccu maraṇaṁ kālakiriyā khandhānaṁ bhedo kaḷevarassa nikkhepo (…),
sn12.2:3.5 idaṁ vuccati maraṇaṁ.
sn12.2:3.6 Iti ayañca jarā, idañca maraṇaṁ.
sn12.2:3.7 Idaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, jarāmaraṇaṁ.
sn12.2:4.1 Katamā ca, bhikkhave, jāti?
sn12.2:4.2 Yā tesaṁ tesaṁ sattānaṁ tamhi tamhi sattanikāye jāti sañjāti okkanti abhinibbatti khandhānaṁ pātubhāvo āyatanānaṁ paṭilābho.
sn12.2:4.3 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, jāti.
sn12.2:5.1 Katamo ca, bhikkhave, bhavo?
sn12.2:5.2 Tayome, bhikkhave, bhavā—
sn12.2:5.3 kāmabhavo, rūpabhavo, arūpabhavo.
sn12.2:5.4 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, bhavo.
sn12.2:6.1 Katamañca, bhikkhave, upādānaṁ?
sn12.2:6.2 Cattārimāni, bhikkhave, upādānāni—
sn12.2:6.3 kāmupādānaṁ, diṭṭhupādānaṁ, sīlabbatupādānaṁ, attavādupādānaṁ.
sn12.2:6.4 Idaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, upādānaṁ.
sn12.2:7.1 Katamā ca, bhikkhave, taṇhā?
sn12.2:7.2 Chayime, bhikkhave, taṇhākāyā—
sn12.2:7.3 rūpataṇhā, saddataṇhā, gandhataṇhā, rasataṇhā, phoṭṭhabbataṇhā, dhammataṇhā.
sn12.2:7.4 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, taṇhā.
sn12.2:8.1 Katamā ca, bhikkhave, vedanā?
sn12.2:8.2 Chayime, bhikkhave, vedanākāyā—
sn12.2:8.3 cakkhusamphassajā vedanā, sotasamphassajā vedanā, ghānasamphassajā vedanā, jivhāsamphassajā vedanā, kāyasamphassajā vedanā, manosamphassajā vedanā.
sn12.2:8.4 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, vedanā.
sn12.2:9.1 Katamo ca, bhikkhave, phasso?
sn12.2:9.2 Chayime, bhikkhave, phassakāyā—
sn12.2:9.3 cakkhusamphasso, sotasamphasso, ghānasamphasso, jivhāsamphasso, kāyasamphasso, manosamphasso.
sn12.2:9.4 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, phasso.
sn12.2:10.1 Katamañca, bhikkhave, saḷāyatanaṁ?
sn12.2:10.2 Cakkhāyatanaṁ, sotāyatanaṁ, ghānāyatanaṁ, jivhāyatanaṁ, kāyāyatanaṁ, manāyatanaṁ—
sn12.2:10.3 idaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, saḷāyatanaṁ.
sn12.2:11.1 Katamañca, bhikkhave, nāmarūpaṁ?
sn12.2:11.2 Vedanā, saññā, cetanā, phasso, manasikāro—
sn12.2:11.3 idaṁ vuccati nāmaṁ.
sn12.2:11.4 Cattāro ca mahābhūtā, catunnañca mahābhūtānaṁ upādāyarūpaṁ.
sn12.2:11.5 Idaṁ vuccati rūpaṁ.
sn12.2:11.6 Iti idañca nāmaṁ, idañca rūpaṁ.
sn12.2:11.7 Idaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, nāmarūpaṁ.
sn12.2:12.1 Katamañca, bhikkhave, viññāṇaṁ?
sn12.2:12.2 Chayime, bhikkhave, viññāṇakāyā—
sn12.2:12.3 cakkhuviññāṇaṁ, sotaviññāṇaṁ, ghānaviññāṇaṁ, jivhāviññāṇaṁ, kāyaviññāṇaṁ, manoviññāṇaṁ.
sn12.2:12.4 Idaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, viññāṇaṁ.
sn12.2:13.1 Katame ca, bhikkhave, saṅkhārā?
sn12.2:13.2 Tayome, bhikkhave, saṅkhārā—
sn12.2:13.3 kāyasaṅkhāro, vacīsaṅkhāro, cittasaṅkhāro.
sn12.2:13.4 Ime vuccanti, bhikkhave, saṅkhārā.
sn12.2:14.1 Katamā ca, bhikkhave, avijjā?
sn12.2:14.2 Yaṁ kho, bhikkhave, dukkhe aññāṇaṁ, dukkhasamudaye aññāṇaṁ, dukkhanirodhe aññāṇaṁ, dukkhanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya aññāṇaṁ.
sn12.2:14.3 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, avijjā.
sn12.2:15.1 Iti kho, bhikkhave, avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā;
sn12.2:15.2 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ …pe…
sn12.2:15.3 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.2:15.4 Avijjāya tveva asesavirāganirodhā saṅkhāranirodho;
sn12.2:15.5 saṅkhāranirodhā viññāṇanirodho …pe…
sn12.2:15.6 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hotī”ti.
sn12.2:15.7 Dutiyaṁ. "

sn12.4:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.4
sn12.4:0.2 1. Buddhavagga
sn12.4:0.3 Vipassīsutta
sn12.4:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati …pe…
sn12.4:1.2 “vipassissa, bhikkhave, bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa pubbeva sambodhā anabhisambuddhassa bodhisattasseva sato etadahosi:
sn12.4:1.3 ‘kicchaṁ vatāyaṁ loko āpanno jāyati ca jīyati ca mīyati ca cavati ca upapajjati ca.
sn12.4:1.4 Atha ca panimassa dukkhassa nissaraṇaṁ nappajānāti jarāmaraṇassa.
sn12.4:1.5 Kudāssu nāma imassa dukkhassa nissaraṇaṁ paññāyissati jarāmaraṇassā’ti?
sn12.4:2.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:2.2 ‘kimhi nu kho sati jarāmaraṇaṁ hoti, kiṁpaccayā jarāmaraṇan’ti?
sn12.4:2.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:2.4 ‘jātiyā kho sati jarāmaraṇaṁ hoti, jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇan’ti.
sn12.4:3.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:3.2 ‘kimhi nu kho sati jāti hoti, kiṁpaccayā jātī’ti?
sn12.4:3.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:3.4 ‘bhave kho sati jāti hoti, bhavapaccayā jātī’ti.
sn12.4:4.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:4.2 ‘kimhi nu kho sati bhavo hoti, kiṁpaccayā bhavo’ti?
sn12.4:4.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:4.4 ‘upādāne kho sati bhavo hoti, upādānapaccayā bhavo’ti.
sn12.4:5.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:5.2 ‘kimhi nu kho sati upādānaṁ hoti, kiṁpaccayā upādānan’ti?
sn12.4:5.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:5.4 ‘taṇhāya kho sati upādānaṁ hoti, taṇhāpaccayā upādānan’ti.
sn12.4:6.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:6.2 ‘kimhi nu kho sati taṇhā hoti, kiṁpaccayā taṇhā’ti?
sn12.4:6.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:6.4 ‘vedanāya kho sati taṇhā hoti, vedanāpaccayā taṇhā’ti.
sn12.4:7.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:7.2 ‘kimhi nu kho sati vedanā hoti, kiṁpaccayā vedanā’ti?
sn12.4:7.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:7.4 ‘phasse kho sati vedanā hoti, phassapaccayā vedanā’ti.
sn12.4:8.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:8.2 ‘kimhi nu kho sati phasso hoti, kiṁpaccayā phasso’ti?
sn12.4:8.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:8.4 ‘saḷāyatane kho sati phasso hoti, saḷāyatanapaccayā phasso’ti.
sn12.4:9.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:9.2 ‘kimhi nu kho sati saḷāyatanaṁ hoti, kiṁpaccayā saḷāyatanan’ti?
sn12.4:9.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:9.4 ‘nāmarūpe kho sati saḷāyatanaṁ hoti, nāmarūpapaccayā saḷāyatanan’ti.
sn12.4:10.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:10.2 ‘kimhi nu kho sati nāmarūpaṁ hoti, kiṁpaccayā nāmarūpan’ti?
sn12.4:10.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:10.4 ‘viññāṇe kho sati nāmarūpaṁ hoti, viññāṇapaccayā nāmarūpan’ti.
sn12.4:11.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:11.2 ‘kimhi nu kho sati viññāṇaṁ hoti, kiṁpaccayā viññāṇan’ti?
sn12.4:11.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:11.4 ‘saṅkhāresu kho sati viññāṇaṁ hoti, saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇan’ti.
sn12.4:12.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:12.2 ‘kimhi nu kho sati saṅkhārā honti, kiṁpaccayā saṅkhārā’ti?
sn12.4:12.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:12.4 ‘avijjāya kho sati saṅkhārā honti, avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā’ti.
sn12.4:13.1 Iti hidaṁ avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā;
sn12.4:13.2 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ …pe…
sn12.4:13.3 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.4:13.4 ‘Samudayo, samudayo’ti kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhuṁ udapādi, ñāṇaṁ udapādi, paññā udapādi, vijjā udapādi, āloko udapādi.
sn12.4:14.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:14.2 ‘kimhi nu kho asati jarāmaraṇaṁ na hoti, kissa nirodhā jarāmaraṇanirodho’ti?
sn12.4:14.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:14.4 ‘jātiyā kho asati jarāmaraṇaṁ na hoti, jātinirodhā jarāmaraṇanirodho’ti.
sn12.4:15.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:15.2 ‘kimhi nu kho asati jāti na hoti, kissa nirodhā jātinirodho’ti?
sn12.4:15.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:15.4 ‘bhave kho asati jāti na hoti, bhavanirodhā jātinirodho’ti.
sn12.4:16.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:16.2 ‘kimhi nu kho asati bhavo na hoti, kissa nirodhā bhavanirodho’ti?
sn12.4:16.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:16.4 ‘upādāne kho asati bhavo na hoti, upādānanirodhā bhavanirodho’ti.
sn12.4:17.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:17.2 ‘kimhi nu kho asati upādānaṁ na hoti, kissa nirodhā upādānanirodho’ti?
sn12.4:17.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:17.4 ‘taṇhāya kho asati upādānaṁ na hoti, taṇhānirodhā upādānanirodho’ti.
sn12.4:18.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:18.2 ‘kimhi nu kho asati taṇhā na hoti, kissa nirodhā taṇhānirodho’ti?
sn12.4:18.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:18.4 ‘vedanāya kho asati taṇhā na hoti, vedanānirodhā taṇhānirodho’ti.
sn12.4:19.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:19.2 ‘kimhi nu kho asati vedanā na hoti, kissa nirodhā vedanānirodho’ti?
sn12.4:19.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:19.4 ‘phasse kho asati vedanā na hoti, phassanirodhā vedanānirodho’ti.
sn12.4:20.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:20.2 ‘kimhi nu kho asati phasso na hoti, kissa nirodhā phassanirodho’ti?
sn12.4:20.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.4:20.4 ‘saḷāyatane kho asati phasso na hoti, saḷāyatananirodhā phassanirodho’ti.
sn12.4:21.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa etadahosi:
sn12.4:21.2 ‘kimhi nu kho asati saḷāyatanaṁ na hoti, kissa nirodhā saḷāyatananirodho’ti?
sn12.4:21.3 Atha kho, bhikkhave, vipassissa bodhisattassa yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:

sn12.11:1.1 Evaṁ me sutaṁ—

sn12.11:1.3 “cattārome, bhikkhave, āhārā bhūtānaṁ vā sattānaṁ ṭhitiyā sambhavesīnaṁ vā anuggahāya.
sn12.11:1.4 Katame cattāro?
sn12.11:1.5 Kabaḷīkāro āhāro oḷāriko vā sukhumo vā, phasso dutiyo, manosañcetanā tatiyā, viññāṇaṁ catutthaṁ.
sn12.11:1.6 Ime kho, bhikkhave, cattāro āhārā bhūtānaṁ vā sattānaṁ ṭhitiyā sambhavesīnaṁ vā anuggahāya.
sn12.11:2.1 Ime, bhikkhave, cattāro āhārā kiṁnidānā kiṁsamudayā kiṁjātikā kiṁpabhavā?
sn12.11:2.2 Ime cattāro āhārā taṇhānidānā taṇhāsamudayā taṇhājātikā taṇhāpabhavā.
sn12.11:2.3 Taṇhā cāyaṁ, bhikkhave, kiṁnidānā kiṁsamudayā kiṁjātikā kiṁpabhavā?
sn12.11:2.4 Taṇhā vedanānidānā vedanāsamudayā vedanājātikā vedanāpabhavā.
sn12.11:2.5 Vedanā cāyaṁ, bhikkhave, kiṁnidānā kiṁsamudayā kiṁjātikā kiṁpabhavā?
sn12.11:2.6 Vedanā phassanidānā phassasamudayā phassajātikā phassapabhavā.
sn12.11:2.7 Phasso cāyaṁ, bhikkhave, kiṁnidāno kiṁsamudayo kiṁjātiko kiṁpabhavo?
sn12.11:2.8 Phasso saḷāyatananidāno saḷāyatanasamudayo saḷāyatanajātiko saḷāyatanapabhavo.
sn12.11:2.9 Saḷāyatanañcidaṁ, bhikkhave, kiṁnidānaṁ kiṁsamudayaṁ kiṁjātikaṁ kiṁpabhavaṁ?
sn12.11:2.10 Saḷāyatanaṁ nāmarūpanidānaṁ nāmarūpasamudayaṁ nāmarūpajātikaṁ nāmarūpapabhavaṁ.
sn12.11:2.11 Nāmarūpañcidaṁ, bhikkhave, kiṁnidānaṁ kiṁsamudayaṁ kiṁjātikaṁ kiṁpabhavaṁ?
sn12.11:2.12 Nāmarūpaṁ viññāṇanidānaṁ viññāṇasamudayaṁ viññāṇajātikaṁ viññāṇapabhavaṁ.
sn12.11:2.13 Viññāṇañcidaṁ, bhikkhave, kiṁnidānaṁ kiṁsamudayaṁ kiṁjātikaṁ kiṁpabhavaṁ?
sn12.11:2.14 Viññāṇaṁ saṅkhāranidānaṁ saṅkhārasamudayaṁ saṅkhārajātikaṁ saṅkhārapabhavaṁ.
sn12.11:2.15 Saṅkhārā cime, bhikkhave, kiṁnidānā kiṁsamudayā kiṁjātikā kiṁpabhavā?
sn12.11:2.16 Saṅkhārā avijjānidānā avijjāsamudayā avijjājātikā avijjāpabhavā.
sn12.11:3.1 Iti kho, bhikkhave, avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā;

sn12.11:3.5 saṅkhāranirodhā viññāṇanirodho …pe…
sn12.11:3.6 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hotī”ti.

sn12.13:2.12 te kho me, bhikkhave, samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samaṇesu ceva samaṇasammatā brāhmaṇesu ca brāhmaṇasammatā; te ca panāyasmanto sāmaññatthañca brahmaññatthañca diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharantī”ti.

sn12.14:0.3 Dutiyasamaṇabrāhmaṇasutta
sn12.14:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.14:1.2 “Ye hi keci, bhikkhave, samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā ime dhamme nappajānanti, imesaṁ dhammānaṁ samudayaṁ nappajānanti, imesaṁ dhammānaṁ nirodhaṁ nappajānanti, imesaṁ dhammānaṁ nirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ nappajānanti, katame dhamme nappajānanti, katamesaṁ dhammānaṁ samudayaṁ nappajānanti, katamesaṁ dhammānaṁ nirodhaṁ nappajānanti, katamesaṁ dhammānaṁ nirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ nappajānanti?
sn12.14:2.1 Jarāmaraṇaṁ nappajānanti, jarāmaraṇasamudayaṁ nappajānanti, jarāmaraṇanirodhaṁ nappajānanti, jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ nappajānanti;
sn12.14:2.2 jātiṁ …pe…
sn12.14:2.3 bhavaṁ …
sn12.14:2.4 upādānaṁ …
sn12.14:2.5 taṇhaṁ …
sn12.14:2.6 vedanaṁ …
sn12.14:2.7 phassaṁ …
sn12.14:2.8 saḷāyatanaṁ …
sn12.14:2.9 nāmarūpaṁ …
sn12.14:2.10 viññāṇaṁ …
sn12.14:2.11 saṅkhāre nappajānanti, saṅkhārasamudayaṁ nappajānanti, saṅkhāranirodhaṁ nappajānanti, saṅkhāranirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ nappajānanti.
sn12.14:2.12 Ime dhamme nappajānanti, imesaṁ dhammānaṁ samudayaṁ nappajānanti, imesaṁ dhammānaṁ nirodhaṁ nappajānanti, imesaṁ dhammānaṁ nirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ nappajānanti.
sn12.14:2.13 Na me te, bhikkhave, samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samaṇesu vā samaṇasammatā brāhmaṇesu vā brāhmaṇasammatā, na ca pana te āyasmanto sāmaññatthaṁ vā brahmaññatthaṁ vā diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharanti.
sn12.14:3.1 Ye ca kho keci, bhikkhave, samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā ime dhamme pajānanti, imesaṁ dhammānaṁ samudayaṁ pajānanti, imesaṁ dhammānaṁ nirodhaṁ pajānanti, imesaṁ dhammānaṁ nirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ pajānanti, katame dhamme pajānanti, katamesaṁ dhammānaṁ samudayaṁ pajānanti, katamesaṁ dhammānaṁ nirodhaṁ pajānanti, katamesaṁ dhammānaṁ nirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ pajānanti?
sn12.14:4.1 Jarāmaraṇaṁ pajānanti, jarāmaraṇasamudayaṁ pajānanti, jarāmaraṇanirodhaṁ pajānanti, jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ pajānanti;
sn12.14:4.2 jātiṁ …pe…
sn12.14:4.3 bhavaṁ …

sn12.14:4.5 taṇhaṁ …
sn12.14:4.6 vedanaṁ …
sn12.14:4.7 phassaṁ …
sn12.14:4.8 saḷāyatanaṁ …
sn12.14:4.9 nāmarūpaṁ …
sn12.14:4.10 viññāṇaṁ …
sn12.14:4.11 saṅkhāre pajānanti, saṅkhārasamudayaṁ pajānanti, saṅkhāranirodhaṁ pajānanti, saṅkhāranirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ pajānanti.
sn12.14:4.12 Ime dhamme pajānanti, imesaṁ dhammānaṁ samudayaṁ pajānanti, imesaṁ dhammānaṁ nirodhaṁ pajānanti, imesaṁ dhammānaṁ nirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ pajānanti.
sn12.14:4.13 Te kho me, bhikkhave, samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samaṇesu ceva samaṇasammatā, brāhmaṇesu ca brāhmaṇasammatā. Te ca panāyasmanto sāmaññatthañca brahmaññatthañca diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharantī”ti.

sn12.15:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.15
sn12.15:0.2 2. Āhāravagga
sn12.15:0.3 Kaccānagottasutta
sn12.15:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.15:1.2 Atha kho āyasmā kaccānagotto yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā kaccānagotto bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.15:1.3 “‘sammādiṭṭhi sammādiṭṭhī’ti, bhante, vuccati.
sn12.15:1.4 Kittāvatā nu kho, bhante, sammādiṭṭhi hotī”ti?
sn12.15:2.1 “Dvayanissito khvāyaṁ, kaccāna, loko yebhuyyena—atthitañceva natthitañca.
sn12.15:2.2 Lokasamudayaṁ kho, kaccāna, yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passato yā loke natthitā sā na hoti.
sn12.15:2.3 Lokanirodhaṁ kho, kaccāna, yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passato yā loke atthitā sā na hoti.
sn12.15:2.4 Upayupādānābhinivesavinibandho khvāyaṁ, kaccāna, loko yebhuyyena.
sn12.15:2.5 Tañcāyaṁ upayupādānaṁ cetaso adhiṭṭhānaṁ abhinivesānusayaṁ na upeti na upādiyati nādhiṭṭhāti: ‘attā me’ti.
sn12.15:2.6 ‘Dukkhameva uppajjamānaṁ uppajjati, dukkhaṁ nirujjhamānaṁ nirujjhatī’ti na kaṅkhati na vicikicchati aparapaccayā ñāṇamevassa ettha hoti.
sn12.15:2.7 Ettāvatā kho, kaccāna, sammādiṭṭhi hoti.
sn12.15:3.1 ‘Sabbamatthī’ti kho, kaccāna, ayameko anto.
sn12.15:3.2 ‘Sabbaṁ natthī’ti ayaṁ dutiyo anto.
sn12.15:3.3 Ete te, kaccāna, ubho ante anupagamma majjhena tathāgato dhammaṁ deseti:
sn12.15:3.4 ‘avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā;
sn12.15:3.5 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ …pe…
sn12.15:3.6 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.15:3.7 Avijjāya tveva asesavirāganirodhā saṅkhāranirodho;
sn12.15:3.8 saṅkhāranirodhā viññāṇanirodho …pe…
sn12.15:3.9 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hotī’”ti.
sn12.15:3.10 Pañcamaṁ. "
sn12.16:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.16
sn12.16:0.2 2. Āhāravagga
sn12.16:0.3 Dhammakathikasutta
sn12.16:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ …
sn12.16:1.2 Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho so bhikkhu bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.16:1.3 “‘dhammakathiko dhammakathiko’ti, bhante, vuccati.
sn12.16:1.4 Kittāvatā nu kho, bhante, dhammakathiko hotī”ti?
sn12.16:2.1 “Jarāmaraṇassa ce bhikkhu nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya dhammaṁ deseti, ‘dhammakathiko bhikkhū’ti alaṁvacanāya.
sn12.16:2.2 Jarāmaraṇassa ce bhikkhu nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya paṭipanno hoti, ‘dhammānudhammappaṭipanno bhikkhū’ti alaṁvacanāya.
sn12.16:2.3 Jarāmaraṇassa ce bhikkhu nibbidā virāgā nirodhā anupādāvimutto hoti, ‘diṭṭhadhammanibbānappatto bhikkhū’ti alaṁvacanāya.
sn12.16:3.1 Jātiyā ce bhikkhu …pe…
sn12.16:3.2 bhavassa ce bhikkhu …
sn12.16:3.3 upādānassa ce bhikkhu …
sn12.16:3.4 taṇhāya ce bhikkhu …
sn12.16:3.5 vedanāya ce bhikkhu …
sn12.16:3.6 phassassa ce bhikkhu …
sn12.16:3.7 saḷāyatanassa ce bhikkhu …
sn12.16:3.8 nāmarūpassa ce bhikkhu …
sn12.16:3.9 viññāṇassa ce bhikkhu …
sn12.16:3.10 saṅkhārānañce bhikkhu …
sn12.16:3.11 avijjāya ce bhikkhu nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya dhammaṁ deseti, ‘dhammakathiko bhikkhū’ti alaṁvacanāya.
sn12.16:3.12 Avijjāya ce bhikkhu nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya paṭipanno hoti, ‘dhammānudhammappaṭipanno bhikkhū’ti alaṁvacanāya.
sn12.16:3.13 Avijjāya ce bhikkhu nibbidā virāgā nirodhā anupādāvimutto hoti, ‘diṭṭhadhammanibbānappatto bhikkhū’ti alaṁvacanāyā”ti.
sn12.16:3.14 Chaṭṭhaṁ. "
sn12.17:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.17
sn12.17:0.2 2. Āhāravagga
sn12.17:0.3 Acelakassapasutta
sn12.17:1.1 Evaṁ me sutaṁ—
sn12.17:1.2 ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe.
sn12.17:1.3 Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṁ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya rājagahaṁ piṇḍāya pāvisi.
sn12.17:1.4 Addasā kho acelo kassapo bhagavantaṁ dūratova āgacchantaṁ.
sn12.17:1.5 Disvāna yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn12.17:1.6 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṁ ṭhito kho acelo kassapo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.17:1.7 “puccheyyāma mayaṁ bhavantaṁ gotamaṁ kañcideva desaṁ, sace no bhavaṁ gotamo okāsaṁ karoti pañhassa veyyākaraṇāyā”ti.
sn12.17:1.8 “Akālo kho tāva, kassapa, pañhassa;
sn12.17:1.9 antaragharaṁ paviṭṭhamhā”ti.
sn12.17:2.1 Dutiyampi kho acelo kassapo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.17:2.2 “puccheyyāma mayaṁ bhavantaṁ gotamaṁ kañcideva desaṁ, sace no bhavaṁ gotamo okāsaṁ karoti pañhassa veyyākaraṇāyā”ti.
sn12.17:2.3 “Akālo kho tāva, kassapa, pañhassa;
sn12.17:2.4 antaragharaṁ paviṭṭhamhā”ti.
sn12.17:2.5 Tatiyampi kho acelo kassapo …pe…
sn12.17:2.6 antaragharaṁ paviṭṭhamhāti.
sn12.17:2.7 Evaṁ vutte, acelo kassapo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.17:2.8 “na kho pana mayaṁ bhavantaṁ gotamaṁ bahudeva pucchitukāmā”ti.
sn12.17:2.9 “Puccha, kassapa, yadākaṅkhasī”ti.
sn12.17:3.1 “Kiṁ nu kho, bho gotama, ‘sayaṅkataṁ dukkhan’ti?
sn12.17:3.2 ‘Mā hevaṁ, kassapā’ti bhagavā avoca.
sn12.17:3.3 ‘Kiṁ pana, bho gotama, paraṅkataṁ dukkhan’ti?
sn12.17:3.4 ‘Mā hevaṁ, kassapā’ti bhagavā avoca.
sn12.17:3.5 ‘Kiṁ nu kho, bho gotama, sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca dukkhan’ti?
sn12.17:3.6 ‘Mā hevaṁ, kassapā’ti bhagavā avoca.
sn12.17:3.7 ‘Kiṁ pana, bho gotama, asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ dukkhan’ti?
sn12.17:3.8 ‘Mā hevaṁ, kassapā’ti bhagavā avoca.
sn12.17:3.9 ‘Kiṁ nu kho, bho gotama, natthi dukkhan’ti?
sn12.17:3.10 ‘Na kho, kassapa, natthi dukkhaṁ.
sn12.17:3.11 Atthi kho, kassapa, dukkhan’ti.
sn12.17:3.12 ‘Tena hi bhavaṁ gotamo dukkhaṁ na jānāti, na passatī’ti.
sn12.17:3.13 ‘Na khvāhaṁ, kassapa, dukkhaṁ na jānāmi, na passāmi.
sn12.17:3.14 Jānāmi khvāhaṁ, kassapa, dukkhaṁ;
sn12.17:3.15 passāmi khvāhaṁ, kassapa, dukkhan’”ti.
sn12.17:4.1 “Kiṁ nu kho, bho gotama, ‘sayaṅkataṁ dukkhan’ti iti puṭṭho samāno ‘mā hevaṁ, kassapā’ti vadesi.
sn12.17:4.2 ‘Kiṁ pana, bho gotama, paraṅkataṁ dukkhan’ti iti puṭṭho samāno ‘mā hevaṁ, kassapā’ti vadesi.
sn12.17:4.3 ‘Kiṁ nu kho, bho gotama, sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca dukkhan’ti iti puṭṭho samāno ‘mā hevaṁ, kassapā’ti vadesi.
sn12.17:4.4 ‘Kiṁ pana, bho gotama, asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ dukkhan’ti iti puṭṭho samāno ‘mā hevaṁ, kassapā’ti vadesi.
sn12.17:4.5 ‘Kiṁ nu kho, bho gotama, natthi dukkhan’ti iti puṭṭho samāno ‘na kho, kassapa, natthi dukkhaṁ, atthi kho, kassapa, dukkhan’ti vadesi.
sn12.17:4.6 ‘Tena hi bhavaṁ gotamo dukkhaṁ na jānāti na passatī’ti iti puṭṭho samāno ‘na khvāhaṁ, kassapa, dukkhaṁ na jānāmi na passāmi.
sn12.17:4.7 Jānāmi khvāhaṁ, kassapa, dukkhaṁ;
sn12.17:4.8 passāmi khvāhaṁ, kassapa, dukkhan’ti vadesi.
sn12.17:4.9 Ācikkhatu ca me, bhante, bhagavā dukkhaṁ.
sn12.17:4.10 Desetu ca me, bhante, bhagavā dukkhan”ti.
sn12.17:5.1 “‘So karoti so paṭisaṁvedayatī’ti kho, kassapa, ādito sato ‘sayaṅkataṁ dukkhan’ti iti vadaṁ sassataṁ etaṁ pareti.
sn12.17:5.2 ‘Añño karoti añño paṭisaṁvedayatī’ti kho, kassapa, vedanābhitunnassa sato ‘paraṅkataṁ dukkhan’ti iti vadaṁ ucchedaṁ etaṁ pareti.
sn12.17:5.3 Ete te, kassapa, ubho ante anupagamma majjhena tathāgato dhammaṁ deseti:
sn12.17:5.4 ‘avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā;
sn12.17:5.5 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ …pe…
sn12.17:5.6 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.17:5.7 Avijjāya tveva asesavirāganirodhā saṅkhāranirodho;
sn12.17:5.8 saṅkhāranirodhā viññāṇanirodho …pe…
sn12.17:5.9 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hotī’”ti.
sn12.17:6.1 Evaṁ vutte, acelo kassapo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.17:6.2 “abhikkantaṁ, bhante, abhikkantaṁ, bhante.
sn12.17:6.3 Seyyathāpi, bhante, nikkujjitaṁ vā ukkujjeyya …pe… ‘cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhantī’ti; evamevaṁ bhagavatā anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito.
sn12.17:6.4 Esāhaṁ, bhante, bhagavantaṁ saraṇaṁ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca.
sn12.17:6.5 Labheyyāhaṁ, bhante, bhagavato santike pabbajjaṁ, labheyyaṁ upasampadan”ti.
sn12.17:7.1 “Yo kho, kassapa, aññatitthiyapubbo imasmiṁ dhammavinaye ākaṅkhati pabbajjaṁ, ākaṅkhati upasampadaṁ, so cattāro māse parivasati. Catunnaṁ māsānaṁ accayena āraddhacittā bhikkhū pabbājenti upasampādenti bhikkhubhāvāya.
sn12.17:7.2 Api ca mayā puggalavemattatā viditā”ti.
sn12.17:8.1 “Sace, bhante, aññatitthiyapubbo imasmiṁ dhammavinaye ākaṅkhati pabbajjaṁ, ākaṅkhati upasampadaṁ, cattāro māse parivasati. Catunnaṁ māsānaṁ accayena āraddhacittā bhikkhū pabbājenti upasampādenti bhikkhubhāvāya. Ahaṁ cattāri vassāni parivasissāmi, catunnaṁ vassānaṁ accayena āraddhacittā bhikkhū pabbājentu upasampādentu bhikkhubhāvāyā”ti.
sn12.17:9.1 Alattha kho acelo kassapo bhagavato santike pabbajjaṁ, alattha upasampadaṁ.
sn12.17:9.2 Acirūpasampanno ca panāyasmā kassapo eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto nacirasseva—yassatthāya kulaputtā sammadeva agārasmā anagāriyaṁ pabbajanti tadanuttaraṁ—brahmacariyapariyosānaṁ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi.
sn12.17:9.3 “Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā”ti abbhaññāsi.
sn12.17:9.4 Aññataro ca panāyasmā kassapo arahataṁ ahosīti.
sn12.17:9.5 Sattamaṁ. "
sn12.18:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.18
sn12.18:0.2 2. Āhāravagga
sn12.18:0.3 Timbarukasutta
sn12.18:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.18:1.2 Atha kho timbaruko paribbājako yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn12.18:1.3 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho timbaruko paribbājako bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.18:2.1 “Kiṁ nu kho, bho gotama, sayaṅkataṁ sukhadukkhanti?
sn12.18:2.2 Mā hevaṁ, timbarukāti bhagavā avoca.
sn12.18:2.3 Kiṁ pana, bho gotama, paraṅkataṁ sukhadukkhanti?
sn12.18:2.4 Mā hevaṁ, timbarukāti bhagavā avoca.
sn12.18:2.5 Kiṁ nu kho, bho gotama, sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca sukhadukkhanti?
sn12.18:2.6 Mā hevaṁ, timbarukāti bhagavā avoca.
sn12.18:2.7 Kiṁ pana, bho gotama, asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ sukhadukkhanti?
sn12.18:2.8 Mā hevaṁ, timbarukāti bhagavā avoca.
sn12.18:2.9 Kiṁ nu kho, bho gotama, natthi sukhadukkhanti?
sn12.18:2.10 Na kho, timbaruka, natthi sukhadukkhaṁ;
sn12.18:2.11 atthi kho, timbaruka, sukhadukkhanti.
sn12.18:2.12 Tena hi bhavaṁ gotamo sukhadukkhaṁ na jānāti, na passatīti?
sn12.18:2.13 Na khvāhaṁ, timbaruka, sukhadukkhaṁ na jānāmi, na passāmi.
sn12.18:2.14 Jānāmi khvāhaṁ, timbaruka, sukhadukkhaṁ;
sn12.18:2.15 passāmi khvāhaṁ, timbaruka, sukhadukkhan”ti.
sn12.18:3.1 “‘Kiṁ nu kho, bho gotama, sayaṅkataṁ sukhadukkhan’ti iti puṭṭho samāno ‘mā hevaṁ, timbarukā’ti vadesi.
sn12.18:3.2 ‘Kiṁ pana, bho gotama, paraṅkataṁ sukhadukkhan’ti iti puṭṭho samāno ‘mā hevaṁ, timbarukā’ti vadesi.
sn12.18:3.3 ‘Kiṁ nu kho, bho gotama, sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca sukhadukkhan’ti iti puṭṭho samāno ‘mā hevaṁ, timbarukā’ti vadesi.
sn12.18:3.4 ‘Kiṁ pana, bho gotama, asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ sukhadukkhan’ti iti puṭṭho samāno ‘mā hevaṁ, timbarukā’ti vadesi.
sn12.18:3.5 ‘Kiṁ nu kho, bho gotama, natthi sukhadukkhan’ti iti puṭṭho samāno ‘na kho, timbaruka, natthi sukhadukkhaṁ;
sn12.18:3.6 atthi kho, timbaruka, sukhadukkhan’ti vadesi.
sn12.18:3.7 ‘Tena hi bhavaṁ gotamo sukhadukkhaṁ na jānāti, na passatī’ti iti puṭṭho samāno ‘na khvāhaṁ, timbaruka, sukhadukkhaṁ na jānāmi, na passāmi.
sn12.18:3.8 Jānāmi khvāhaṁ, timbaruka, sukhadukkhaṁ;
sn12.18:3.9 passāmi khvāhaṁ, timbaruka, sukhadukkhan’ti vadesi.
sn12.18:3.10 Ācikkhatu ca me bhavaṁ gotamo sukhadukkhaṁ.
sn12.18:3.11 Desetu ca me bhavaṁ gotamo sukhadukkhan”ti.
sn12.18:4.1 “‘Sā vedanā, so vedayatī’ti kho, timbaruka, ādito sato ‘sayaṅkataṁ sukhadukkhan’ti evampāhaṁ na vadāmi.
sn12.18:4.2 ‘Aññā vedanā, añño vedayatī’ti kho, timbaruka, vedanābhitunnassa sato ‘paraṅkataṁ sukhadukkhan’ti evampāhaṁ na vadāmi.
sn12.18:4.3 Ete te, timbaruka, ubho ante anupagamma majjhena tathāgato dhammaṁ deseti:
sn12.18:4.4 ‘avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā;
sn12.18:4.5 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ …pe…
sn12.18:4.6 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.18:4.7 Avijjāya tveva asesavirāganirodhā saṅkhāranirodho;
sn12.18:4.8 saṅkhāranirodhā viññāṇanirodho …pe…
sn12.18:4.9 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hotī’”ti.
sn12.18:5.1 Evaṁ vutte, timbaruko paribbājako bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.18:5.2 “abhikkantaṁ, bho gotama …pe…
sn12.18:5.3 esāhaṁ bhavantaṁ gotamaṁ saraṇaṁ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca.
sn12.18:5.4 Upāsakaṁ maṁ bhavaṁ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṁ saraṇaṁ gatan”ti.
sn12.18:5.5 Aṭṭhamaṁ. "
sn12.19:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.19
sn12.19:0.2 2. Āhāravagga
sn12.19:0.3 Bālapaṇḍitasutta
sn12.19:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.19:1.2 “Avijjānīvaraṇassa, bhikkhave, bālassa taṇhāya sampayuttassa evamayaṁ kāyo samudāgato.
sn12.19:1.3 Iti ayañceva kāyo bahiddhā ca nāmarūpaṁ, itthetaṁ dvayaṁ, dvayaṁ paṭicca phasso saḷevāyatanāni, yehi phuṭṭho bālo sukhadukkhaṁ paṭisaṁvedayati etesaṁ vā aññatarena.
sn12.19:2.1 Avijjānīvaraṇassa, bhikkhave, paṇḍitassa taṇhāya sampayuttassa evamayaṁ kāyo samudāgato.
sn12.19:2.2 Iti ayañceva kāyo bahiddhā ca nāmarūpaṁ, itthetaṁ dvayaṁ, dvayaṁ paṭicca phasso saḷevāyatanāni, yehi phuṭṭho paṇḍito sukhadukkhaṁ paṭisaṁvedayati etesaṁ vā aññatarena.
sn12.19:3.1 Tatra, bhikkhave, ko viseso ko adhippayāso kiṁ nānākaraṇaṁ paṇḍitassa bālenā”ti?
sn12.19:3.2 “Bhagavaṁmūlakā no, bhante, dhammā, bhagavaṁnettikā, bhagavaṁpaṭisaraṇā. Sādhu vata, bhante, bhagavantaṁyeva paṭibhātu etassa bhāsitassa attho. Bhagavato sutvā bhikkhū dhāressantī”ti.
sn12.19:4.1 “Tena hi, bhikkhave, suṇātha, sādhukaṁ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmī”ti.
sn12.19:4.2 “Evaṁ, bhante”ti kho te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.
sn12.19:4.3 Bhagavā etadavoca:
sn12.19:5.1 “Yāya ca, bhikkhave, avijjāya nivutassa bālassa yāya ca taṇhāya sampayuttassa ayaṁ kāyo samudāgato, sā ceva avijjā bālassa appahīnā sā ca taṇhā aparikkhīṇā.
sn12.19:5.2 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn12.19:5.3 Na, bhikkhave, bālo acari brahmacariyaṁ sammā dukkhakkhayāya.
sn12.19:5.4 Tasmā bālo kāyassa bhedā kāyūpago hoti,
sn12.19:5.5 so kāyūpago samāno na parimuccati jātiyā jarāmaraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi.
sn12.19:5.6 Na parimuccati dukkhasmāti vadāmi.
sn12.19:6.1 Yāya ca, bhikkhave, avijjāya nivutassa paṇḍitassa yāya ca taṇhāya sampayuttassa ayaṁ kāyo samudāgato, sā ceva avijjā paṇḍitassa pahīnā, sā ca taṇhā parikkhīṇā.
sn12.19:6.2 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn12.19:6.3 Acari, bhikkhave, paṇḍito brahmacariyaṁ sammā dukkhakkhayāya.
sn12.19:6.4 Tasmā paṇḍito kāyassa bhedā na kāyūpago hoti.
sn12.19:6.5 So akāyūpago samāno parimuccati jātiyā jarāmaraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi.
sn12.19:6.6 Parimuccati dukkhasmāti vadāmi.
sn12.19:6.7 Ayaṁ kho, bhikkhave, viseso, ayaṁ adhippayāso, idaṁ nānākaraṇaṁ paṇḍitassa bālena yadidaṁ brahmacariyavāso”ti.
sn12.19:6.8 Navamaṁ. "
sn12.20:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.20
sn12.20:0.2 2. Āhāravagga
sn12.20:0.3 Paccayasutta
sn12.20:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.20:1.2 “Paṭiccasamuppādañca vo, bhikkhave, desessāmi paṭiccasamuppanne ca dhamme.
sn12.20:1.3 Taṁ suṇātha, sādhukaṁ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmī”ti.
sn12.20:1.4 “Evaṁ, bhante”ti kho te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.
sn12.20:1.5 Bhagavā etadavoca:
sn12.20:2.1 “Katamo ca, bhikkhave, paṭiccasamuppādo?
sn12.20:2.2 Jātipaccayā, bhikkhave, jarāmaraṇaṁ.
sn12.20:2.3 Uppādā vā tathāgatānaṁ anuppādā vā tathāgatānaṁ, ṭhitāva sā dhātu dhammaṭṭhitatā dhammaniyāmatā idappaccayatā.
sn12.20:2.4 Taṁ tathāgato abhisambujjhati abhisameti.
sn12.20:2.5 Abhisambujjhitvā abhisametvā ācikkhati deseti paññāpeti paṭṭhapeti vivarati vibhajati uttānīkaroti.
sn12.20:2.6 ‘Passathā’ti cāha:
sn12.20:2.7 ‘jātipaccayā, bhikkhave, jarāmaraṇaṁ’.
sn12.20:3.1 Bhavapaccayā, bhikkhave, jāti …pe…
sn12.20:3.2 upādānapaccayā, bhikkhave, bhavo …
sn12.20:3.3 taṇhāpaccayā, bhikkhave, upādānaṁ …
sn12.20:3.4 vedanāpaccayā, bhikkhave, taṇhā …
sn12.20:3.5 phassapaccayā, bhikkhave, vedanā …
sn12.20:3.6 saḷāyatanapaccayā, bhikkhave, phasso …
sn12.20:3.7 nāmarūpapaccayā, bhikkhave, saḷāyatanaṁ …
sn12.20:3.8 viññāṇapaccayā, bhikkhave, nāmarūpaṁ …
sn12.20:3.9 saṅkhārapaccayā, bhikkhave, viññāṇaṁ …
sn12.20:3.10 avijjāpaccayā, bhikkhave, saṅkhārā
sn12.20:3.11 uppādā vā tathāgatānaṁ anuppādā vā tathāgatānaṁ, ṭhitāva sā dhātu dhammaṭṭhitatā dhammaniyāmatā idappaccayatā.
sn12.20:3.12 Taṁ tathāgato abhisambujjhati abhisameti.
sn12.20:3.13 Abhisambujjhitvā abhisametvā ācikkhati deseti paññāpeti paṭṭhapeti vivarati vibhajati uttānīkaroti.
sn12.20:3.14 ‘Passathā’ti cāha:
sn12.20:3.15 ‘avijjāpaccayā, bhikkhave, saṅkhārā’.
sn12.20:3.16 Iti kho, bhikkhave, yā tatra tathatā avitathatā anaññathatā idappaccayatā—
sn12.20:3.17 ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, paṭiccasamuppādo.
sn12.20:4.1 Katame ca, bhikkhave, paṭiccasamuppannā dhammā?
sn12.20:4.2 Jarāmaraṇaṁ, bhikkhave, aniccaṁ saṅkhataṁ paṭiccasamuppannaṁ khayadhammaṁ vayadhammaṁ virāgadhammaṁ nirodhadhammaṁ.
sn12.20:4.3 Jāti, bhikkhave, aniccā saṅkhatā paṭiccasamuppannā khayadhammā vayadhammā virāgadhammā nirodhadhammā.
sn12.20:4.4 Bhavo, bhikkhave, anicco saṅkhato paṭiccasamuppanno khayadhammo vayadhammo virāgadhammo nirodhadhammo.
sn12.20:4.5 Upādānaṁ bhikkhave …pe…
sn12.20:4.6 taṇhā, bhikkhave …
sn12.20:4.7 vedanā, bhikkhave …
sn12.20:4.8 phasso, bhikkhave …
sn12.20:4.9 saḷāyatanaṁ, bhikkhave …
sn12.20:4.10 nāmarūpaṁ, bhikkhave …
sn12.20:4.11 viññāṇaṁ, bhikkhave …
sn12.20:4.12 saṅkhārā, bhikkhave …
sn12.20:4.13 avijjā, bhikkhave, aniccā saṅkhatā paṭiccasamuppannā khayadhammā vayadhammā virāgadhammā nirodhadhammā.
sn12.20:4.14 Ime vuccanti, bhikkhave, paṭiccasamuppannā dhammā.
sn12.20:5.1 Yato kho, bhikkhave, ariyasāvakassa ‘ayañca paṭiccasamuppādo, ime ca paṭiccasamuppannā dhammā’ yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhā honti, so vata pubbantaṁ vā paṭidhāvissati:
sn12.20:5.2 ‘ahosiṁ nu kho ahaṁ atītamaddhānaṁ, nanu kho ahosiṁ atītamaddhānaṁ, kiṁ nu kho ahosiṁ atītamaddhānaṁ, kathaṁ nu kho ahosiṁ atītamaddhānaṁ, kiṁ hutvā kiṁ ahosiṁ nu kho ahaṁ atītamaddhānan’ti;
sn12.20:5.3 aparantaṁ vā upadhāvissati:
sn12.20:5.4 ‘bhavissāmi nu kho ahaṁ anāgatamaddhānaṁ, nanu kho bhavissāmi anāgatamaddhānaṁ, kiṁ nu kho bhavissāmi anāgatamaddhānaṁ, kathaṁ nu kho bhavissāmi anāgatamaddhānaṁ, kiṁ hutvā kiṁ bhavissāmi nu kho ahaṁ anāgatamaddhānan’ti;
sn12.20:5.5 etarahi vā paccuppannaṁ addhānaṁ ajjhattaṁ kathaṅkathī bhavissati:
sn12.20:5.6 ‘ahaṁ nu khosmi, no nu khosmi, kiṁ nu khosmi, kathaṁ nu khosmi, ayaṁ nu kho satto kuto āgato, so kuhiṁ gamissatī’ti—
sn12.20:5.7 netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.
sn12.20:5.8 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn12.20:5.9 Tathā hi, bhikkhave, ariyasāvakassa ayañca paṭiccasamuppādo ime ca paṭiccasamuppannā dhammā yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhā”ti.
sn12.20:5.10 Dasamaṁ.
sn12.20:5.11 Āhāravaggo dutiyo.
sn12.20:6.0 Tassuddānaṁ
sn12.20:6.1 Āhāraṁ phagguno ceva,
sn12.20:6.2 Dve ca samaṇabrāhmaṇā;
sn12.20:6.3 Kaccānagotta dhammakathikaṁ,
sn12.20:6.4 Acelaṁ timbarukena ca;
sn12.20:6.5 Bālapaṇḍitato ceva,
sn12.20:6.6 Dasamo paccayena cāti. "

sn12.21:0.2 3. Dasabalavagga
sn12.21:0.3 Dasabalasutta
sn12.21:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.21:1.2 “Dasabalasamannāgato, bhikkhave, tathāgato catūhi ca vesārajjehi samannāgato āsabhaṁ ṭhānaṁ paṭijānāti, parisāsu sīhanādaṁ nadati, brahmacakkaṁ pavatteti—
sn12.21:1.3 iti rūpaṁ iti rūpassa samudayo iti rūpassa atthaṅgamo,
sn12.21:1.4 iti vedanā iti vedanāya samudayo iti vedanāya atthaṅgamo,
sn12.21:1.5 iti saññā iti saññāya samudayo iti saññāya atthaṅgamo,
sn12.21:1.6 iti saṅkhārā iti saṅkhārānaṁ samudayo iti saṅkhārānaṁ atthaṅgamo,
sn12.21:1.7 iti viññāṇaṁ iti viññāṇassa samudayo iti viññāṇassa atthaṅgamo.
sn12.21:1.8 Iti imasmiṁ sati idaṁ hoti, imassuppādā idaṁ uppajjati.
sn12.21:1.9 Imasmiṁ asati idaṁ na hoti, imassa nirodhā idaṁ nirujjhati.
sn12.21:1.10 Yadidaṁ avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā;
sn12.21:1.11 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ …pe…
sn12.21:1.12 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.21:1.13 Avijjāya tveva asesavirāganirodhā saṅkhāranirodho;
sn12.21:1.14 saṅkhāranirodhā viññāṇanirodho …pe…
sn12.21:1.15 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hotī”ti.
sn12.21:1.16 Paṭhamaṁ. "
sn12.22:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.22
sn12.22:0.2 3. Dasabalavagga
sn12.22:0.3 Dutiyadasabalasutta
sn12.22:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.22:1.2 “Dasabalasamannāgato, bhikkhave, tathāgato catūhi ca vesārajjehi samannāgato āsabhaṁ ṭhānaṁ paṭijānāti, parisāsu sīhanādaṁ nadati, brahmacakkaṁ pavatteti:
sn12.22:1.3 ‘iti rūpaṁ iti rūpassa samudayo iti rūpassa atthaṅgamo,
sn12.22:1.4 iti vedanā iti vedanāya samudayo iti vedanāya atthaṅgamo,
sn12.22:1.5 iti saññā iti saññāya samudayo iti saññāya atthaṅgamo,
sn12.22:1.6 iti saṅkhārā iti saṅkhārānaṁ samudayo iti saṅkhārānaṁ atthaṅgamo,
sn12.22:1.7 iti viññāṇaṁ iti viññāṇassa samudayo iti viññāṇassa atthaṅgamo.
sn12.22:1.8 Iti imasmiṁ sati idaṁ hoti, imassuppādā idaṁ uppajjati;
sn12.22:1.9 imasmiṁ asati idaṁ na hoti imassa nirodhā idaṁ nirujjhati.
sn12.22:1.10 Yadidaṁ avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā;
sn12.22:1.11 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ …pe…
sn12.22:1.12 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.22:1.13 Avijjāya tveva asesavirāganirodhā saṅkhāranirodho;
sn12.22:1.14 saṅkhāranirodhā viññāṇanirodho …pe…
sn12.22:1.15 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hoti’.
sn12.22:2.1 Evaṁ svākkhāto, bhikkhave, mayā dhammo uttāno vivaṭo pakāsito chinnapilotiko.
sn12.22:2.2 Evaṁ svākkhāte kho, bhikkhave, mayā dhamme uttāne vivaṭe pakāsite chinnapilotike alameva saddhāpabbajitena kulaputtena vīriyaṁ ārabhituṁ:
sn12.22:2.3 ‘kāmaṁ taco ca nhāru ca aṭṭhi ca avasissatu, sarīre upassussatu maṁsalohitaṁ. Yaṁ taṁ purisathāmena purisavīriyena purisaparakkamena pattabbaṁ, na taṁ apāpuṇitvā vīriyassa saṇṭhānaṁ bhavissatī’ti.
sn12.22:3.1 Dukkhaṁ, bhikkhave, kusīto viharati vokiṇṇo pāpakehi akusalehi dhammehi, mahantañca sadatthaṁ parihāpeti.
sn12.22:3.2 Āraddhavīriyo ca kho, bhikkhave, sukhaṁ viharati pavivitto pāpakehi akusalehi dhammehi, mahantañca sadatthaṁ paripūreti.
sn12.22:3.3 Na, bhikkhave, hīnena aggassa patti hoti.
sn12.22:3.4 Aggena ca kho, bhikkhave, aggassa patti hoti.
sn12.22:3.5 Maṇḍapeyyamidaṁ, bhikkhave, brahmacariyaṁ, satthā sammukhībhūto.
sn12.22:3.6 Tasmātiha, bhikkhave, vīriyaṁ ārabhatha appattassa pattiyā, anadhigatassa adhigamāya, asacchikatassa sacchikiriyāya.
sn12.22:3.7 ‘Evaṁ no ayaṁ amhākaṁ pabbajjā avañjhā bhavissati saphalā saudrayā.
sn12.22:3.8 Yesañca mayaṁ paribhuñjāma cīvarapiṇḍapātasenāsanagilānappaccayabhesajjaparikkhāraṁ tesaṁ te kārā amhesu mahapphalā bhavissanti mahānisaṁsā’ti—
sn12.22:3.9 evañhi vo, bhikkhave, sikkhitabbaṁ.
sn12.22:3.10 Attatthaṁ vā hi, bhikkhave, sampassamānena alameva appamādena sampādetuṁ;
sn12.22:3.11 paratthaṁ vā hi, bhikkhave, sampassamānena alameva appamādena sampādetuṁ;
sn12.22:3.12 ubhayatthaṁ vā hi, bhikkhave, sampassamānena alameva appamādena sampādetun”ti.
sn12.22:3.13 Dutiyaṁ. "
sn12.23:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.23
sn12.23:0.2 3. Dasabalavagga
sn12.23:0.3 Upanisasutta
sn12.23:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.23:1.2 “Jānato ahaṁ, bhikkhave, passato āsavānaṁ khayaṁ vadāmi, no ajānato no apassato.
sn12.23:1.3 Kiñca, bhikkhave, jānato kiṁ passato āsavānaṁ khayo hoti?
sn12.23:1.4 Iti rūpaṁ iti rūpassa samudayo iti rūpassa atthaṅgamo,
sn12.23:1.5 iti vedanā …pe…
sn12.23:1.6 iti saññā …
sn12.23:1.7 iti saṅkhārā …
sn12.23:1.8 iti viññāṇaṁ iti viññāṇassa samudayo iti viññāṇassa atthaṅgamoti.
sn12.23:1.9 Evaṁ kho, bhikkhave, jānato evaṁ passato āsavānaṁ khayo hoti.
sn12.23:2.1 Yampissa taṁ, bhikkhave, khayasmiṁ khayeñāṇaṁ, tampi saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:2.2 Kā ca, bhikkhave, khayeñāṇassa upanisā?
sn12.23:2.3 ‘Vimuttī’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:2.4 Vimuttimpāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:2.5 Kā ca, bhikkhave, vimuttiyā upanisā?
sn12.23:2.6 ‘Virāgo’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:2.7 Virāgampāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:2.8 Kā ca, bhikkhave, virāgassa upanisā?
sn12.23:2.9 ‘Nibbidā’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:2.10 Nibbidampāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:2.11 Kā ca, bhikkhave, nibbidāya upanisā?
sn12.23:2.12 ‘Yathābhūtañāṇadassanan’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:2.13 Yathābhūtañāṇadassanampāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:2.14 Kā ca, bhikkhave, yathābhūtañāṇadassanassa upanisā?
sn12.23:2.15 ‘Samādhī’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:2.16 Samādhimpāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:3.1 Kā ca, bhikkhave, samādhissa upanisā?
sn12.23:3.2 ‘Sukhan’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:3.3 Sukhampāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:3.4 Kā ca, bhikkhave, sukhassa upanisā?
sn12.23:3.5 ‘Passaddhī’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:3.6 Passaddhimpāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:3.7 Kā ca, bhikkhave, passaddhiyā upanisā?
sn12.23:3.8 ‘Pītī’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:3.9 Pītimpāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:3.10 Kā ca, bhikkhave, pītiyā upanisā?
sn12.23:3.11 ‘Pāmojjan’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:3.12 Pāmojjampāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:3.13 Kā ca, bhikkhave, pāmojjassa upanisā?
sn12.23:3.14 ‘Saddhā’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:3.15 Saddhampāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:4.1 Kā ca, bhikkhave, saddhāya upanisā?
sn12.23:4.2 ‘Dukkhan’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:4.3 Dukkhampāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:4.4 Kā ca, bhikkhave, dukkhassa upanisā?
sn12.23:4.5 ‘Jātī’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:4.6 Jātimpāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:4.7 Kā ca, bhikkhave, jātiyā upanisā?
sn12.23:4.8 ‘Bhavo’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:4.9 Bhavampāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:4.10 Kā ca, bhikkhave, bhavassa upanisā?
sn12.23:4.11 ‘Upādānan’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:4.12 Upādānampāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:4.13 Kā ca, bhikkhave, upādānassa upanisā?
sn12.23:4.14 ‘Taṇhā’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:4.15 Taṇhampāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanisaṁ vadāmi, no anupanisaṁ.
sn12.23:5.1 Kā ca, bhikkhave, taṇhāya upanisā?
sn12.23:5.2 ‘Vedanā’tissa vacanīyaṁ …pe…
sn12.23:5.3 ‘phasso’tissa vacanīyaṁ …
sn12.23:5.4 ‘saḷāyatanan’tissa vacanīyaṁ …
sn12.23:5.5 ‘nāmarūpan’tissa vacanīyaṁ …
sn12.23:5.6 ‘viññāṇan’tissa vacanīyaṁ …
sn12.23:5.7 ‘saṅkhārā’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:5.8 Saṅkhārepāhaṁ, bhikkhave, saupanise vadāmi, no anupanise.
sn12.23:5.9 Kā ca, bhikkhave, saṅkhārānaṁ upanisā?
sn12.23:5.10 ‘Avijjā’tissa vacanīyaṁ.
sn12.23:6.1 Iti kho, bhikkhave, avijjūpanisā saṅkhārā,
sn12.23:6.2 saṅkhārūpanisaṁ viññāṇaṁ,
sn12.23:6.3 viññāṇūpanisaṁ nāmarūpaṁ,
sn12.23:6.4 nāmarūpūpanisaṁ saḷāyatanaṁ,
sn12.23:6.5 saḷāyatanūpaniso phasso,
sn12.23:6.6 phassūpanisā vedanā,
sn12.23:6.7 vedanūpanisā taṇhā,
sn12.23:6.8 taṇhūpanisaṁ upādānaṁ,
sn12.23:6.9 upādānūpaniso bhavo,
sn12.23:6.10 bhavūpanisā jāti,
sn12.23:6.11 jātūpanisaṁ dukkhaṁ,
sn12.23:6.12 dukkhūpanisā saddhā,
sn12.23:6.13 saddhūpanisaṁ pāmojjaṁ,
sn12.23:6.14 pāmojjūpanisā pīti,
sn12.23:6.15 pītūpanisā passaddhi,
sn12.23:6.16 passaddhūpanisaṁ sukhaṁ,
sn12.23:6.17 sukhūpaniso samādhi,
sn12.23:6.18 samādhūpanisaṁ yathābhūtañāṇadassanaṁ,
sn12.23:6.19 yathābhūtañāṇadassanūpanisā nibbidā,
sn12.23:6.20 nibbidūpaniso virāgo,
sn12.23:6.21 virāgūpanisā vimutti,
sn12.23:6.22 vimuttūpanisaṁ khayeñāṇaṁ.
sn12.23:7.1 Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, uparipabbate thullaphusitake deve vassante taṁ udakaṁ yathāninnaṁ pavattamānaṁ pabbatakandarapadarasākhā paripūreti. Pabbatakandarapadarasākhāparipūrā kusobbhe paripūrenti. Kusobbhā paripūrā mahāsobbhe paripūrenti. Mahāsobbhā paripūrā kunnadiyo paripūrenti. Kunnadiyo paripūrā mahānadiyo paripūrenti. Mahānadiyo paripūrā mahāsamuddaṁ paripūrenti.
sn12.23:8.1 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, avijjūpanisā saṅkhārā, saṅkhārūpanisaṁ viññāṇaṁ, viññāṇūpanisaṁ nāmarūpaṁ, nāmarūpūpanisaṁ saḷāyatanaṁ, saḷāyatanūpaniso phasso, phassūpanisā vedanā, vedanūpanisā taṇhā, taṇhūpanisaṁ upādānaṁ, upādānūpaniso bhavo, bhavūpanisā jāti, jātūpanisaṁ dukkhaṁ, dukkhūpanisā saddhā, saddhūpanisaṁ pāmojjaṁ, pāmojjūpanisā pīti, pītūpanisā passaddhi, passaddhūpanisaṁ sukhaṁ, sukhūpaniso samādhi, samādhūpanisaṁ yathābhūtañāṇadassanaṁ, yathābhūtañāṇadassanūpanisā nibbidā, nibbidūpaniso virāgo, virāgūpanisā vimutti, vimuttūpanisaṁ khayeñāṇan”ti.
sn12.23:8.2 Tatiyaṁ. "
sn12.24:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.24
sn12.24:0.2 3. Dasabalavagga
sn12.24:0.3 Aññatitthiyasutta
sn12.24:1.1 Rājagahe viharati veḷuvane.
sn12.24:1.2 Atha kho āyasmā sāriputto pubbaṇhasamayaṁ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya rājagahaṁ piṇḍāya pāvisi.
sn12.24:1.3 Atha kho āyasmato sāriputtassa etadahosi:
sn12.24:1.4 “atippago kho tāva rājagahe piṇḍāya carituṁ.
sn12.24:1.5 Yannūnāhaṁ yena aññatitthiyānaṁ paribbājakānaṁ ārāmo tenupasaṅkameyyan”ti.
sn12.24:2.1 Atha kho āyasmā sāriputto yena aññatitthiyānaṁ paribbājakānaṁ ārāmo tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā tehi aññatitthiyehi paribbājakehi saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn12.24:2.2 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinnaṁ kho āyasmantaṁ sāriputtaṁ te aññatitthiyā paribbājakā etadavocuṁ:
sn12.24:3.1 “Santāvuso sāriputta, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkataṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti.
sn12.24:3.2 Santi panāvuso sāriputta, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā paraṅkataṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti.
sn12.24:3.3 Santāvuso sāriputta, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca dukkhaṁ paññapenti.
sn12.24:3.4 Santi panāvuso sāriputta, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti.
sn12.24:3.5 Idha, panāvuso sāriputta, samaṇo gotamo kiṁvādī kimakkhāyī?
sn12.24:3.6 Kathaṁ byākaramānā ca mayaṁ vuttavādino ceva samaṇassa gotamassa assāma, na ca samaṇaṁ gotamaṁ abhūtena abbhācikkheyyāma, dhammassa cānudhammaṁ byākareyyāma, na ca koci sahadhammiko vādānupāto gārayhaṁ ṭhānaṁ āgaccheyyā”ti?
sn12.24:4.1 “Paṭiccasamuppannaṁ kho, āvuso, dukkhaṁ vuttaṁ bhagavatā.
sn12.24:4.2 Kiṁ paṭicca?
sn12.24:4.3 Phassaṁ paṭicca.
sn12.24:4.4 Iti vadaṁ vuttavādī ceva bhagavato assa, na ca bhagavantaṁ abhūtena abbhācikkheyya, dhammassa cānudhammaṁ byākareyya, na ca koci sahadhammiko vādānupāto gārayhaṁ ṭhānaṁ āgaccheyya.
sn12.24:5.1 Tatrāvuso, ye te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkataṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti tadapi phassapaccayā.
sn12.24:5.2 Yepi te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā paraṅkataṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti tadapi phassapaccayā.
sn12.24:5.3 Yepi te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca dukkhaṁ paññapenti tadapi phassapaccayā.
sn12.24:5.4 Yepi te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti tadapi phassapaccayā.
sn12.24:6.1 Tatrāvuso, ye te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkataṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti, te vata aññatra phassā paṭisaṁvedissantīti netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.
sn12.24:6.2 Yepi te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā paraṅkataṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti, te vata aññatra phassā paṭisaṁvedissantīti netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.
sn12.24:6.3 Yepi te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca dukkhaṁ paññapenti, te vata aññatra phassā paṭisaṁvedissantīti netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.
sn12.24:6.4 Yepi te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti, te vata aññatra phassā paṭisaṁvedissantīti netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjatī”ti.
sn12.24:7.1 Assosi kho āyasmā ānando āyasmato sāriputtassa tehi aññatitthiyehi paribbājakehi saddhiṁ imaṁ kathāsallāpaṁ.
sn12.24:7.2 Atha kho āyasmā ānando rājagahe piṇḍāya caritvā pacchābhattaṁ piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi.
sn12.24:7.3 Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā ānando yāvatako āyasmato sāriputtassa tehi aññatitthiyehi paribbājakehi saddhiṁ ahosi kathāsallāpo taṁ sabbaṁ bhagavato ārocesi.
sn12.24:8.1 “Sādhu sādhu, ānanda, yathā taṁ sāriputto sammā byākaramāno byākareyya.
sn12.24:8.2 Paṭiccasamuppannaṁ kho, ānanda, dukkhaṁ vuttaṁ mayā.
sn12.24:8.3 Kiṁ paṭicca?
sn12.24:8.4 Phassaṁ paṭicca.
sn12.24:8.5 Iti vadaṁ vuttavādī ceva me assa, na ca maṁ abhūtena abbhācikkheyya, dhammassa cānudhammaṁ byākareyya, na ca koci sahadhammiko vādānupāto gārayhaṁ ṭhānaṁ āgaccheyya.
sn12.24:9.1 Tatrānanda, ye te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkataṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti tadapi phassapaccayā.
sn12.24:9.2 Yepi te …pe…
sn12.24:9.3 yepi te …pe…
sn12.24:9.4 yepi te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti tadapi phassapaccayā.
sn12.24:10.1 Tatrānanda, yepi te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkataṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti, te vata aññatra phassā paṭisaṁvedissantīti netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.
sn12.24:10.2 Yepi te …pe…
sn12.24:10.3 yepi te …pe…
sn12.24:10.4 yepi te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti, te vata aññatra phassā paṭisaṁvedissantīti netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.
sn12.24:11.1 Ekamidāhaṁ, ānanda, samayaṁ idheva rājagahe viharāmi veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe.
sn12.24:11.2 Atha khvāhaṁ, ānanda, pubbaṇhasamayaṁ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya rājagahaṁ piṇḍāya pāvisiṁ.
sn12.24:11.3 Tassa mayhaṁ, ānanda, etadahosi:
sn12.24:11.4 ‘atippago kho tāva rājagahe piṇḍāya carituṁ.
sn12.24:11.5 Yannūnāhaṁ yena aññatitthiyānaṁ paribbājakānaṁ ārāmo tenupasaṅkameyyan’ti.
sn12.24:12.1 Atha khvāhaṁ, ānanda, yena aññatitthiyānaṁ paribbājakānaṁ ārāmo tenupasaṅkamiṁ; upasaṅkamitvā tehi aññatitthiyehi paribbājakehi saddhiṁ sammodiṁ.
sn12.24:12.2 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdiṁ. Ekamantaṁ nisinnaṁ kho maṁ, ānanda, te aññatitthiyā paribbājakā etadavocuṁ:
sn12.24:13.1 ‘Santāvuso gotama, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkataṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti.
sn12.24:13.2 Santi panāvuso gotama, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā paraṅkataṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti.
sn12.24:13.3 Santāvuso gotama, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca dukkhaṁ paññapenti.
sn12.24:13.4 Santi panāvuso gotama, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti.
sn12.24:13.5 Idha no āyasmā gotamo kiṁvādī kimakkhāyī?
sn12.24:13.6 Kathaṁ byākaramānā ca mayaṁ vuttavādino ceva āyasmato gotamassa assāma, na ca āyasmantaṁ gotamaṁ abhūtena abbhācikkheyyāma, dhammassa cānudhammaṁ byākareyyāma, na ca koci sahadhammiko vādānupāto gārayhaṁ ṭhānaṁ āgaccheyyā’ti?
sn12.24:14.1 Evaṁ vuttāhaṁ, ānanda, te aññatitthiye paribbājake etadavocaṁ:
sn12.24:14.2 ‘paṭiccasamuppannaṁ kho, āvuso, dukkhaṁ vuttaṁ mayā.
sn12.24:14.3 Kiṁ paṭicca?
sn12.24:14.4 Phassaṁ paṭicca.
sn12.24:14.5 Iti vadaṁ vuttavādī ceva me assa, na ca maṁ abhūtena abbhācikkheyya, dhammassa cānudhammaṁ byākareyya, na ca koci sahadhammiko vādānupāto gārayhaṁ ṭhānaṁ āgaccheyyāti.
sn12.24:15.1 Tatrāvuso, ye te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkataṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti tadapi phassapaccayā.
sn12.24:15.2 Yepi te …pe…

sn12.24:16.1 Tatrāvuso, ye te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkataṁ dukkhaṁ paññapenti, te vata aññatra phassā paṭisaṁvedissantīti netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.
sn12.24:16.2 Yepi te …pe…

sn12.24:17.1 “Acchariyaṁ bhante, abbhutaṁ bhante.
sn12.24:17.2 Yatra hi nāma ekena padena sabbo attho vutto bhavissati.
sn12.24:17.3 Siyā nu kho, bhante, esevattho vitthārena vuccamāno gambhīro ceva assa gambhīrāvabhāso cā”ti?
sn12.24:18.1 “Tena hānanda, taññevettha paṭibhātū”ti.
sn12.24:18.2 “Sace maṁ, bhante, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.24:18.3 ‘jarāmaraṇaṁ, āvuso ānanda, kiṁnidānaṁ kiṁsamudayaṁ kiṁjātikaṁ kiṁpabhavan’ti?
sn12.24:18.4 Evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyaṁ:
sn12.24:18.5 ‘jarāmaraṇaṁ kho, āvuso, jātinidānaṁ jātisamudayaṁ jātijātikaṁ jātipabhavan’ti.
sn12.24:18.6 Evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyaṁ.
sn12.24:19.1 Sace maṁ, bhante, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.24:19.2 ‘jāti panāvuso ānanda, kiṁnidānā kiṁsamudayā kiṁjātikā kiṁpabhavā’ti?
sn12.24:19.3 Evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyaṁ:

sn12.25:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.25
sn12.25:0.2 3. Dasabalavagga
sn12.25:0.3 Bhūmijasutta
sn12.25:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.25:1.2 Atha kho āyasmā bhūmijo sāyanhasamayaṁ paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito yenāyasmā sāriputto tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā sāriputtena saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn12.25:1.3 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā bhūmijo āyasmantaṁ sāriputtaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.25:2.1 “Santāvuso sāriputta, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkataṁ sukhadukkhaṁ paññapenti.
sn12.25:2.2 Santi panāvuso sāriputta, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā paraṅkataṁ sukhadukkhaṁ paññapenti.
sn12.25:2.3 Santāvuso sāriputta, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca sukhadukkhaṁ paññapenti.
sn12.25:2.4 Santi panāvuso sāriputta, eke samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ sukhadukkhaṁ paññapenti.
sn12.25:2.5 Idha no, āvuso sāriputta, bhagavā kiṁvādī kimakkhāyī,
sn12.25:2.6 kathaṁ byākaramānā ca mayaṁ vuttavādino ceva bhagavato assāma, na ca bhagavantaṁ abhūtena abbhācikkheyyāma, dhammassa cānudhammaṁ byākareyyāma, na ca koci sahadhammiko vādānupāto gārayhaṁ ṭhānaṁ āgaccheyyā”ti?
sn12.25:3.1 “Paṭiccasamuppannaṁ kho, āvuso, sukhadukkhaṁ vuttaṁ bhagavatā.
sn12.25:3.2 Kiṁ paṭicca?
sn12.25:3.3 Phassaṁ paṭicca.
sn12.25:3.4 Iti vadaṁ vuttavādī ceva bhagavato assa, na ca bhagavantaṁ abhūtena abbhācikkheyya, dhammassa cānudhammaṁ byākareyya, na ca koci sahadhammiko vādānupāto gārayhaṁ ṭhānaṁ āgaccheyya.
sn12.25:4.1 Tatrāvuso, ye te samaṇabrāhmaṇā kammavādā sayaṅkataṁ sukhadukkhaṁ paññapenti, tadapi phassapaccayā.
sn12.25:4.2 Yepi te …pe…
sn12.25:4.3 yepi te …pe…

sn12.30:1.3 ye hi keci, bhikkhave, samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā jarāmaraṇaṁ nappajānanti, jarāmaraṇasamudayaṁ nappajānanti, jarāmaraṇanirodhaṁ nappajānanti, jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ nappajānanti te vata jarāmaraṇaṁ samatikkamma ṭhassantīti netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.
sn12.30:1.4 Jātiṁ nappajānanti …pe…
sn12.30:1.5 bhavaṁ …
sn12.30:1.6 upādānaṁ …
sn12.30:1.7 taṇhaṁ …
sn12.30:1.8 vedanaṁ …
sn12.30:1.9 phassaṁ …
sn12.30:1.10 saḷāyatanaṁ …
sn12.30:1.11 nāmarūpaṁ …
sn12.30:1.12 viññāṇaṁ …
sn12.30:1.13 saṅkhāre nappajānanti, saṅkhārasamudayaṁ nappajānanti, saṅkhāranirodhaṁ nappajānanti, saṅkhāranirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ nappajānanti te vata saṅkhāre samatikkamma ṭhassantīti netaṁ ṭhānaṁ vijjati.
sn12.30:2.1 Ye ca kho keci, bhikkhave, samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā jarāmaraṇaṁ pajānanti, jarāmaraṇasamudayaṁ pajānanti, jarāmaraṇanirodhaṁ pajānanti, jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ pajānanti te vata jarāmaraṇaṁ samatikkamma ṭhassantīti ṭhānametaṁ vijjati.
sn12.30:2.2 Jātiṁ pajānanti …pe…

sn12.30:2.5 taṇhaṁ …
sn12.30:2.6 vedanaṁ …

sn12.30:2.8 saḷāyatanaṁ …
sn12.30:2.9 nāmarūpaṁ …
sn12.30:2.10 viññāṇaṁ …
sn12.30:2.11 saṅkhāre pajānanti, saṅkhārasamudayaṁ pajānanti, saṅkhāranirodhaṁ pajānanti, saṅkhāranirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ pajānanti.
sn12.30:2.12 Te vata saṅkhāre samatikkamma ṭhassantīti ṭhānametaṁ vijjatī”ti.
sn12.30:2.13 Dasamaṁ.
sn12.30:2.14 Dasabalavaggo tatiyo.

sn12.30:3.2 Aññatitthiyabhūmijo;
sn12.30:3.3 Upavāṇo paccayo bhikkhu,
sn12.30:3.4 Dve ca samaṇabrāhmaṇāti. "
sn12.31:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.31
sn12.31:0.2 4. Kaḷārakhattiyavagga
sn12.31:0.3 Bhūtasutta
sn12.31:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.31:1.2 Tatra kho bhagavā āyasmantaṁ sāriputtaṁ āmantesi:
sn12.31:1.3 “vuttamidaṁ, sāriputta, pārāyane ajitapañhe:
sn12.31:2.1 ‘Ye ca saṅkhātadhammāse,
sn12.31:2.2 ye ca sekkhā puthū idha;
sn12.31:2.3 Tesaṁ me nipako iriyaṁ,
sn12.31:2.4 puṭṭho pabrūhi mārisā’ti.
sn12.31:3.1 Imassa nu kho, sāriputta, saṅkhittena bhāsitassa kathaṁ vitthārena attho daṭṭhabbo”ti?
sn12.31:3.2 Evaṁ vutte, āyasmā sāriputto tuṇhī ahosi.
sn12.31:4.1 Dutiyampi kho bhagavā āyasmantaṁ sāriputtaṁ āmantesi …pe…
sn12.31:4.2 dutiyampi kho āyasmā sāriputto tuṇhī ahosi.
sn12.31:4.3 Tatiyampi kho bhagavā āyasmantaṁ sāriputtaṁ āmantesi:
sn12.31:4.4 “vuttamidaṁ, sāriputta, pārāyane ajitapañhe:
sn12.31:5.1 ‘Ye ca saṅkhātadhammāse,
sn12.31:5.2 ye ca sekkhā puthū idha;
sn12.31:5.3 Tesaṁ me nipako iriyaṁ,
sn12.31:5.4 puṭṭho pabrūhi mārisā’ti.
sn12.31:6.1 Imassa nu kho, sāriputta, saṅkhittena bhāsitassa kathaṁ vitthārena attho daṭṭhabbo”ti?
sn12.31:6.2 Tatiyampi kho āyasmā sāriputto tuṇhī ahosi.
sn12.31:7.1 “Bhūtamidanti, sāriputta, passasī”ti?
sn12.31:7.2 “Bhūtamidanti, bhante, yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passati.
sn12.31:7.3 Bhūtamidanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya disvā bhūtassa nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya paṭipanno hoti.
sn12.31:7.4 Tadāhārasambhavanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passati.
sn12.31:7.5 Tadāhārasambhavanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya disvā āhārasambhavassa nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya paṭipanno hoti.
sn12.31:7.6 Tadāhāranirodhā yaṁ bhūtaṁ taṁ nirodhadhammanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passati.
sn12.31:7.7 Tadāhāranirodhā yaṁ bhūtaṁ taṁ nirodhadhammanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya disvā nirodhadhammassa nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya paṭipanno hoti.
sn12.31:7.8 Evaṁ kho, bhante, sekkho hoti.
sn12.31:8.1 Kathañca, bhante, saṅkhātadhammo hoti?
sn12.31:8.2 Bhūtamidanti, bhante, yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passati.
sn12.31:8.3 Bhūtamidanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya disvā bhūtassa nibbidā virāgā nirodhā anupādā vimutto hoti.
sn12.31:8.4 Tadāhārasambhavanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passati.
sn12.31:8.5 Tadāhārasambhavanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya disvā āhārasambhavassa nibbidā virāgā nirodhā anupādā vimutto hoti.
sn12.31:8.6 Tadāhāranirodhā yaṁ bhūtaṁ taṁ nirodhadhammanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passati.
sn12.31:8.7 Tadāhāranirodhā yaṁ bhūtaṁ taṁ nirodhadhammanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya disvā nirodhadhammassa nibbidā virāgā nirodhā anupādā vimutto hoti.
sn12.31:8.8 Evaṁ kho, bhante, saṅkhātadhammo hoti.
sn12.31:8.9 Iti kho, bhante, yaṁ taṁ vuttaṁ pārāyane ajitapañhe:
sn12.31:9.1 ‘Ye ca saṅkhātadhammāse,
sn12.31:9.2 ye ca sekkhā puthū idha;
sn12.31:9.3 Tesaṁ me nipako iriyaṁ,
sn12.31:9.4 puṭṭho pabrūhi mārisā’ti.
sn12.31:10.1 Imassa khvāhaṁ, bhante, saṅkhittena bhāsitassa evaṁ vitthārena atthaṁ ājānāmī”ti.
sn12.31:11.1 “Sādhu sādhu, sāriputta, bhūtamidanti, sāriputta, yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passati.
sn12.31:11.2 Bhūtamidanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya disvā bhūtassa nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya paṭipanno hoti.
sn12.31:11.3 Tadāhārasambhavanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passati.
sn12.31:11.4 Tadāhārasambhavanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya disvā āhārasambhavassa nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya paṭipanno hoti.
sn12.31:11.5 Tadāhāranirodhā yaṁ bhūtaṁ taṁ nirodhadhammanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passati.
sn12.31:11.6 Tadāhāranirodhā yaṁ bhūtaṁ taṁ nirodhadhammanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya disvā nirodhadhammassa nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya paṭipanno hoti.
sn12.31:11.7 Evaṁ kho, sāriputta, sekkho hoti.
sn12.31:12.1 Kathañca, sāriputta, saṅkhātadhammo hoti?
sn12.31:12.2 Bhūtamidanti, sāriputta, yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passati.
sn12.31:12.3 Bhūtamidanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya disvā bhūtassa nibbidā virāgā nirodhā anupādā vimutto hoti.
sn12.31:12.4 Tadāhārasambhavanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passati.
sn12.31:12.5 Tadāhārasambhavanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya disvā āhārasambhavassa nibbidā virāgā nirodhā anupādā vimutto hoti.
sn12.31:12.6 Tadāhāranirodhā yaṁ bhūtaṁ taṁ nirodhadhammanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya passati.
sn12.31:12.7 Tadāhāranirodhā yaṁ bhūtaṁ taṁ nirodhadhammanti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññā disvā nirodhadhammassa nibbidā virāgā nirodhā anupādā vimutto hoti.
sn12.31:12.8 Evaṁ kho, sāriputta, saṅkhātadhammo hoti.
sn12.31:12.9 Iti kho, sāriputta, yaṁ taṁ vuttaṁ pārāyane ajitapañhe:
sn12.31:13.1 ‘Ye ca saṅkhātadhammāse,
sn12.31:13.2 ye ca sekkhā puthū idha;
sn12.31:13.3 Tesaṁ me nipako iriyaṁ,
sn12.31:13.4 puṭṭho pabrūhi mārisā’ti.
sn12.31:14.1 Imassa kho, sāriputta, saṅkhittena bhāsitassa evaṁ vitthārena attho daṭṭhabbo”ti.
sn12.31:14.2 Paṭhamaṁ. "
sn12.32:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.32
sn12.32:0.2 4. Kaḷārakhattiyavagga
sn12.32:0.3 Kaḷārasutta
sn12.32:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.32:1.2 Atha kho kaḷārakhattiyo bhikkhu yenāyasmā sāriputto tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā sāriputtena saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn12.32:1.3 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho kaḷārakhattiyo bhikkhu āyasmantaṁ sāriputtaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.32:1.4 “moḷiyaphagguno, āvuso sāriputta, bhikkhu sikkhaṁ paccakkhāya hīnāyāvatto”ti.
sn12.32:1.5 “Na hi nūna so āyasmā imasmiṁ dhammavinaye assāsamalatthā”ti.
sn12.32:2.1 “Tena hāyasmā sāriputto imasmiṁ dhammavinaye assāsaṁ patto”ti?
sn12.32:3.1 “Na khvāhaṁ, āvuso, kaṅkhāmī”ti.
sn12.32:3.2 “Āyatiṁ, panāvuso”ti?
sn12.32:4.1 “Na khvāhaṁ, āvuso, vicikicchāmī”ti.
sn12.32:5.1 Atha kho kaḷārakhattiyo bhikkhu uṭṭhāyāsanā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho kaḷārakhattiyo bhikkhu bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.32:5.2 “āyasmatā, bhante, sāriputtena aññā byākatā:
sn12.32:5.3 ‘khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānāmī”ti.
sn12.32:6.1 Atha kho bhagavā aññataraṁ bhikkhuṁ āmantesi:
sn12.32:6.2 “ehi tvaṁ, bhikkhu, mama vacanena sāriputtaṁ āmantehi:
sn12.32:6.3 ‘satthā taṁ, āvuso sāriputta, āmantetī’”ti.
sn12.32:6.4 “Evaṁ, bhante”ti kho so bhikkhu bhagavato paṭissutvā yenāyasmā sāriputto tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṁ sāriputtaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.32:6.5 “satthā taṁ, āvuso sāriputta, āmantetī”ti.
sn12.32:6.6 “Evaṁ, āvuso”ti kho āyasmā sāriputto tassa bhikkhuno paṭissutvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinnaṁ kho āyasmantaṁ sāriputtaṁ bhagavā etadavoca:
sn12.32:6.7 “saccaṁ kira tayā, sāriputta, aññā byākatā:
sn12.32:6.8 ‘khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānāmī”ti?
sn12.32:6.9 “Na kho, bhante, etehi padehi etehi byañjanehi attho vutto”ti.
sn12.32:6.10 “Yena kenacipi, sāriputta, pariyāyena kulaputto aññaṁ byākaroti, atha kho byākataṁ byākatato daṭṭhabban”ti.
sn12.32:6.11 “Nanu ahampi, bhante, evaṁ vadāmi:
sn12.32:6.12 ‘na kho, bhante, etehi padehi etehi byañjanehi attho vutto’”ti.
sn12.32:7.1 “Sace taṁ, sāriputta, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.32:7.2 ‘kathaṁ jānatā pana tayā, āvuso sāriputta, kathaṁ passatā aññā byākatā—
sn12.32:7.3 khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyāti pajānāmī’ti.
sn12.32:7.4 Evaṁ puṭṭho tvaṁ, sāriputta, kinti byākareyyāsī”ti?
sn12.32:8.1 “Sace maṁ, bhante, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.32:8.2 ‘kathaṁ jānatā pana tayā, āvuso sāriputta, kathaṁ passatā aññā byākatā—
sn12.32:8.3 khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyāti pajānāmī’ti;
sn12.32:8.4 evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyaṁ:
sn12.32:8.5 ‘yaṁnidānā, āvuso, jāti, tassa nidānassa khayā khīṇasmiṁ khīṇāmhīti viditaṁ.
sn12.32:8.6 Khīṇāmhīti viditvā—
sn12.32:8.7 khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyāti pajānāmī’ti.
sn12.32:8.8 Evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyan”ti.
sn12.32:9.1 “Sace pana taṁ, sāriputta, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.32:9.2 ‘jāti panāvuso sāriputta, kiṁnidānā kiṁsamudayā kiṁjātikā kiṁpabhavā’ti?
sn12.32:9.3 Evaṁ puṭṭho taṁ, sāriputta, kinti byākareyyāsī”ti?
sn12.32:9.4 “Sace maṁ, bhante, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.32:9.5 ‘jāti panāvuso sāriputta, kiṁnidānā kiṁsamudayā kiṁjātikā kiṁpabhavā’ti?
sn12.32:9.6 Evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyaṁ:
sn12.32:9.7 ‘jāti kho, āvuso, bhavanidānā bhavasamudayā bhavajātikā bhavappabhavā’ti.
sn12.32:9.8 Evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyan”ti.
sn12.32:10.1 “Sace pana taṁ, sāriputta, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.32:10.2 ‘bhavo panāvuso sāriputta, kiṁnidāno kiṁsamudayo kiṁjātiko kiṁpabhavo’ti?
sn12.32:10.3 Evaṁ puṭṭho tvaṁ, sāriputta, kinti byākareyyāsī”ti?
sn12.32:10.4 “Sace maṁ, bhante, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.32:10.5 ‘bhavo panāvuso sāriputta, kiṁnidāno kiṁsamudayo kiṁjātiko kiṁpabhavo’ti?
sn12.32:10.6 Evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyaṁ:
sn12.32:10.7 ‘bhavo kho, āvuso, upādānanidāno upādānasamudayo upādānajātiko upādānappabhavo’ti.
sn12.32:10.8 Evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyan”ti.
sn12.32:11.1 “Sace pana taṁ, sāriputta, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.32:11.2 ‘upādānaṁ panāvuso …pe…
sn12.32:11.3 sace pana taṁ, sāriputta, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ—
sn12.32:11.4 taṇhā panāvuso sāriputta, kiṁnidānā kiṁsamudayā kiṁjātikā kiṁpabhavā’ti?
sn12.32:11.5 Evaṁ puṭṭho tvaṁ, sāriputta, kinti byākareyyāsī”ti?
sn12.32:11.6 “Sace maṁ, bhante, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.32:11.7 ‘taṇhā panāvuso sāriputta, kiṁnidānā kiṁsamudayā kiṁjātikā kiṁpabhavā’ti?
sn12.32:11.8 Evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyaṁ:
sn12.32:11.9 ‘taṇhā kho, āvuso, vedanānidānā vedanāsamudayā vedanājātikā vedanāpabhavā’ti.
sn12.32:11.10 Evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyan”ti.
sn12.32:12.1 “Sace pana taṁ, sāriputta, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.32:12.2 ‘kathaṁ jānato pana te, āvuso sāriputta, kathaṁ passato yā vedanāsu nandī sā na upaṭṭhāsī’ti.
sn12.32:12.3 Evaṁ puṭṭho tvaṁ, sāriputta, kinti byākareyyāsī”ti?
sn12.32:12.4 “Sace maṁ, bhante, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.32:12.5 ‘kathaṁ jānato pana te, āvuso sāriputta, kathaṁ passato yā vedanāsu nandī sā na upaṭṭhāsī’ti evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyaṁ:
sn12.32:12.6 ‘tisso kho imā, āvuso, vedanā.
sn12.32:12.7 Katamā tisso?
sn12.32:12.8 Sukhā vedanā, dukkhā vedanā, adukkhamasukhā vedanā.
sn12.32:12.9 Imā kho, āvuso, tisso vedanā aniccā.
sn12.32:12.10 Yadaniccaṁ taṁ dukkhanti
sn12.32:12.11 viditaṁ, yā vedanāsu nandī sā na upaṭṭhāsī’ti.
sn12.32:12.12 Evaṁ, puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyan”ti.
sn12.32:13.1 “Sādhu sādhu, sāriputta.
sn12.32:13.2 Ayampi kho, sāriputta, pariyāyo, etasseva atthassa saṅkhittena veyyākaraṇāya:
sn12.32:13.3 ‘yaṁ kiñci vedayitaṁ taṁ dukkhasmin’”ti.
sn12.32:14.1 “Sace pana taṁ, sāriputta, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.32:14.2 ‘kathaṁ vimokkhā pana tayā, āvuso sāriputta, aññā byākatā—
sn12.32:14.3 khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyāti pajānāmī’ti?
sn12.32:14.4 Evaṁ puṭṭho tvaṁ, sāriputta, kinti byākareyyāsī”ti?
sn12.32:14.5 “Sace maṁ, bhante, evaṁ puccheyyuṁ:
sn12.32:14.6 ‘kathaṁ vimokkhā pana tayā, āvuso sāriputta, aññā byākatā—
sn12.32:14.7 khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyāti pajānāmī’ti.
sn12.32:14.8 Evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyaṁ:
sn12.32:14.9 ‘ajjhattaṁ vimokkhā khvāhaṁ, āvuso, sabbupādānakkhayā tathā sato viharāmi yathā sataṁ viharantaṁ āsavā nānussavanti, attānañca nāvajānāmī’ti.
sn12.32:14.10 Evaṁ puṭṭhohaṁ, bhante, evaṁ byākareyyan”ti.
sn12.32:15.1 “Sādhu sādhu, sāriputta.
sn12.32:15.2 Ayampi kho sāriputta, pariyāyo etasseva atthassa saṅkhittena veyyākaraṇāya—
sn12.32:15.3 ye āsavā samaṇena vuttā tesvāhaṁ na kaṅkhāmi, te me pahīnāti na vicikicchāmī”ti.
sn12.32:15.4 Idamavoca bhagavā.
sn12.32:15.5 Idaṁ vatvā sugato uṭṭhāyāsanā vihāraṁ pāvisi.
sn12.32:16.1 Tatra kho āyasmā sāriputto acirapakkantassa bhagavato bhikkhū āmantesi:
sn12.32:16.2 “pubbe appaṭisaṁviditaṁ maṁ, āvuso, bhagavā paṭhamaṁ pañhaṁ apucchi, tassa me ahosi dandhāyitattaṁ.
sn12.32:16.3 Yato ca kho me, āvuso, bhagavā paṭhamaṁ pañhaṁ anumodi, tassa mayhaṁ, āvuso, etadahosi—
sn12.32:16.4 divasañcepi maṁ bhagavā etamatthaṁ puccheyya aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi, divasampāhaṁ bhagavato etamatthaṁ byākareyyaṁ aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi.
sn12.32:16.5 Rattiñcepi maṁ bhagavā etamatthaṁ puccheyya aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi, rattimpāhaṁ bhagavato etamatthaṁ byākareyyaṁ aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi.
sn12.32:16.6 Rattindivaṁ cepi maṁ bhagavā etamatthaṁ puccheyya aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi, rattindivampāhaṁ bhagavato etamatthaṁ byākareyyaṁ aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi.
sn12.32:16.7 Dve rattindivāni cepi maṁ bhagavā etamatthaṁ puccheyya …pe…
sn12.32:16.8 dve rattindivānipāhaṁ bhagavato etamatthaṁ byākareyyaṁ …pe…
sn12.32:16.9 tīṇi rattindivāni cepi maṁ bhagavā etamatthaṁ puccheyya …pe…
sn12.32:16.10 tīṇi rattindivānipāhaṁ bhagavato etamatthaṁ byākareyyaṁ …pe…
sn12.32:16.11 cattāri rattindivāni cepi maṁ bhagavā etamatthaṁ puccheyya …pe…
sn12.32:16.12 cattāri rattindivānipāhaṁ bhagavato etamatthaṁ byākareyyaṁ …pe…
sn12.32:16.13 pañca rattindivāni cepi maṁ bhagavā etamatthaṁ puccheyya …pe…
sn12.32:16.14 pañca rattindivānipāhaṁ bhagavato etamatthaṁ byākareyyaṁ …pe…
sn12.32:16.15 cha rattindivāni cepi maṁ bhagavā etamatthaṁ puccheyya …pe…
sn12.32:16.16 cha rattindivānipāhaṁ bhagavato etamatthaṁ byākareyyaṁ …pe…
sn12.32:16.17 satta rattindivāni cepi maṁ bhagavā etamatthaṁ puccheyya aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi, satta rattindivānipāhaṁ bhagavato etamatthaṁ byākareyyaṁ aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehī”ti.
sn12.32:17.1 Atha kho kaḷārakhattiyo bhikkhu uṭṭhāyāsanā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho kaḷārakhattiyo bhikkhu bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.32:17.2 “āyasmatā, bhante, sāriputtena sīhanādo nadito—
sn12.32:17.3 pubbe appaṭisaṁviditaṁ maṁ, āvuso, bhagavā paṭhamaṁ pañhaṁ apucchi, tassa me ahosi dandhāyitattaṁ.
sn12.32:17.4 Yato ca kho me, āvuso, bhagavā paṭhamaṁ pañhaṁ anumodi, tassa mayhaṁ, āvuso, etadahosi—
sn12.32:17.5 divasañcepi maṁ bhagavā etamatthaṁ puccheyya aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi, divasampāhaṁ bhagavato etamatthaṁ byākareyyaṁ aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi;
sn12.32:17.6 rattiñcepi …pe…
sn12.32:17.7 rattindivañcepi maṁ bhagavā …pe…
sn12.32:17.8 dve rattindivāni cepi maṁ bhagavā …pe…
sn12.32:17.9 tīṇi …
sn12.32:17.10 cattāri …
sn12.32:17.11 pañca …
sn12.32:17.12 cha …
sn12.32:17.13 satta rattindivāni cepi maṁ bhagavā etamatthaṁ puccheyya aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi, satta rattindivānipāhaṁ bhagavato etamatthaṁ byākareyyaṁ aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehī”ti.
sn12.32:18.1 “Sā hi, bhikkhu, sāriputtassa dhammadhātu suppaṭividdhā, yassā dhammadhātuyā suppaṭividdhattā divasaṁ cepāhaṁ sāriputtaṁ etamatthaṁ puccheyyaṁ aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi, divasampi me sāriputto etamatthaṁ byākareyya aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi.
sn12.32:18.2 Rattiṁ cepāhaṁ sāriputtaṁ etamatthaṁ puccheyyaṁ aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi, rattimpi me sāriputto etamatthaṁ byākareyya …pe…
sn12.32:18.3 rattindivaṁ cepāhaṁ sāriputtaṁ etamatthaṁ puccheyyaṁ, rattindivampi me sāriputto etamatthaṁ byākareyya …

sn12.32:18.5 tīṇi rattindivāni cepāhaṁ sāriputtaṁ etamatthaṁ puccheyyaṁ, tīṇi rattindivānipi me sāriputto etamatthaṁ byākareyya …
sn12.32:18.6 cattāri rattindivāni cepāhaṁ sāriputtaṁ etamatthaṁ puccheyyaṁ, cattāri rattindivānipi me sāriputto etamatthaṁ byākareyya …

sn12.32:18.8 cha rattindivāni cepāhaṁ sāriputtaṁ etamatthaṁ puccheyyaṁ, cha rattindivānipi me sāriputto etamatthaṁ byākareyya …
sn12.32:18.9 satta rattindivāni cepāhaṁ sāriputtaṁ etamatthaṁ puccheyyaṁ aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehi, satta rattindivānipi me sāriputto etamatthaṁ byākareyya aññamaññehi padehi aññamaññehi pariyāyehī”ti.
