sn12.33:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.33
sn12.33:0.2 4. Kaḷārakhattiyavagga
sn12.33:0.3 Ñāṇavatthusutta
sn12.33:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ …
sn12.33:1.2 “Catucattārīsaṁ vo, bhikkhave, ñāṇavatthūni desessāmi,
sn12.33:1.3 taṁ suṇātha, sādhukaṁ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmī”ti.
sn12.33:1.4 “Evaṁ, bhante”ti kho te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.
sn12.33:1.5 Bhagavā etadavoca:
sn12.33:2.1 “Katamāni, bhikkhave, catucattārīsaṁ ñāṇavatthūni?
sn12.33:2.2 Jarāmaraṇe ñāṇaṁ, jarāmaraṇasamudaye ñāṇaṁ, jarāmaraṇanirodhe ñāṇaṁ, jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.33:2.3 jātiyā ñāṇaṁ, jātisamudaye ñāṇaṁ, jātinirodhe ñāṇaṁ, jātinirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.33:2.4 bhave ñāṇaṁ, bhavasamudaye ñāṇaṁ, bhavanirodhe ñāṇaṁ, bhavanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.33:2.5 upādāne ñāṇaṁ, upādānasamudaye ñāṇaṁ, upādānanirodhe ñāṇaṁ, upādānanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.33:2.6 taṇhāya ñāṇaṁ, taṇhāsamudaye ñāṇaṁ, taṇhānirodhe ñāṇaṁ, taṇhānirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.33:2.7 vedanāya ñāṇaṁ, vedanāsamudaye ñāṇaṁ, vedanānirodhe ñāṇaṁ, vedanānirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.33:2.8 phasse ñāṇaṁ …pe…
sn12.33:2.9 saḷāyatane ñāṇaṁ …
sn12.33:2.10 nāmarūpe ñāṇaṁ …
sn12.33:2.11 viññāṇe ñāṇaṁ …
sn12.33:2.12 saṅkhāresu ñāṇaṁ, saṅkhārasamudaye ñāṇaṁ, saṅkhāranirodhe ñāṇaṁ, saṅkhāranirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ñāṇaṁ.
sn12.33:2.13 Imāni vuccanti, bhikkhave, catucattārīsaṁ ñāṇavatthūni.
sn12.33:3.1 Katamañca, bhikkhave, jarāmaraṇaṁ?
sn12.33:3.2 Yā tesaṁ tesaṁ sattānaṁ tamhi tamhi sattanikāye jarā jīraṇatā khaṇḍiccaṁ pāliccaṁ valittacatā āyuno saṁhāni indriyānaṁ paripāko,
sn12.33:3.3 ayaṁ vuccati jarā.
sn12.33:3.4 Yā tesaṁ tesaṁ sattānaṁ tamhā tamhā sattanikāyā cuti cavanatā bhedo antaradhānaṁ maccu maraṇaṁ kālakiriyā khandhānaṁ bhedo kaḷevarassa nikkhepo.
sn12.33:3.5 Idaṁ vuccati maraṇaṁ.
sn12.33:3.6 Iti ayañca jarā, idañca maraṇaṁ;
sn12.33:3.7 idaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, jarāmaraṇaṁ.
sn12.33:4.1 Jātisamudayā jarāmaraṇasamudayo;
sn12.33:4.2 jātinirodhā jarāmaraṇanirodho;
sn12.33:4.3 ayameva ariyo aṭṭhaṅgiko maggo jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminī paṭipadā, seyyathidaṁ—
sn12.33:4.4 sammādiṭṭhi …pe… sammāsamādhi.
sn12.33:5.1 Yato kho, bhikkhave, ariyasāvako evaṁ jarāmaraṇaṁ pajānāti, evaṁ jarāmaraṇasamudayaṁ pajānāti, evaṁ jarāmaraṇanirodhaṁ pajānāti, evaṁ jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ pajānāti, idamassa dhamme ñāṇaṁ.
sn12.33:5.2 So iminā dhammena diṭṭhena viditena akālikena pattena pariyogāḷhena atītānāgatena yaṁ neti.
sn12.33:6.1 Ye kho keci atītamaddhānaṁ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā jarāmaraṇaṁ abbhaññaṁsu, jarāmaraṇasamudayaṁ abbhaññaṁsu, jarāmaraṇanirodhaṁ abbhaññaṁsu, jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ abbhaññaṁsu, sabbete evameva abbhaññaṁsu, seyyathāpāhaṁ etarahi.
sn12.33:7.1 Yepi hi keci anāgatamaddhānaṁ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā jarāmaraṇaṁ abhijānissanti, jarāmaraṇasamudayaṁ abhijānissanti, jarāmaraṇanirodhaṁ abhijānissanti, jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ abhijānissanti, sabbete evameva abhijānissanti, seyyathāpāhaṁ etarahīti.
sn12.33:7.2 Idamassa anvaye ñāṇaṁ.
sn12.33:8.1 Yato kho, bhikkhave, ariyasāvakassa imāni dve ñāṇāni parisuddhāni honti pariyodātāni—
sn12.33:8.2 dhamme ñāṇañca anvaye ñāṇañca.
sn12.33:8.3 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, ariyasāvako diṭṭhisampanno itipi, dassanasampanno itipi, āgato imaṁ saddhammaṁ itipi, passati imaṁ saddhammaṁ itipi, sekkhena ñāṇena samannāgato itipi, sekkhāya vijjāya samannāgato itipi, dhammasotaṁ samāpanno itipi, ariyo nibbedhikapañño itipi, amatadvāraṁ āhacca tiṭṭhati itipīti.
sn12.33:9.1 Katamā ca, bhikkhave, jāti …
sn12.33:9.2 katamo ca, bhikkhave, bhavo …
sn12.33:9.3 katamañca, bhikkhave, upādānaṁ …
sn12.33:9.4 katamā ca, bhikkhave, taṇhā …
sn12.33:9.5 katamā ca, bhikkhave, vedanā …
sn12.33:9.6 katamo ca, bhikkhave, phasso …
sn12.33:9.7 katamañca, bhikkhave, saḷāyatanaṁ …
sn12.33:9.8 katamañca, bhikkhave, nāmarūpaṁ …
sn12.33:9.9 katamañca, bhikkhave, viññāṇaṁ …
sn12.33:9.10 katame ca, bhikkhave, saṅkhārā?
sn12.33:9.11 Tayome, bhikkhave, saṅkhārā—
sn12.33:9.12 kāyasaṅkhāro, vacīsaṅkhāro, cittasaṅkhāroti.
sn12.33:9.13 Ime vuccanti, bhikkhave, saṅkhārā.
sn12.33:10.1 Avijjāsamudayā saṅkhārasamudayo;
sn12.33:10.2 avijjānirodhā saṅkhāranirodho;
sn12.33:10.3 ayameva ariyo aṭṭhaṅgiko maggo saṅkhāranirodhagāminī paṭipadā, seyyathidaṁ—
sn12.33:10.4 sammādiṭṭhi …pe… sammāsamādhi.
sn12.33:11.1 Yato kho, bhikkhave, ariyasāvako evaṁ saṅkhāre pajānāti, evaṁ saṅkhārasamudayaṁ pajānāti, evaṁ saṅkhāranirodhaṁ pajānāti, evaṁ saṅkhāranirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ pajānāti, idamassa dhamme ñāṇaṁ.
sn12.33:11.2 So iminā dhammena diṭṭhena viditena akālikena pattena pariyogāḷhena atītānāgatena yaṁ neti.
sn12.33:12.1 Ye kho keci atītamaddhānaṁ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā saṅkhāre abbhaññaṁsu, saṅkhārasamudayaṁ abbhaññaṁsu, saṅkhāranirodhaṁ abbhaññaṁsu, saṅkhāranirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ abbhaññaṁsu, sabbete evameva abbhaññaṁsu, seyyathāpāhaṁ etarahi.
sn12.33:13.1 Ye hipi keci anāgatamaddhānaṁ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā saṅkhāre abhijānissanti, saṅkhārasamudayaṁ abhijānissanti, saṅkhāranirodhaṁ abhijānissanti, saṅkhāranirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ abhijānissanti, sabbete evameva abhijānissanti, seyyathāpāhaṁ etarahi.
sn12.33:13.2 Idamassa anvaye ñāṇaṁ.
sn12.33:14.1 Yato kho, bhikkhave, ariyasāvakassa imāni dve ñāṇāni parisuddhāni honti pariyodātāni—
sn12.33:14.2 dhamme ñāṇañca anvaye ñāṇañca.
sn12.33:14.3 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, ariyasāvako diṭṭhisampanno itipi, dassanasampanno itipi, āgato imaṁ saddhammaṁ itipi, passati imaṁ saddhammaṁ itipi, sekkhena ñāṇena samannāgato itipi, sekkhāya vijjāya samannāgato itipi, dhammasotaṁ samāpanno itipi, ariyo nibbedhikapañño itipi, amatadvāraṁ āhacca tiṭṭhati itipī”ti.
sn12.33:14.4 Tatiyaṁ. "
sn12.34:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.34
sn12.34:0.2 4. Kaḷārakhattiyavagga
sn12.34:0.3 Dutiyañāṇavatthusutta
sn12.34:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.34:1.2 “Sattasattari vo, bhikkhave, ñāṇavatthūni desessāmi.
sn12.34:1.3 Taṁ suṇātha, sādhukaṁ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmī”ti.
sn12.34:1.4 “Evaṁ, bhante”ti kho te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.
sn12.34:1.5 Bhagavā etadavoca:
sn12.34:2.1 “Katamāni, bhikkhave, sattasattari ñāṇavatthūni?
sn12.34:2.2 Jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇanti ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.34:2.3 asati jātiyā natthi jarāmaraṇanti ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.34:2.4 atītampi addhānaṁ jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇanti ñāṇaṁ, asati jātiyā natthi jarāmaraṇanti ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.34:2.5 anāgatampi addhānaṁ jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇanti ñāṇaṁ, asati jātiyā natthi jarāmaraṇanti ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.34:2.6 yampissa taṁ dhammaṭṭhitiñāṇaṁ tampi khayadhammaṁ vayadhammaṁ virāgadhammaṁ nirodhadhammanti ñāṇaṁ.
sn12.34:3.1 Bhavapaccayā jātīti ñāṇaṁ …pe…
sn12.34:3.2 upādānapaccayā bhavoti ñāṇaṁ …
sn12.34:3.3 taṇhāpaccayā upādānanti ñāṇaṁ …
sn12.34:3.4 vedanāpaccayā taṇhāti ñāṇaṁ …
sn12.34:3.5 phassapaccayā vedanāti ñāṇaṁ …
sn12.34:3.6 saḷāyatanapaccayā phassoti ñāṇaṁ …
sn12.34:3.7 nāmarūpapaccayā saḷāyatananti ñāṇaṁ …
sn12.34:3.8 viññāṇapaccayā nāmarūpanti ñāṇaṁ …
sn12.34:3.9 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇanti ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.34:3.10 avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārāti ñāṇaṁ, asati avijjāya natthi saṅkhārāti ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.34:3.11 atītampi addhānaṁ avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārāti ñāṇaṁ, asati avijjāya natthi saṅkhārāti ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.34:3.12 anāgatampi addhānaṁ avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārāti ñāṇaṁ, asati avijjāya natthi saṅkhārāti ñāṇaṁ;
sn12.34:3.13 yampissa taṁ dhammaṭṭhitiñāṇaṁ tampi khayadhammaṁ vayadhammaṁ virāgadhammaṁ nirodhadhammanti ñāṇaṁ.
sn12.34:3.14 Imāni vuccanti, bhikkhave, sattasattari ñāṇavatthūnī”ti.
sn12.34:3.15 Catutthaṁ. "
sn12.35:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.35
sn12.35:0.2 4. Kaḷārakhattiyavagga
sn12.35:0.3 Avijjāpaccayasutta
sn12.35:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.35:1.2 “Avijjāpaccayā, bhikkhave, saṅkhārā;
sn12.35:1.3 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ …pe…
sn12.35:1.4 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hotī”ti.
sn12.35:1.5 Evaṁ vutte, aññataro bhikkhu bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.35:1.6 “‘katamaṁ nu kho, bhante, jarāmaraṇaṁ, kassa ca panidaṁ jarāmaraṇan’ti?
sn12.35:1.7 ‘No kallo pañho’ti bhagavā avoca, ‘katamaṁ jarāmaraṇaṁ, kassa ca panidaṁ jarāmaraṇan’ti iti vā, bhikkhu, yo vadeyya, ‘aññaṁ jarāmaraṇaṁ aññassa ca panidaṁ jarāmaraṇan’ti, iti vā, bhikkhu, yo vadeyya, ubhayametaṁ ekatthaṁ byañjanameva nānaṁ.
sn12.35:1.8 Taṁ jīvaṁ taṁ sarīranti vā, bhikkhu, diṭṭhiyā sati brahmacariyavāso na hoti.
sn12.35:1.9 Aññaṁ jīvaṁ aññaṁ sarīranti vā, bhikkhu, diṭṭhiyā sati brahmacariyavāso na hoti.
sn12.35:1.10 Ete te, bhikkhu, ubho ante anupagamma majjhena tathāgato dhammaṁ deseti:
sn12.35:1.11 ‘jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇan’”ti.
sn12.35:2.1 “Katamā nu kho, bhante, jāti, kassa ca panāyaṁ jātī”ti?
sn12.35:2.2 “No kallo pañho”ti bhagavā avoca, “‘katamā jāti, kassa ca panāyaṁ jātī’ti iti vā, bhikkhu, yo vadeyya, ‘aññā jāti aññassa ca panāyaṁ jātī’ti iti vā, bhikkhu, yo vadeyya, ubhayametaṁ ekatthaṁ byañjanameva nānaṁ.
sn12.35:2.3 Taṁ jīvaṁ taṁ sarīranti vā, bhikkhu, diṭṭhiyā sati brahmacariyavāso na hoti.
sn12.35:2.4 Aññaṁ jīvaṁ aññaṁ sarīranti vā, bhikkhu, diṭṭhiyā sati brahmacariyavāso na hoti.
sn12.35:2.5 Ete te, bhikkhu, ubho ante anupagamma majjhena tathāgato dhammaṁ deseti:
sn12.35:2.6 ‘bhavapaccayā jātī’”ti.

sn12.41:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.41
sn12.41:0.2 5. Gahapativagga
sn12.41:0.3 Pañcaverabhayasutta
sn12.41:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.41:1.2 Atha kho anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinnaṁ kho anāthapiṇḍikaṁ gahapatiṁ bhagavā etadavoca:
sn12.41:2.1 “Yato kho, gahapati, ariyasāvakassa pañca bhayāni verāni vūpasantāni honti, catūhi ca sotāpattiyaṅgehi samannāgato hoti, ariyo cassa ñāyo paññāya sudiṭṭho hoti suppaṭividdho, so ākaṅkhamāno attanāva attānaṁ byākareyya:
sn12.41:2.2 ‘khīṇanirayomhi khīṇatiracchānayoni khīṇapettivisayo khīṇāpāyaduggativinipāto, sotāpannohamasmi avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano’ti.
sn12.41:3.1 Katamāni pañca bhayāni verāni vūpasantāni honti?
sn12.41:3.2 Yaṁ, gahapati, pāṇātipātī pāṇātipātapaccayā diṭṭhadhammikampi bhayaṁ veraṁ pasavati, samparāyikampi bhayaṁ veraṁ pasavati, cetasikampi dukkhaṁ domanassaṁ paṭisaṁvedayati, pāṇātipātā paṭiviratassa evaṁ taṁ bhayaṁ veraṁ vūpasantaṁ hoti.
sn12.41:4.1 Yaṁ, gahapati, adinnādāyī adinnādānapaccayā diṭṭhadhammikampi bhayaṁ veraṁ pasavati, samparāyikampi bhayaṁ veraṁ pasavati, cetasikampi dukkhaṁ domanassaṁ paṭisaṁvedayati, adinnādānā paṭiviratassa evaṁ taṁ bhayaṁ veraṁ vūpasantaṁ hoti.
sn12.41:5.1 Yaṁ, gahapati, kāmesumicchācārī kāmesumicchācārapaccayā diṭṭhadhammikampi bhayaṁ veraṁ pasavati, samparāyikampi bhayaṁ veraṁ pasavati, cetasikampi dukkhaṁ domanassaṁ paṭisaṁvedayati, kāmesumicchācārā paṭiviratassa evaṁ taṁ bhayaṁ veraṁ vūpasantaṁ hoti.
sn12.41:6.1 Yaṁ, gahapati, musāvādī musāvādapaccayā diṭṭhadhammikampi bhayaṁ veraṁ pasavati, samparāyikampi bhayaṁ veraṁ pasavati, cetasikampi dukkhaṁ domanassaṁ paṭisaṁvedayati, musāvādā paṭiviratassa evaṁ taṁ bhayaṁ veraṁ vūpasantaṁ hoti.
sn12.41:7.1 Yaṁ, gahapati, surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhāyī surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhānapaccayā diṭṭhadhammikampi bhayaṁ veraṁ pasavati, samparāyikampi bhayaṁ veraṁ pasavati, cetasikampi dukkhaṁ domanassaṁ paṭisaṁvedayati, surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhānā paṭiviratassa evaṁ taṁ bhayaṁ veraṁ vūpasantaṁ hoti.
sn12.41:7.2 Imāni pañca bhayāni verāni vūpasantāni honti.
sn12.41:8.1 Katamehi catūhi sotāpattiyaṅgehi samannāgato hoti?
sn12.41:8.2 Idha, gahapati, ariyasāvako buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti:
sn12.41:8.3 ‘itipi so bhagavā arahaṁ sammāsambuddho vijjācaraṇasampanno sugato lokavidū anuttaro purisadammasārathi satthā devamanussānaṁ buddho bhagavā’ti.
sn12.41:9.1 Dhamme aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti:
sn12.41:9.2 ‘svākkhāto bhagavatā dhammo sandiṭṭhiko akāliko ehipassiko opaneyyiko paccattaṁ veditabbo viññūhī’ti.
sn12.41:10.1 Saṅghe aveccappasādena samannāgato hoti:
sn12.41:10.2 ‘suppaṭipanno bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho, ujuppaṭipanno bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho, ñāyappaṭipanno bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho, sāmīcippaṭipanno bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho, yadidaṁ cattāri purisayugāni aṭṭha purisapuggalā, esa bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho āhuneyyo pāhuneyyo dakkhiṇeyyo añjalikaraṇīyo anuttaraṁ puññakkhettaṁ lokassā’ti.
sn12.41:11.1 Ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgato hoti akhaṇḍehi acchiddehi asabalehi akammāsehi bhujissehi viññuppasatthehi aparāmaṭṭhehi samādhisaṁvattanikehi.
sn12.41:11.2 Imehi catūhi sotāpattiyaṅgehi samannāgato hoti.
sn12.41:12.1 Katamo cassa ariyo ñāyo paññāya sudiṭṭho hoti suppaṭividdho?
sn12.41:12.2 Idha, gahapati, ariyasāvako paṭiccasamuppādaññeva sādhukaṁ yoniso manasi karoti:
sn12.41:12.3 ‘iti imasmiṁ sati idaṁ hoti, imasmiṁ asati idaṁ na hoti;
sn12.41:12.4 imassuppādā idaṁ uppajjati, imassa nirodhā idaṁ nirujjhati.
sn12.41:12.5 Yadidaṁ avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā;
sn12.41:12.6 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ …pe…
sn12.41:12.7 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.41:12.8 Avijjāya tveva asesavirāganirodhā saṅkhāranirodho;
sn12.41:12.9 saṅkhāranirodhā viññāṇanirodho …pe…
sn12.41:12.10 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hoti.
sn12.41:12.11 Ayamassa ariyo ñāyo paññāya sudiṭṭho hoti suppaṭividdho.
sn12.41:13.1 Yato kho, gahapati, ariyasāvakassa imāni pañca bhayāni verāni vūpasantāni honti, imehi catūhi sotāpattiyaṅgehi samannāgato hoti, ayañcassa ariyo ñāyo paññāya sudiṭṭho hoti suppaṭividdho, so ākaṅkhamāno attanāva attānaṁ byākareyya:
sn12.41:13.2 ‘khīṇanirayomhi khīṇatiracchānayoni khīṇapettivisayo khīṇāpāyaduggativinipāto, sotāpannohamasmi avinipātadhammo niyato sambodhiparāyano’”ti.

sn12.47:4.1 Evaṁ vutte, jāṇussoṇi brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:

sn12.47:4.3 pāṇupetaṁ saraṇaṁ gatan”ti.
sn12.47:4.4 Sattamaṁ. "

sn12.48:0.2 5. Gahapativagga
sn12.48:0.3 Lokāyatikasutta
sn12.48:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.48:1.2 Atha kho lokāyatiko brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā …pe…

sn12.48:3.1 “Kiṁ pana, bho gotama, sabbaṁ natthī”ti?
sn12.48:3.2 “‘Sabbaṁ natthī’ti kho, brāhmaṇa, dutiyametaṁ lokāyataṁ”.
sn12.48:4.1 “Kiṁ nu kho, bho gotama, sabbamekattan”ti?
sn12.48:4.2 “‘Sabbamekattan’ti kho, brāhmaṇa, tatiyametaṁ lokāyataṁ”.

sn12.48:6.2 ‘avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā;
sn12.48:6.3 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ …pe…

sn12.49:0.3 Ariyasāvakasutta
sn12.49:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.49:1.2 “Na, bhikkhave, sutavato ariyasāvakassa evaṁ hoti:
sn12.49:1.3 ‘kiṁ nu kho—
sn12.49:1.4 kismiṁ sati kiṁ hoti, kissuppādā kiṁ uppajjati?
sn12.49:1.5 Kismiṁ sati saṅkhārā honti, kismiṁ sati viññāṇaṁ hoti, kismiṁ sati nāmarūpaṁ hoti, kismiṁ sati saḷāyatanaṁ hoti, kismiṁ sati phasso hoti, kismiṁ sati vedanā hoti, kismiṁ sati taṇhā hoti, kismiṁ sati upādānaṁ hoti, kismiṁ sati bhavo hoti, kismiṁ sati jāti hoti, kismiṁ sati jarāmaraṇaṁ hotī’ti?
sn12.49:2.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, sutavato ariyasāvakassa aparappaccayā ñāṇamevettha hoti:
sn12.49:2.2 ‘imasmiṁ sati idaṁ hoti, imassuppādā idaṁ uppajjati.
sn12.49:2.3 Avijjāya sati saṅkhārā honti;
sn12.49:2.4 saṅkhāresu sati viññāṇaṁ hoti;
sn12.49:2.5 viññāṇe sati nāmarūpaṁ hoti;
sn12.49:2.6 nāmarūpe sati saḷāyatanaṁ hoti;
sn12.49:2.7 saḷāyatane sati phasso hoti;
sn12.49:2.8 phasse sati vedanā hoti;
sn12.49:2.9 vedanāya sati taṇhā hoti;
sn12.49:2.10 taṇhāya sati upādānaṁ hoti;
sn12.49:2.11 upādāne sati bhavo hoti;
sn12.49:2.12 bhave sati jāti hoti;
sn12.49:2.13 jātiyā sati jarāmaraṇaṁ hotī’ti.
sn12.49:2.14 So evaṁ pajānāti:
sn12.49:2.15 ‘evamayaṁ loko samudayatī’ti.
sn12.49:3.1 Na, bhikkhave, sutavato ariyasāvakassa evaṁ hoti:
sn12.49:3.2 ‘kiṁ nu kho—
sn12.49:3.3 kismiṁ asati kiṁ na hoti, kissa nirodhā kiṁ nirujjhati?
sn12.49:3.4 Kismiṁ asati saṅkhārā na honti, kismiṁ asati viññāṇaṁ na hoti, kismiṁ asati nāmarūpaṁ na hoti, kismiṁ asati saḷāyatanaṁ na hoti, kismiṁ asati phasso na hoti, kismiṁ asati vedanā na hoti, kismiṁ asati taṇhā na hoti, kismiṁ asati upādānaṁ na hoti, kismiṁ asati bhavo na hoti, kismiṁ asati jāti na hoti, kismiṁ asati jarāmaraṇaṁ na hotī’ti?
sn12.49:4.1 Atha kho, bhikkhave, sutavato ariyasāvakassa aparappaccayā ñāṇamevettha hoti:
sn12.49:4.2 ‘imasmiṁ asati idaṁ na hoti, imassa nirodhā idaṁ nirujjhati.
sn12.49:4.3 Avijjāya asati saṅkhārā na honti;
sn12.49:4.4 saṅkhāresu asati viññāṇaṁ na hoti;
sn12.49:4.5 viññāṇe asati nāmarūpaṁ na hoti;
sn12.49:4.6 nāmarūpe asati saḷāyatanaṁ na hoti …pe…
sn12.49:4.7 bhavo na hoti …
sn12.49:4.8 jāti na hoti …
sn12.49:4.9 jātiyā asati jarāmaraṇaṁ na hotī’ti.
sn12.49:4.10 So evaṁ pajānāti:
sn12.49:4.11 ‘evamayaṁ loko nirujjhatī’ti.
sn12.49:5.1 Yato kho, bhikkhave, ariyasāvako evaṁ lokassa samudayañca atthaṅgamañca yathābhūtaṁ pajānāti, ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, ariyasāvako diṭṭhisampanno itipi …pe…
sn12.49:5.2 amatadvāraṁ āhacca tiṭṭhati itipī”ti.
sn12.49:5.3 Navamaṁ. "

sn12.51:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.51
sn12.51:0.2 6. Dukkhavagga
sn12.51:0.3 Parivīmaṁsanasutta
sn12.51:1.1 Evaṁ me sutaṁ—
sn12.51:1.2 ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.
sn12.51:1.3 Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi:
sn12.51:1.4 “bhikkhavo”ti.
sn12.51:1.5 “Bhadante”ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.
sn12.51:1.6 Bhagavā etadavoca:
sn12.51:2.1 “Kittāvatā nu kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu parivīmaṁsamāno parivīmaṁseyya sabbaso sammā dukkhakkhayāyā”ti?
sn12.51:2.2 “Bhagavaṁmūlakā no, bhante, dhammā bhagavaṁnettikā bhagavaṁpaṭisaraṇā. Sādhu vata, bhante, bhagavantaṁyeva paṭibhātu etassa bhāsitassa attho. Bhagavato sutvā bhikkhū dhāressantī”ti.
sn12.51:2.3 “Tena hi, bhikkhave, suṇātha, sādhukaṁ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmī”ti.
sn12.51:2.4 “Evaṁ, bhante”ti kho te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.
sn12.51:2.5 Bhagavā etadavoca:
sn12.51:3.1 “Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu parivīmaṁsamāno parivīmaṁsati:
sn12.51:3.2 ‘yaṁ kho idaṁ anekavidhaṁ nānappakārakaṁ dukkhaṁ loke uppajjati jarāmaraṇaṁ;
sn12.51:3.3 idaṁ nu kho dukkhaṁ kiṁnidānaṁ kiṁsamudayaṁ kiṁjātikaṁ kiṁpabhavaṁ?
sn12.51:3.4 Kismiṁ sati jarāmaraṇaṁ hoti, kismiṁ asati jarāmaraṇaṁ na hotī’ti?
sn12.51:3.5 So parivīmaṁsamāno evaṁ pajānāti:
sn12.51:3.6 ‘yaṁ kho idaṁ anekavidhaṁ nānappakārakaṁ dukkhaṁ loke uppajjati jarāmaraṇaṁ, idaṁ kho dukkhaṁ jātinidānaṁ jātisamudayaṁ jātijātikaṁ jātippabhavaṁ.
sn12.51:3.7 Jātiyā sati jarāmaraṇaṁ hoti, jātiyā asati jarāmaraṇaṁ na hotī’ti.
sn12.51:4.1 So jarāmaraṇañca pajānāti, jarāmaraṇasamudayañca pajānāti, jarāmaraṇanirodhañca pajānāti, yā ca jarāmaraṇanirodhasāruppagāminī paṭipadā tañca pajānāti, tathā paṭipanno ca hoti anudhammacārī;
sn12.51:4.2 ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sabbaso sammā dukkhakkhayāya paṭipanno jarāmaraṇanirodhāya.
sn12.51:5.1 Athāparaṁ parivīmaṁsamāno parivīmaṁsati:
sn12.51:5.2 ‘jāti panāyaṁ kiṁnidānā kiṁsamudayā kiṁjātikā kiṁpabhavā, kismiṁ sati jāti hoti, kismiṁ asati jāti na hotī’ti?
sn12.51:5.3 So parivīmaṁsamāno evaṁ pajānāti:
sn12.51:5.4 ‘jāti bhavanidānā bhavasamudayā bhavajātikā bhavappabhavā;
sn12.51:5.5 bhave sati jāti hoti, bhave asati jāti na hotī’ti.
sn12.51:6.1 So jātiñca pajānāti, jātisamudayañca pajānāti, jātinirodhañca pajānāti, yā ca jātinirodhasāruppagāminī paṭipadā tañca pajānāti, tathā paṭipanno ca hoti anudhammacārī;
sn12.51:6.2 ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sabbaso sammā dukkhakkhayāya paṭipanno jātinirodhāya.
sn12.51:7.1 Athāparaṁ parivīmaṁsamāno parivīmaṁsati:
sn12.51:7.2 ‘bhavo panāyaṁ kiṁnidāno …pe…
sn12.51:7.3 upādānaṁ panidaṁ kiṁnidānaṁ …
sn12.51:7.4 taṇhā panāyaṁ kiṁnidānā …
sn12.51:7.5 vedanā …
sn12.51:7.6 phasso …
sn12.51:7.7 saḷāyatanaṁ panidaṁ kiṁnidānaṁ …
sn12.51:7.8 nāmarūpaṁ panidaṁ …
sn12.51:7.9 viññāṇaṁ panidaṁ …
sn12.51:7.10 saṅkhārā panime kiṁnidānā kiṁsamudayā kiṁjātikā kiṁpabhavā;
sn12.51:7.11 kismiṁ sati saṅkhārā honti, kismiṁ asati saṅkhārā na hontī’ti?
sn12.51:7.12 So parivīmaṁsamāno evaṁ pajānāti:
sn12.51:7.13 ‘saṅkhārā avijjānidānā avijjāsamudayā avijjājātikā avijjāpabhavā;
sn12.51:7.14 avijjāya sati saṅkhārā honti, avijjāya asati saṅkhārā na hontī’ti.
sn12.51:8.1 So saṅkhāre ca pajānāti, saṅkhārasamudayañca pajānāti, saṅkhāranirodhañca pajānāti, yā ca saṅkhāranirodhasāruppagāminī paṭipadā tañca pajānāti, tathā paṭipanno ca hoti anudhammacārī;
sn12.51:8.2 ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sabbaso sammā dukkhakkhayāya paṭipanno saṅkhāranirodhāya.
sn12.51:9.1 Avijjāgato yaṁ, bhikkhave, purisapuggalo puññañce saṅkhāraṁ abhisaṅkharoti, puññūpagaṁ hoti viññāṇaṁ.
sn12.51:9.2 Apuññañce saṅkhāraṁ abhisaṅkharoti, apuññūpagaṁ hoti viññāṇaṁ.
sn12.51:9.3 Āneñjañce saṅkhāraṁ abhisaṅkharoti āneñjūpagaṁ hoti viññāṇaṁ.
sn12.51:9.4 Yato kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno avijjā pahīnā hoti vijjā uppannā, so avijjāvirāgā vijjuppādā neva puññābhisaṅkhāraṁ abhisaṅkharoti na apuññābhisaṅkhāraṁ abhisaṅkharoti na āneñjābhisaṅkhāraṁ abhisaṅkharoti.
sn12.51:9.5 Anabhisaṅkharonto anabhisañcetayanto na kiñci loke upādiyati;
sn12.51:9.6 anupādiyaṁ na paritassati, aparitassaṁ paccattaññeva parinibbāyati.
sn12.51:9.7 ‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānāti.
sn12.51:10.1 So sukhañce vedanaṁ vedayati, sā aniccāti pajānāti, anajjhositāti pajānāti, anabhinanditāti pajānāti.
sn12.51:10.2 Dukkhañce vedanaṁ vedayati, sā aniccāti pajānāti, anajjhositāti pajānāti, anabhinanditāti pajānāti.
sn12.51:10.3 Adukkhamasukhañce vedanaṁ vedayati, sā aniccāti pajānāti, anajjhositāti pajānāti, anabhinanditāti pajānāti.
sn12.51:10.4 So sukhañce vedanaṁ vedayati, visaṁyutto naṁ vedayati.
sn12.51:10.5 Dukkhañce vedanaṁ vedayati, visaṁyutto naṁ vedayati.
sn12.51:10.6 Adukkhamasukhañce vedanaṁ vedayati, visaṁyutto naṁ vedayati.
sn12.51:11.1 So kāyapariyantikaṁ vedanaṁ vedayamāno kāyapariyantikaṁ vedanaṁ vedayāmīti pajānāti, jīvitapariyantikaṁ vedanaṁ vedayamāno jīvitapariyantikaṁ vedanaṁ vedayāmīti pajānāti.
sn12.51:11.2 Kāyassa bhedā uddhaṁ jīvitapariyādānā idheva sabbavedayitāni anabhinanditāni sītībhavissanti, sarīrāni avasissantīti pajānāti.
sn12.51:12.1 Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, puriso kumbhakārapākā uṇhaṁ kumbhaṁ uddharitvā same bhūmibhāge paṭisisseyya.
sn12.51:12.2 Tatra yāyaṁ usmā sā tattheva vūpasameyya, kapallāni avasisseyyuṁ.
sn12.51:12.3 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu kāyapariyantikaṁ vedanaṁ vedayamāno kāyapariyantikaṁ vedanaṁ vedayāmīti pajānāti, jīvitapariyantikaṁ vedanaṁ vedayamāno jīvitapariyantikaṁ vedanaṁ vedayāmīti pajānāti.
sn12.51:12.4 Kāyassa bhedā uddhaṁ jīvitapariyādānā idheva sabbavedayitāni anabhinanditāni sītībhavissanti, sarīrāni avasissantīti pajānāti.
sn12.51:13.1 Taṁ kiṁ maññatha, bhikkhave,
sn12.51:13.2 api nu kho khīṇāsavo bhikkhu puññābhisaṅkhāraṁ vā abhisaṅkhareyya apuññābhisaṅkhāraṁ vā abhisaṅkhareyya āneñjābhisaṅkhāraṁ vā abhisaṅkhareyyā”ti?
sn12.51:13.3 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.51:14.1 “Sabbaso vā pana saṅkhāresu asati, saṅkhāranirodhā api nu kho viññāṇaṁ paññāyethā”ti?
sn12.51:14.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.51:15.1 “Sabbaso vā pana viññāṇe asati, viññāṇanirodhā api nu kho nāmarūpaṁ paññāyethā”ti?
sn12.51:15.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.51:16.1 “Sabbaso vā pana nāmarūpe asati, nāmarūpanirodhā api nu kho saḷāyatanaṁ paññāyethā”ti?
sn12.51:16.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.51:17.1 “Sabbaso vā pana saḷāyatane asati, saḷāyatananirodhā api nu kho phasso paññāyethā”ti?
sn12.51:17.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.51:18.1 “Sabbaso vā pana phasse asati, phassanirodhā api nu kho vedanā paññāyethā”ti?
sn12.51:18.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.51:19.1 “Sabbaso vā pana vedanāya asati, vedanānirodhā api nu kho taṇhā paññāyethā”ti?
sn12.51:19.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.51:20.1 “Sabbaso vā pana taṇhāya asati, taṇhānirodhā api nu kho upādānaṁ paññāyethā”ti?
sn12.51:20.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.51:21.1 “Sabbaso vā pana upādāne asati, upādānanirodhā api nu kho bhavo paññāyethā”ti.
sn12.51:21.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.51:22.1 “Sabbaso vā pana bhave asati, bhavanirodhā api nu kho jāti paññāyethā”ti?
sn12.51:22.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.

sn12.51:23.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.

sn12.60:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā kurūsu viharati kammāsadhammaṁ nāma kurūnaṁ nigamo.
sn12.60:1.2 Atha kho āyasmā ānando yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā ānando bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.60:1.3 “acchariyaṁ, bhante, abbhutaṁ, bhante.
sn12.60:1.4 Yāva gambhīro cāyaṁ, bhante, paṭiccasamuppādo gambhīrāvabhāso ca, atha ca pana me uttānakuttānako viya khāyatī”ti.
sn12.60:2.1 “Mā hevaṁ, ānanda, mā hevaṁ, ānanda.
sn12.60:2.2 Gambhīro cāyaṁ, ānanda, paṭiccasamuppādo gambhīrāvabhāso ca.
sn12.60:2.3 Etassa, ānanda, dhammassa ananubodhā appaṭivedhā evamayaṁ pajā tantākulakajātā kulagaṇṭhikajātā muñjapabbajabhūtā apāyaṁ duggatiṁ vinipātaṁ saṁsāraṁ nātivattati.
sn12.60:3.1 Upādāniyesu, ānanda, dhammesu assādānupassino viharato taṇhā pavaḍḍhati.
sn12.60:3.2 Taṇhāpaccayā upādānaṁ;
sn12.60:3.3 upādānapaccayā bhavo;
sn12.60:3.4 bhavapaccayā jāti;
sn12.60:3.5 jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇaṁ sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsā sambhavanti.
sn12.60:3.6 Evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.60:4.1 Seyyathāpi, ānanda, mahārukkho.
sn12.60:4.2 Tassa yāni ceva mūlāni adhogamāni, yāni ca tiriyaṅgamāni, sabbāni tāni uddhaṁ ojaṁ abhiharanti.
sn12.60:4.3 Evañhi so, ānanda, mahārukkho tadāhāro tadupādāno ciraṁ dīghamaddhānaṁ tiṭṭheyya.
sn12.60:4.4 Evameva kho, ānanda, upādāniyesu dhammesu assādānupassino viharato taṇhā pavaḍḍhati.
sn12.60:4.5 Taṇhāpaccayā upādānaṁ;
sn12.60:4.6 upādānapaccayā bhavo …pe…
sn12.60:4.7 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.60:5.1 Upādāniyesu, ānanda, dhammesu ādīnavānupassino viharato taṇhā nirujjhati.
sn12.60:5.2 Taṇhānirodhā upādānanirodho;
sn12.60:5.3 upādānanirodhā bhavanirodho …pe…
sn12.60:5.4 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hoti.
sn12.60:6.1 Seyyathāpi, ānanda, mahārukkho.
sn12.60:6.2 Atha puriso āgaccheyya kuddālapiṭakaṁ ādāya.
sn12.60:6.3 So taṁ rukkhaṁ mūle chindeyya, mūle chetvā palikhaṇeyya, palikhaṇitvā mūlāni uddhareyya antamaso usīranāḷimattānipi.
sn12.60:6.4 So taṁ rukkhaṁ khaṇḍākhaṇḍikaṁ chindeyya.
sn12.60:6.5 Khaṇḍākhaṇḍikaṁ chinditvā phāleyya;
sn12.60:6.6 phāletvā sakalikaṁ sakalikaṁ kareyya, sakalikaṁ sakalikaṁ karitvā vātātape visoseyya, vātātape visosetvā agginā ḍaheyya, agginā ḍahetvā masiṁ kareyya, masiṁ karitvā mahāvāte vā ophuṇeyya, nadiyā vā sīghasotāya pavāheyya.
sn12.60:6.7 Evañhi so, ānanda, mahārukkho ucchinnamūlo assa tālāvatthukato anabhāvaṅkato āyatiṁ anuppādadhammo.
sn12.60:6.8 Evameva kho, ānanda, upādāniyesu dhammesu ādīnavānupassino viharato taṇhā nirujjhati.
sn12.60:6.9 Taṇhānirodhā upādānanirodho;
sn12.60:6.10 upādānanirodhā bhavanirodho;
sn12.60:6.11 bhavanirodhā jātinirodho;
sn12.60:6.12 jātinirodhā jarāmaraṇaṁ sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupāyāsā nirujjhanti.
sn12.60:6.13 Evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hotī”ti.
sn12.60:6.14 Dasamaṁ.
sn12.60:6.15 Dukkhavaggo chaṭṭho.
sn12.60:7.0 Tassuddānaṁ
sn12.60:7.1 Parivīmaṁsanupādānaṁ,
sn12.60:7.2 dve ca saṁyojanāni ca;
sn12.60:7.3 Mahārukkhena dve vuttā,
sn12.60:7.4 taruṇena ca sattamaṁ;
sn12.60:7.5 Nāmarūpañca viññāṇaṁ,
sn12.60:7.6 nidānena ca te dasāti. "
sn12.61:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.61
sn12.61:0.2 7. Mahāvagga
sn12.61:0.3 Assutavāsutta
sn12.61:1.1 Evaṁ me sutaṁ—
sn12.61:1.2 ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme …
sn12.61:1.3 “assutavā, bhikkhave, puthujjano imasmiṁ cātumahābhūtikasmiṁ kāyasmiṁ nibbindeyyapi virajjeyyapi vimucceyyapi.
sn12.61:1.4 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn12.61:1.5 Dissati, bhikkhave, imassa cātumahābhūtikassa kāyassa ācayopi apacayopi ādānampi nikkhepanampi.
sn12.61:1.6 Tasmā tatrāssutavā puthujjano nibbindeyyapi virajjeyyapi vimucceyyapi.
sn12.61:2.1 Yañca kho etaṁ, bhikkhave, vuccati cittaṁ itipi, mano itipi, viññāṇaṁ itipi, tatrāssutavā puthujjano nālaṁ nibbindituṁ nālaṁ virajjituṁ nālaṁ vimuccituṁ.
sn12.61:2.2 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn12.61:2.3 Dīgharattañhetaṁ, bhikkhave, assutavato puthujjanassa ajjhositaṁ mamāyitaṁ parāmaṭṭhaṁ:
sn12.61:2.4 ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’ti.
sn12.61:2.5 Tasmā tatrāssutavā puthujjano nālaṁ nibbindituṁ nālaṁ virajjituṁ nālaṁ vimuccituṁ.
sn12.61:3.1 Varaṁ, bhikkhave, assutavā puthujjano imaṁ cātumahābhūtikaṁ kāyaṁ attato upagaccheyya, na tveva cittaṁ.
sn12.61:3.2 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn12.61:3.3 Dissatāyaṁ, bhikkhave, cātumahābhūtiko kāyo ekampi vassaṁ tiṭṭhamāno dvepi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno tīṇipi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno cattāripi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno pañcapi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno dasapi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno vīsatipi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno tiṁsampi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno cattārīsampi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno paññāsampi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno vassasatampi tiṭṭhamāno, bhiyyopi tiṭṭhamāno.
sn12.61:4.1 Yañca kho etaṁ, bhikkhave, vuccati cittaṁ itipi, mano itipi, viññāṇaṁ itipi, taṁ rattiyā ca divasassa ca aññadeva uppajjati aññaṁ nirujjhati.
sn12.61:4.2 Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, makkaṭo araññe pavane caramāno sākhaṁ gaṇhati, taṁ muñcitvā aññaṁ gaṇhati, taṁ muñcitvā aññaṁ gaṇhati;
sn12.61:4.3 evameva kho, bhikkhave, yamidaṁ vuccati cittaṁ itipi, mano itipi, viññāṇaṁ itipi, taṁ rattiyā ca divasassa ca aññadeva uppajjati aññaṁ nirujjhati.
sn12.61:5.1 Tatra, bhikkhave, sutavā ariyasāvako paṭiccasamuppādaṁyeva sādhukaṁ yoniso manasi karoti:
sn12.61:5.2 ‘iti imasmiṁ sati idaṁ hoti, imassuppādā idaṁ uppajjati;
sn12.61:5.3 imasmiṁ asati idaṁ na hoti, imassa nirodhā idaṁ nirujjhati—
sn12.61:5.4 yadidaṁ avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā;
sn12.61:5.5 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ …pe…
sn12.61:5.6 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.61:5.7 Avijjāya tveva asesavirāganirodhā saṅkhāranirodho;
sn12.61:5.8 saṅkhāranirodhā viññāṇanirodho …pe…
sn12.61:5.9 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hotī’ti.
sn12.61:6.1 Evaṁ passaṁ, bhikkhave, sutavā ariyasāvako rūpasmimpi nibbindati, vedanāyapi nibbindati, saññāyapi nibbindati, saṅkhāresupi nibbindati, viññāṇasmimpi nibbindati;
sn12.61:6.2 nibbindaṁ virajjati, virāgā vimuccati, vimuttasmiṁ vimuttamiti ñāṇaṁ hoti.
sn12.61:6.3 ‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānātī”ti.
sn12.61:6.4 Paṭhamaṁ. "

sn12.62:1.4 Dissati, bhikkhave, imassa cātumahābhūtikassa kāyassa ācayopi apacayopi ādānampi nikkhepanampi.
sn12.62:1.5 Tasmā tatrāssutavā puthujjano nibbindeyyapi virajjeyyapi vimucceyyapi.
sn12.62:1.6 Yañca kho etaṁ, bhikkhave, vuccati cittaṁ itipi, mano itipi, viññāṇaṁ itipi, tatrāssutavā puthujjano nālaṁ nibbindituṁ nālaṁ virajjituṁ nālaṁ vimuccituṁ.
sn12.62:1.7 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn12.62:1.8 Dīgharattañhetaṁ, bhikkhave, assutavato puthujjanassa ajjhositaṁ mamāyitaṁ parāmaṭṭhaṁ:
sn12.62:1.9 ‘etaṁ mama, esohamasmi, eso me attā’ti.
sn12.62:1.10 Tasmā tatrāssutavā puthujjano nālaṁ nibbindituṁ nālaṁ virajjituṁ nālaṁ vimuccituṁ.
sn12.62:2.1 Varaṁ, bhikkhave, assutavā puthujjano imaṁ cātumahābhūtikaṁ kāyaṁ attato upagaccheyya, na tveva cittaṁ.
sn12.62:2.2 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn12.62:2.3 Dissatāyaṁ, bhikkhave, cātumahābhūtiko kāyo ekampi vassaṁ tiṭṭhamāno dvepi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno tīṇipi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno cattāripi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno pañcapi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno dasapi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno vīsatipi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno tiṁsampi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno cattārīsampi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno paññāsampi vassāni tiṭṭhamāno vassasatampi tiṭṭhamāno, bhiyyopi tiṭṭhamāno.
sn12.62:2.4 Yañca kho etaṁ, bhikkhave, vuccati cittaṁ itipi, mano itipi, viññāṇaṁ itipi, taṁ rattiyā ca divasassa ca aññadeva uppajjati aññaṁ nirujjhati.
sn12.62:3.1 Tatra, bhikkhave, sutavā ariyasāvako paṭiccasamuppādaṁyeva sādhukaṁ yoniso manasi karoti:
sn12.62:3.2 ‘iti imasmiṁ sati idaṁ hoti, imassuppādā idaṁ uppajjati;
sn12.62:3.3 imasmiṁ asati idaṁ na hoti, imassa nirodhā idaṁ nirujjhatī’ti.
sn12.62:3.4 Sukhavedaniyaṁ, bhikkhave, phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati sukhavedanā.
sn12.62:3.5 Tasseva sukhavedaniyassa phassassa nirodhā yaṁ tajjaṁ vedayitaṁ sukhavedaniyaṁ phassaṁ paṭicca uppannā sukhavedanā sā nirujjhati sā vūpasammati.
sn12.62:3.6 Dukkhavedaniyaṁ, bhikkhave, phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati dukkhavedanā.
sn12.62:3.7 Tasseva dukkhavedaniyassa phassassa nirodhā yaṁ tajjaṁ vedayitaṁ dukkhavedaniyaṁ phassaṁ paṭicca uppannā dukkhavedanā sā nirujjhati sā vūpasammati.
sn12.62:3.8 Adukkhamasukhavedaniyaṁ, bhikkhave, phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati adukkhamasukhavedanā.
sn12.62:3.9 Tasseva adukkhamasukhavedaniyassa phassassa nirodhā yaṁ tajjaṁ vedayitaṁ adukkhamasukhavedaniyaṁ phassaṁ paṭicca uppannā adukkhamasukhavedanā sā nirujjhati sā vūpasammati.
sn12.62:4.1 Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, dvinnaṁ kaṭṭhānaṁ saṅghaṭṭanasamodhānā usmā jāyati tejo abhinibbattati. Tesaṁyeva dvinnaṁ kaṭṭhānaṁ nānākatavinibbhogā yā tajjā usmā sā nirujjhati sā vūpasammati;
sn12.62:4.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave, sukhavedaniyaṁ phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati sukhavedanā.
sn12.62:4.3 Tasseva sukhavedaniyassa phassassa nirodhā yaṁ tajjaṁ vedayitaṁ sukhavedaniyaṁ phassaṁ paṭicca uppannā sukhavedanā sā nirujjhati sā vūpasammati …pe…
sn12.62:4.4 dukkhavedaniyaṁ phassaṁ paṭicca …
sn12.62:4.5 adukkhamasukhavedaniyaṁ phassaṁ paṭicca uppajjati adukkhamasukhavedanā.
sn12.62:4.6 Tasseva adukkhamasukhavedaniyassa phassassa nirodhā yaṁ tajjaṁ vedayitaṁ adukkhamasukhavedaniyaṁ phassaṁ paṭicca uppannā adukkhamasukhavedanā sā nirujjhati sā vūpasammati.
sn12.62:5.1 Evaṁ passaṁ, bhikkhave, sutavā ariyasāvako phassepi nibbindati, vedanāyapi nibbindati, saññāyapi nibbindati, saṅkhāresupi nibbindati, viññāṇasmimpi nibbindati;
sn12.62:5.2 nibbindaṁ virajjati, virāgā vimuccati, vimuttasmiṁ vimuttamiti ñāṇaṁ hoti.
sn12.62:5.3 ‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānātī”ti.
sn12.62:5.4 Dutiyaṁ. "
sn12.63:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.63
sn12.63:0.2 7. Mahāvagga
sn12.63:0.3 Puttamaṁsasutta
sn12.63:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ …
sn12.63:1.2 “cattārome, bhikkhave, āhārā bhūtānaṁ vā sattānaṁ ṭhitiyā sambhavesīnaṁ vā anuggahāya.
sn12.63:1.3 Katame cattāro?
sn12.63:1.4 Kabaḷīkāro āhāro oḷāriko vā sukhumo vā, phasso dutiyo, manosañcetanā tatiyā, viññāṇaṁ catutthaṁ.
sn12.63:1.5 Ime kho, bhikkhave, cattāro āhārā bhūtānaṁ vā sattānaṁ ṭhitiyā sambhavesīnaṁ vā anuggahāya.
sn12.63:2.1 Kathañca, bhikkhave, kabaḷīkāro āhāro daṭṭhabbo?
sn12.63:2.2 Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, dve jāyampatikā parittaṁ sambalaṁ ādāya kantāramaggaṁ paṭipajjeyyuṁ.
sn12.63:2.3 Tesamassa ekaputtako piyo manāpo.
sn12.63:2.4 Atha kho tesaṁ, bhikkhave, dvinnaṁ jāyampatikānaṁ kantāragatānaṁ yā parittā sambalamattā, sā parikkhayaṁ pariyādānaṁ gaccheyya.
sn12.63:2.5 Siyā ca nesaṁ kantārāvaseso anatiṇṇo.
sn12.63:2.6 Atha kho tesaṁ, bhikkhave, dvinnaṁ jāyampatikānaṁ evamassa:
sn12.63:2.7 ‘amhākaṁ kho yā parittā sambalamattā sā parikkhīṇā pariyādiṇṇā.
sn12.63:2.8 Atthi cāyaṁ kantārāvaseso anittiṇṇo.
sn12.63:2.9 Yannūna mayaṁ imaṁ ekaputtakaṁ piyaṁ manāpaṁ vadhitvā vallūrañca soṇḍikañca karitvā puttamaṁsāni khādantā evaṁ taṁ kantārāvasesaṁ nitthareyyāma, mā sabbeva tayo vinassimhā’ti.
sn12.63:2.10 Atha kho te, bhikkhave, dve jāyampatikā taṁ ekaputtakaṁ piyaṁ manāpaṁ vadhitvā vallūrañca soṇḍikañca karitvā puttamaṁsāni khādantā evaṁ taṁ kantārāvasesaṁ nitthareyyuṁ.
sn12.63:2.11 Te puttamaṁsāni ceva khādeyyuṁ, ure ca paṭipiseyyuṁ:
sn12.63:2.12 ‘kahaṁ, ekaputtaka, kahaṁ, ekaputtakā’ti.
sn12.63:3.1 Taṁ kiṁ maññatha, bhikkhave,
sn12.63:3.2 api nu te davāya vā āhāraṁ āhāreyyuṁ, madāya vā āhāraṁ āhāreyyuṁ, maṇḍanāya vā āhāraṁ āhāreyyuṁ, vibhūsanāya vā āhāraṁ āhāreyyun”ti?
sn12.63:3.3 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.63:3.4 “Nanu te, bhikkhave, yāvadeva kantārassa nittharaṇatthāya āhāraṁ āhāreyyun”ti?
sn12.63:3.5 “Evaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.63:3.6 “‘Evameva khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, kabaḷīkāro āhāro daṭṭhabbo’ti vadāmi.
sn12.63:3.7 Kabaḷīkāre, bhikkhave, āhāre pariññāte pañca kāmaguṇiko rāgo pariññāto hoti.
sn12.63:3.8 Pañca kāmaguṇike rāge pariññāte natthi taṁ saṁyojanaṁ yena saṁyojanena saṁyutto ariyasāvako puna imaṁ lokaṁ āgaccheyya.
sn12.63:4.1 Kathañca, bhikkhave, phassāhāro daṭṭhabbo?
sn12.63:4.2 Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, gāvī niccammā kuṭṭañce nissāya tiṭṭheyya. Ye kuṭṭanissitā pāṇā te naṁ khādeyyuṁ.
sn12.63:4.3 Rukkhañce nissāya tiṭṭheyya, ye rukkhanissitā pāṇā te naṁ khādeyyuṁ.
sn12.63:4.4 Udakañce nissāya tiṭṭheyya, ye udakanissitā pāṇā te naṁ khādeyyuṁ.
sn12.63:4.5 Ākāsañce nissāya tiṭṭheyya, ye ākāsanissitā pāṇā te naṁ khādeyyuṁ.
sn12.63:4.6 Yaṁ yadeva hi sā, bhikkhave, gāvī niccammā nissāya tiṭṭheyya, ye tannissitā pāṇā te naṁ khādeyyuṁ.
sn12.63:4.7 Evameva khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, ‘phassāhāro daṭṭhabbo’ti vadāmi.
sn12.63:4.8 Phasse, bhikkhave, āhāre pariññāte tisso vedanā pariññātā honti.
sn12.63:4.9 Tīsu vedanāsu pariññātāsu ariyasāvakassa natthi kiñci uttarikaraṇīyanti vadāmi.
sn12.63:5.1 Kathañca, bhikkhave, manosañcetanāhāro daṭṭhabbo?
sn12.63:5.2 Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, aṅgārakāsu sādhikaporisā puṇṇā aṅgārānaṁ vītaccikānaṁ vītadhūmānaṁ.
sn12.63:5.3 Atha puriso āgaccheyya jīvitukāmo amaritukāmo sukhakāmo dukkhappaṭikūlo.
sn12.63:5.4 Tamenaṁ dve balavanto purisā nānābāhāsu gahetvā taṁ aṅgārakāsuṁ upakaḍḍheyyuṁ.
sn12.63:5.5 Atha kho, bhikkhave, tassa purisassa ārakāvassa cetanā ārakā patthanā ārakā paṇidhi.
sn12.63:5.6 Taṁ kissa hetu?
sn12.63:5.7 Evañhi, bhikkhave, tassa purisassa hoti:
sn12.63:5.8 ‘imañcāhaṁ aṅgārakāsuṁ papatissāmi, tatonidānaṁ maraṇaṁ vā nigacchāmi maraṇamattaṁ vā dukkhan’ti.
sn12.63:5.9 Evameva khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, ‘manosañcetanāhāro daṭṭhabbo’ti vadāmi.
sn12.63:5.10 Manosañcetanāya, bhikkhave, āhāre pariññāte tisso taṇhā pariññātā honti.
sn12.63:5.11 Tīsu taṇhāsu pariññātāsu ariyasāvakassa natthi kiñci uttarikaraṇīyanti vadāmi.
sn12.63:6.1 Kathañca, bhikkhave, viññāṇāhāro daṭṭhabbo?
sn12.63:6.2 Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, coraṁ āgucāriṁ gahetvā rañño dasseyyuṁ:
sn12.63:6.3 ‘ayaṁ te, deva, coro āgucārī, imassa yaṁ icchasi taṁ daṇḍaṁ paṇehī’ti.
sn12.63:6.4 Tamenaṁ rājā evaṁ vadeyya:
sn12.63:6.5 ‘gacchatha, bho, imaṁ purisaṁ pubbaṇhasamayaṁ sattisatena hanathā’ti.
sn12.63:6.6 Tamenaṁ pubbaṇhasamayaṁ sattisatena haneyyuṁ.
sn12.63:6.7 Atha rājā majjhanhikasamayaṁ evaṁ vadeyya:
sn12.63:6.8 ‘ambho, kathaṁ so puriso’ti?
sn12.63:6.9 ‘Tatheva, deva, jīvatī’ti.
sn12.63:6.10 Tamenaṁ rājā evaṁ vadeyya:
sn12.63:6.11 ‘gacchatha, bho, taṁ purisaṁ majjhanhikasamayaṁ sattisatena hanathā’ti.
sn12.63:6.12 Tamenaṁ majjhanhikasamayaṁ sattisatena haneyyuṁ.
sn12.63:6.13 Atha rājā sāyanhasamayaṁ evaṁ vadeyya:
sn12.63:6.14 ‘ambho, kathaṁ so puriso’ti?
sn12.63:6.15 ‘Tatheva, deva, jīvatī’ti.
sn12.63:6.16 Tamenaṁ rājā evaṁ vadeyya:
sn12.63:6.17 ‘gacchatha, bho, taṁ purisaṁ sāyanhasamayaṁ sattisatena hanathā’ti.
sn12.63:6.18 Tamenaṁ sāyanhasamayaṁ sattisatena haneyyuṁ.
sn12.63:6.19 Taṁ kiṁ maññatha, bhikkhave,
sn12.63:6.20 api nu so puriso divasaṁ tīhi sattisatehi haññamāno tatonidānaṁ dukkhaṁ domanassaṁ paṭisaṁvediyethā”ti?
sn12.63:6.21 “Ekissāpi, bhante, sattiyā haññamāno tatonidānaṁ dukkhaṁ domanassaṁ paṭisaṁvediyetha;
sn12.63:6.22 ko pana vādo tīhi sattisatehi haññamāno”ti.
sn12.63:6.23 “Evameva khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, viññāṇāhāro daṭṭhabboti vadāmi.
sn12.63:6.24 Viññāṇe, bhikkhave, āhāre pariññāte nāmarūpaṁ pariññātaṁ hoti, nāmarūpe pariññāte ariyasāvakassa natthi kiñci uttarikaraṇīyanti vadāmī”ti.
sn12.63:6.25 Tatiyaṁ. "

sn12.65:0.3 Nagarasutta
sn12.65:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.65:1.2 “Pubbe me, bhikkhave, sambodhā anabhisambuddhassa bodhisattasseva sato etadahosi:
sn12.65:1.3 ‘kicchā vatāyaṁ loko āpanno jāyati ca jīyati ca mīyati ca cavati ca upapajjati ca.
sn12.65:1.4 Atha ca panimassa dukkhassa nissaraṇaṁ nappajānāti jarāmaraṇassa.
sn12.65:1.5 Kudāssu nāma imassa dukkhassa nissaraṇaṁ paññāyissati jarāmaraṇassā’ti?
sn12.65:1.6 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, etadahosi:
sn12.65:1.7 ‘kimhi nu kho sati jarāmaraṇaṁ hoti, kiṁpaccayā jarāmaraṇan’ti?
sn12.65:1.8 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.65:1.9 ‘jātiyā kho sati jarāmaraṇaṁ hoti, jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇan’ti.
sn12.65:2.1 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, etadahosi:
sn12.65:2.2 ‘kimhi nu kho sati jāti hoti …pe…
sn12.65:2.3 bhavo hoti …
sn12.65:2.4 upādānaṁ hoti …
sn12.65:2.5 taṇhā hoti …
sn12.65:2.6 vedanā hoti …
sn12.65:2.7 phasso hoti …
sn12.65:2.8 saḷāyatanaṁ hoti …
sn12.65:2.9 nāmarūpaṁ hoti …
sn12.65:2.10 kiṁpaccayā nāmarūpan’ti?
sn12.65:2.11 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.65:2.12 ‘viññāṇe kho sati nāmarūpaṁ hoti, viññāṇapaccayā nāmarūpan’ti.
sn12.65:2.13 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, etadahosi:
sn12.65:2.14 ‘kimhi nu kho sati viññāṇaṁ hoti, kiṁpaccayā viññāṇan’ti?
sn12.65:2.15 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.65:2.16 ‘nāmarūpe kho sati viññāṇaṁ hoti, nāmarūpapaccayā viññāṇan’ti.
sn12.65:3.1 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, etadahosi—
sn12.65:3.2 paccudāvattati kho idaṁ viññāṇaṁ nāmarūpamhā na paraṁ gacchati.
sn12.65:3.3 Ettāvatā jāyetha vā jīyetha vā mīyetha vā cavetha vā upapajjetha vā, yadidaṁ nāmarūpapaccayā viññāṇaṁ;
sn12.65:3.4 viññāṇapaccayā nāmarūpaṁ;
sn12.65:3.5 nāmarūpapaccayā saḷāyatanaṁ;
sn12.65:3.6 saḷāyatanapaccayā phasso …pe…
sn12.65:3.7 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.65:3.8 ‘Samudayo, samudayo’ti kho me, bhikkhave, pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhuṁ udapādi ñāṇaṁ udapādi paññā udapādi vijjā udapādi āloko udapādi.
sn12.65:4.1 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, etadahosi:
sn12.65:4.2 ‘kimhi nu kho asati, jarāmaraṇaṁ na hoti;
sn12.65:4.3 kissa nirodhā jarāmaraṇanirodho’ti?
sn12.65:4.4 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.65:4.5 ‘jātiyā kho asati, jarāmaraṇaṁ na hoti;
sn12.65:4.6 jātinirodhā jarāmaraṇanirodho’ti.
sn12.65:4.7 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, etadahosi:
sn12.65:4.8 ‘kimhi nu kho asati jāti na hoti …pe…
sn12.65:4.9 bhavo na hoti …
sn12.65:4.10 upādānaṁ na hoti …
sn12.65:4.11 taṇhā na hoti …
sn12.65:4.12 vedanā na hoti …
sn12.65:4.13 phasso na hoti …
sn12.65:4.14 saḷāyatanaṁ na hoti …
sn12.65:4.15 nāmarūpaṁ na hoti.
sn12.65:4.16 Kissa nirodhā nāmarūpanirodho’ti?
sn12.65:4.17 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.65:4.18 ‘viññāṇe kho asati, nāmarūpaṁ na hoti;
sn12.65:4.19 viññāṇanirodhā nāmarūpanirodho’ti.
sn12.65:5.1 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, etadahosi:
sn12.65:5.2 ‘kimhi nu kho asati viññāṇaṁ na hoti;
sn12.65:5.3 kissa nirodhā viññāṇanirodho’ti?
sn12.65:5.4 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, yoniso manasikārā ahu paññāya abhisamayo:
sn12.65:5.5 ‘nāmarūpe kho asati, viññāṇaṁ na hoti;
sn12.65:5.6 nāmarūpanirodhā viññāṇanirodho’ti.
sn12.65:6.1 Tassa mayhaṁ, bhikkhave, etadahosi—
sn12.65:6.2 adhigato kho myāyaṁ maggo bodhāya yadidaṁ—
sn12.65:6.3 nāmarūpanirodhā viññāṇanirodho;
sn12.65:6.4 viññāṇanirodhā nāmarūpanirodho;
sn12.65:6.5 nāmarūpanirodhā saḷāyatananirodho;
sn12.65:6.6 saḷāyatananirodhā phassanirodho …pe…
sn12.65:6.7 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hoti.
sn12.65:6.8 ‘Nirodho, nirodho’ti kho me, bhikkhave, pubbe ananussutesu dhammesu cakkhuṁ udapādi ñāṇaṁ udapādi paññā udapādi vijjā udapādi āloko udapādi.
sn12.65:7.1 Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, puriso araññe pavane caramāno passeyya purāṇaṁ maggaṁ purāṇañjasaṁ pubbakehi manussehi anuyātaṁ.
sn12.65:7.2 So tamanugaccheyya.
sn12.65:7.3 Tamanugacchanto passeyya purāṇaṁ nagaraṁ purāṇaṁ rājadhāniṁ pubbakehi manussehi ajjhāvuṭṭhaṁ ārāmasampannaṁ vanasampannaṁ pokkharaṇīsampannaṁ uddhāpavantaṁ ramaṇīyaṁ.
sn12.65:7.4 Atha kho so, bhikkhave, puriso rañño vā rājamahāmattassa vā āroceyya:
sn12.65:7.5 ‘yagghe, bhante, jāneyyāsi—ahaṁ addasaṁ araññe pavane caramāno purāṇaṁ maggaṁ purāṇañjasaṁ pubbakehi manussehi anuyātaṁ tamanugacchiṁ.
sn12.65:7.6 Tamanugacchanto addasaṁ purāṇaṁ nagaraṁ purāṇaṁ rājadhāniṁ pubbakehi manussehi ajjhāvuṭṭhaṁ ārāmasampannaṁ vanasampannaṁ pokkharaṇīsampannaṁ uddhāpavantaṁ ramaṇīyaṁ.
sn12.65:7.7 Taṁ, bhante, nagaraṁ māpehī’ti.
sn12.65:7.8 Atha kho so, bhikkhave, rājā vā rājamahāmatto vā taṁ nagaraṁ māpeyya.
sn12.65:7.9 Tadassa nagaraṁ aparena samayena iddhañceva phītañca bāhujaññaṁ ākiṇṇamanussaṁ vuddhivepullappattaṁ.
sn12.65:7.10 Evameva khvāhaṁ, bhikkhave, addasaṁ purāṇaṁ maggaṁ purāṇañjasaṁ pubbakehi sammāsambuddhehi anuyātaṁ.
sn12.65:8.1 Katamo ca so, bhikkhave, purāṇamaggo purāṇañjaso pubbakehi sammāsambuddhehi anuyāto?
sn12.65:8.2 Ayameva ariyo aṭṭhaṅgiko maggo, seyyathidaṁ—
sn12.65:8.3 sammādiṭṭhi …pe… sammāsamādhi.
sn12.65:8.4 Ayaṁ kho so, bhikkhave, purāṇamaggo purāṇañjaso pubbakehi sammāsambuddhehi anuyāto, tamanugacchiṁ;
sn12.65:8.5 tamanugacchanto jarāmaraṇaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ;
sn12.65:8.6 jarāmaraṇasamudayaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ;
sn12.65:8.7 jarāmaraṇanirodhaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ;
sn12.65:8.8 jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ.
sn12.65:8.9 Tamanugacchiṁ;
sn12.65:8.10 tamanugacchanto jātiṁ abbhaññāsiṁ …pe…
sn12.65:8.11 bhavaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ …
sn12.65:8.12 upādānaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ …
sn12.65:8.13 taṇhaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ …
sn12.65:8.14 vedanaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ …
sn12.65:8.15 phassaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ …
sn12.65:8.16 saḷāyatanaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ …
sn12.65:8.17 nāmarūpaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ …
sn12.65:8.18 viññāṇaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ.
sn12.65:8.19 Tamanugacchiṁ;
sn12.65:8.20 tamanugacchanto saṅkhāre abbhaññāsiṁ;
sn12.65:8.21 saṅkhārasamudayaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ;
sn12.65:8.22 saṅkhāranirodhaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ;
sn12.65:8.23 saṅkhāranirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ abbhaññāsiṁ.
sn12.65:8.24 Tadabhiññāya ācikkhiṁ bhikkhūnaṁ bhikkhunīnaṁ upāsakānaṁ upāsikānaṁ.
sn12.65:8.25 Tayidaṁ, bhikkhave, brahmacariyaṁ iddhañceva phītañca vitthārikaṁ bāhujaññaṁ puthubhūtaṁ yāva devamanussehi suppakāsitan”ti.
sn12.65:8.26 Pañcamaṁ. "
sn12.66:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.66
sn12.66:0.2 7. Mahāvagga
sn12.66:0.3 Sammasasutta
sn12.66:1.1 Evaṁ me sutaṁ—
sn12.66:1.2 ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā kurūsu viharati kammāsadhammaṁ nāma kurūnaṁ nigamo.
sn12.66:1.3 Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi:
sn12.66:1.4 “bhikkhavo”ti.
sn12.66:1.5 “Bhadante”ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.
sn12.66:1.6 Bhagavā etadavoca:
sn12.66:1.7 “sammasatha no tumhe, bhikkhave, antaraṁ sammasan”ti.
sn12.66:1.8 Evaṁ vutte, aññataro bhikkhu bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.66:1.9 “ahaṁ kho, bhante, sammasāmi antaraṁ sammasan”ti.
sn12.66:1.10 “Yathā kathaṁ pana tvaṁ, bhikkhu, sammasasi antaraṁ sammasan”ti?
sn12.66:1.11 Atha kho so bhikkhu byākāsi.
sn12.66:1.12 Yathā so bhikkhu byākāsi na so bhikkhu bhagavato cittaṁ ārādhesi.
sn12.66:2.1 Evaṁ vutte, āyasmā ānando bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.66:2.2 “etassa, bhagavā, kālo; etassa, sugata, kālo;
sn12.66:2.3 yaṁ bhagavā antaraṁ sammasaṁ bhāseyya. Bhagavato sutvā bhikkhū dhāressantī”ti.
sn12.66:2.4 “Tenahānanda, suṇātha, sādhukaṁ manasi karotha, bhāsissāmī”ti.
sn12.66:2.5 “Evaṁ, bhante”ti kho te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṁ.
sn12.66:2.6 Bhagavā etadavoca:
sn12.66:3.1 “Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sammasamāno sammasati antaraṁ sammasaṁ:
sn12.66:3.2 ‘yaṁ kho idaṁ anekavidhaṁ nānappakārakaṁ dukkhaṁ loke uppajjati jarāmaraṇaṁ.
sn12.66:3.3 Idaṁ kho dukkhaṁ kiṁnidānaṁ kiṁsamudayaṁ kiṁjātikaṁ kiṁpabhavaṁ, kismiṁ sati jarāmaraṇaṁ hoti, kismiṁ asati jarāmaraṇaṁ na hotī’ti?
sn12.66:3.4 So sammasamāno evaṁ jānāti:
sn12.66:3.5 ‘yaṁ kho idaṁ anekavidhaṁ nānappakārakaṁ dukkhaṁ loke uppajjati jarāmaraṇaṁ.
sn12.66:3.6 Idaṁ kho dukkhaṁ upadhinidānaṁ upadhisamudayaṁ upadhijātikaṁ upadhipabhavaṁ, upadhismiṁ sati jarāmaraṇaṁ hoti, upadhismiṁ asati jarāmaraṇaṁ na hotī’ti.
sn12.66:3.7 So jarāmaraṇañca pajānāti jarāmaraṇasamudayañca pajānāti jarāmaraṇanirodhañca pajānāti yā ca jarāmaraṇanirodhasāruppagāminī paṭipadā tañca pajānāti.
sn12.66:3.8 Tathāpaṭipanno ca hoti anudhammacārī.
sn12.66:3.9 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sabbaso sammā dukkhakkhayāya paṭipanno jarāmaraṇanirodhāya.
sn12.66:4.1 Athāparaṁ sammasamāno sammasati antaraṁ sammasaṁ:
sn12.66:4.2 ‘upadhi panāyaṁ kiṁnidāno kiṁsamudayo kiṁjātiko kiṁpabhavo, kismiṁ sati upadhi hoti, kismiṁ asati upadhi na hotī’ti?
sn12.66:4.3 So sammasamāno evaṁ jānāti:
sn12.66:4.4 ‘upadhi taṇhānidāno taṇhāsamudayo taṇhājātiko taṇhāpabhavo, taṇhāya sati upadhi hoti, taṇhāya asati upadhi na hotī’ti.
sn12.66:4.5 So upadhiñca pajānāti upadhisamudayañca pajānāti upadhinirodhañca pajānāti yā ca upadhinirodhasāruppagāminī paṭipadā tañca pajānāti.
sn12.66:4.6 Tathāpaṭipanno ca hoti anudhammacārī.
sn12.66:4.7 Ayaṁ vuccati, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sabbaso sammā dukkhakkhayāya paṭipanno upadhinirodhāya.
sn12.66:5.1 Athāparaṁ sammasamāno sammasati antaraṁ sammasaṁ:
sn12.66:5.2 ‘taṇhā panāyaṁ kattha uppajjamānā uppajjati, kattha nivisamānā nivisatī’ti?
sn12.66:5.3 So sammasamāno evaṁ jānāti—
sn12.66:5.4 yaṁ kho loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ etthesā taṇhā uppajjamānā uppajjati, ettha nivisamānā nivisati.
sn12.66:5.5 Kiñca loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ?
sn12.66:5.6 Cakkhuṁ loke piyarūpaṁ, sātarūpaṁ, etthesā taṇhā uppajjamānā uppajjati, ettha nivisamānā nivisati.
sn12.66:5.7 Sotaṁ loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ …pe…
sn12.66:5.8 ghānaṁ loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ …
sn12.66:5.9 jivhā loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ …
sn12.66:5.10 kāyo loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ …
sn12.66:5.11 mano loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ, etthesā taṇhā uppajjamānā uppajjati ettha nivisamānā nivisati.
sn12.66:6.1 Ye hi keci, bhikkhave, atītamaddhānaṁ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yaṁ loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ taṁ niccato addakkhuṁ sukhato addakkhuṁ attato addakkhuṁ ārogyato addakkhuṁ khemato addakkhuṁ.
sn12.66:6.2 Te taṇhaṁ vaḍḍhesuṁ.
sn12.66:6.3 Ye taṇhaṁ vaḍḍhesuṁ te upadhiṁ vaḍḍhesuṁ.
sn12.66:6.4 Ye upadhiṁ vaḍḍhesuṁ te dukkhaṁ vaḍḍhesuṁ.
sn12.66:6.5 Ye dukkhaṁ vaḍḍhesuṁ te na parimucciṁsu jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi, na parimucciṁsu dukkhasmāti vadāmi.
sn12.66:7.1 Yepi hi keci, bhikkhave, anāgatamaddhānaṁ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yaṁ loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ taṁ niccato dakkhissanti sukhato dakkhissanti attato dakkhissanti ārogyato dakkhissanti khemato dakkhissanti.
sn12.66:7.2 Te taṇhaṁ vaḍḍhissanti.
sn12.66:7.3 Ye taṇhaṁ vaḍḍhissanti te upadhiṁ vaḍḍhissanti.
sn12.66:7.4 Ye upadhiṁ vaḍḍhissanti te dukkhaṁ vaḍḍhissanti.
sn12.66:7.5 Ye dukkhaṁ vaḍḍhissanti te na parimuccissanti jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi, na parimuccissanti dukkhasmāti vadāmi.
sn12.66:8.1 Yepi hi keci, bhikkhave, etarahi samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yaṁ loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ taṁ niccato passanti sukhato passanti attato passanti ārogyato passanti khemato passanti.
sn12.66:8.2 Te taṇhaṁ vaḍḍhenti.
sn12.66:8.3 Ye taṇhaṁ vaḍḍhenti te upadhiṁ vaḍḍhenti.
sn12.66:8.4 Ye upadhiṁ vaḍḍhenti te dukkhaṁ vaḍḍhenti.
sn12.66:8.5 Ye dukkhaṁ vaḍḍhenti te na parimuccanti jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi, na parimuccanti dukkhasmāti vadāmi.
sn12.66:9.1 Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, āpānīyakaṁso vaṇṇasampanno gandhasampanno rasasampanno.
sn12.66:9.2 So ca kho visena saṁsaṭṭho.
sn12.66:9.3 Atha puriso āgaccheyya ghammābhitatto ghammapareto kilanto tasito pipāsito.
sn12.66:9.4 Tamenaṁ evaṁ vadeyyuṁ:
sn12.66:9.5 ‘ayaṁ te, ambho purisa, āpānīyakaṁso vaṇṇasampanno gandhasampanno rasasampanno;
sn12.66:9.6 so ca kho visena saṁsaṭṭho.
sn12.66:9.7 Sace ākaṅkhasi piva.
sn12.66:9.8 Pivato hi kho taṁ chādessati vaṇṇenapi gandhenapi rasenapi, pivitvā ca pana tatonidānaṁ maraṇaṁ vā nigacchasi maraṇamattaṁ vā dukkhan’ti.
sn12.66:9.9 So taṁ āpānīyakaṁsaṁ sahasā appaṭisaṅkhā piveyya, nappaṭinissajjeyya.
sn12.66:9.10 So tatonidānaṁ maraṇaṁ vā nigaccheyya maraṇamattaṁ vā dukkhaṁ.
sn12.66:9.11 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, ye hi keci atītamaddhānaṁ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yaṁ loke piyarūpaṁ …pe…
sn12.66:9.12 anāgatamaddhānaṁ …pe…
sn12.66:9.13 etarahi samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yaṁ loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ taṁ niccato passanti sukhato passanti attato passanti ārogyato passanti khemato passanti, te taṇhaṁ vaḍḍhenti.
sn12.66:9.14 Ye taṇhaṁ vaḍḍhenti te upadhiṁ vaḍḍhenti.
sn12.66:9.15 Ye upadhiṁ vaḍḍhenti te dukkhaṁ vaḍḍhenti.
sn12.66:9.16 Ye dukkhaṁ vaḍḍhenti te na parimuccanti jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi, na parimuccanti dukkhasmāti vadāmi.
sn12.66:10.1 Ye ca kho keci, bhikkhave, atītamaddhānaṁ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yaṁ loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ taṁ aniccato addakkhuṁ dukkhato addakkhuṁ anattato addakkhuṁ rogato addakkhuṁ bhayato addakkhuṁ,
sn12.66:10.2 te taṇhaṁ pajahiṁsu.
sn12.66:10.3 Ye taṇhaṁ pajahiṁsu te upadhiṁ pajahiṁsu.
sn12.66:10.4 Ye upadhiṁ pajahiṁsu te dukkhaṁ pajahiṁsu.
sn12.66:10.5 Ye dukkhaṁ pajahiṁsu te parimucciṁsu jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi, parimucciṁsu dukkhasmāti vadāmi.
sn12.66:11.1 Yepi hi keci, bhikkhave, anāgatamaddhānaṁ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yaṁ loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ taṁ aniccato dakkhissanti dukkhato dakkhissanti anattato dakkhissanti rogato dakkhissanti bhayato dakkhissanti,
sn12.66:11.2 te taṇhaṁ pajahissanti.
sn12.66:11.3 Ye taṇhaṁ pajahissanti …pe…
sn12.66:11.4 parimuccissanti dukkhasmāti vadāmi.
sn12.66:12.1 Yepi hi keci, bhikkhave, etarahi samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yaṁ loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ taṁ aniccato passanti dukkhato passanti anattato passanti rogato passanti bhayato passanti,
sn12.66:12.2 te taṇhaṁ pajahanti.
sn12.66:12.3 Ye taṇhaṁ pajahanti te upadhiṁ pajahanti.
sn12.66:12.4 Ye upadhiṁ pajahanti te dukkhaṁ pajahanti.
sn12.66:12.5 Ye dukkhaṁ pajahanti te parimuccanti jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi, parimuccanti dukkhasmāti vadāmi.
sn12.66:13.1 Seyyathāpi, bhikkhave, āpānīyakaṁso vaṇṇasampanno gandhasampanno rasasampanno.
sn12.66:13.2 So ca kho visena saṁsaṭṭho.
sn12.66:13.3 Atha puriso āgaccheyya ghammābhitatto ghammapareto kilanto tasito pipāsito.
sn12.66:13.4 Tamenaṁ evaṁ vadeyyuṁ:
sn12.66:13.5 ‘ayaṁ te, ambho purisa, āpānīyakaṁso vaṇṇasampanno gandhasampanno rasasampanno
sn12.66:13.6 so ca kho visena saṁsaṭṭho.
sn12.66:13.7 Sace ākaṅkhasi piva.
sn12.66:13.8 Pivato hi kho taṁ chādessati vaṇṇenapi gandhenapi rasenapi; pivitvā ca pana tatonidānaṁ maraṇaṁ vā nigacchasi maraṇamattaṁ vā dukkhan’ti.
sn12.66:13.9 Atha kho, bhikkhave, tassa purisassa evamassa:
sn12.66:13.10 ‘sakkā kho me ayaṁ surāpipāsitā pānīyena vā vinetuṁ dadhimaṇḍakena vā vinetuṁ bhaṭṭhaloṇikāya vā vinetuṁ loṇasovīrakena vā vinetuṁ, na tvevāhaṁ taṁ piveyyaṁ, yaṁ mama assa dīgharattaṁ hitāya sukhāyā’ti.
sn12.66:13.11 So taṁ āpānīyakaṁsaṁ paṭisaṅkhā na piveyya, paṭinissajjeyya.
sn12.66:13.12 So tatonidānaṁ na maraṇaṁ vā nigaccheyya maraṇamattaṁ vā dukkhaṁ.
sn12.66:13.13 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, ye hi keci atītamaddhānaṁ samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yaṁ loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ taṁ aniccato addakkhuṁ dukkhato addakkhuṁ anattato addakkhuṁ rogato addakkhuṁ bhayato addakkhuṁ,
sn12.66:13.14 te taṇhaṁ pajahiṁsu.
sn12.66:13.15 Ye taṇhaṁ pajahiṁsu te upadhiṁ pajahiṁsu.
sn12.66:13.16 Ye upadhiṁ pajahiṁsu te dukkhaṁ pajahiṁsu.
sn12.66:13.17 Ye dukkhaṁ pajahiṁsu te parimucciṁsu jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi, parimucciṁsu dukkhasmāti vadāmi.
sn12.66:14.1 Yepi hi keci, bhikkhave, anāgatamaddhānaṁ …pe…
sn12.66:14.2 etarahi samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā yaṁ loke piyarūpaṁ sātarūpaṁ taṁ aniccato passanti dukkhato passanti anattato passanti rogato passanti bhayato passanti,
sn12.66:14.3 te taṇhaṁ pajahanti.
sn12.66:14.4 Ye taṇhaṁ pajahanti te upadhiṁ pajahanti.
sn12.66:14.5 Ye upadhiṁ pajahanti te dukkhaṁ pajahanti.
sn12.66:14.6 Ye dukkhaṁ pajahanti te parimuccanti jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi, parimuccanti dukkhasmāti vadāmī”ti.
sn12.66:14.7 Chaṭṭhaṁ. "
sn12.67:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.67
sn12.67:0.2 7. Mahāvagga
sn12.67:0.3 Naḷakalāpīsutta
sn12.67:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ āyasmā ca sāriputto āyasmā ca mahākoṭṭhiko bārāṇasiyaṁ viharanti isipatane migadāye.
sn12.67:1.2 Atha kho āyasmā mahākoṭṭhiko sāyanhasamayaṁ paṭisallānā vuṭṭhito yenāyasmā sāriputto tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā sāriputtena saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn12.67:1.3 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā mahākoṭṭhiko āyasmantaṁ sāriputtaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.67:1.4 “kiṁ nu kho, āvuso sāriputta, sayaṅkataṁ jarāmaraṇaṁ, paraṅkataṁ jarāmaraṇaṁ, sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca jarāmaraṇaṁ, udāhu asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ jarāmaraṇan”ti?
sn12.67:1.5 “Na kho, āvuso koṭṭhika, sayaṅkataṁ jarāmaraṇaṁ, na paraṅkataṁ jarāmaraṇaṁ, na sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca jarāmaraṇaṁ, nāpi asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ jarāmaraṇaṁ.
sn12.67:1.6 Api ca jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇan”ti.
sn12.67:2.1 “Kiṁ nu kho, āvuso sāriputta, sayaṅkatā jāti, paraṅkatā jāti, sayaṅkatā ca paraṅkatā ca jāti, udāhu asayaṅkārā aparaṅkārā adhiccasamuppannā jātī”ti?
sn12.67:2.2 “Na kho, āvuso koṭṭhika, sayaṅkatā jāti, na paraṅkatā jāti, na sayaṅkatā ca paraṅkatā ca jāti, nāpi asayaṅkārā aparaṅkārā adhiccasamuppannā jāti.
sn12.67:2.3 Api ca bhavapaccayā jātī”ti.
sn12.67:3.1 “Kiṁ nu kho, āvuso sāriputta, sayaṅkato bhavo …pe…
sn12.67:3.2 sayaṅkataṁ upādānaṁ …
sn12.67:3.3 sayaṅkatā taṇhā …
sn12.67:3.4 sayaṅkatā vedanā …
sn12.67:3.5 sayaṅkato phasso …
sn12.67:3.6 sayaṅkataṁ saḷāyatanaṁ …
sn12.67:3.7 sayaṅkataṁ nāmarūpaṁ, paraṅkataṁ nāmarūpaṁ, sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca nāmarūpaṁ, udāhu asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ nāmarūpan”ti?
sn12.67:3.8 “Na kho, āvuso koṭṭhika, sayaṅkataṁ nāmarūpaṁ, na paraṅkataṁ nāmarūpaṁ, na sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca nāmarūpaṁ, nāpi asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ, adhiccasamuppannaṁ nāmarūpaṁ.
sn12.67:3.9 Api ca viññāṇapaccayā nāmarūpan”ti.
sn12.67:4.1 “Kiṁ nu kho, āvuso sāriputta, sayaṅkataṁ viññāṇaṁ, paraṅkataṁ viññāṇaṁ, sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca viññāṇaṁ, udāhu asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ viññāṇan”ti?
sn12.67:4.2 “Na kho, āvuso koṭṭhika, sayaṅkataṁ viññāṇaṁ, na paraṅkataṁ viññāṇaṁ, na sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca viññāṇaṁ, nāpi asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ viññāṇaṁ.
sn12.67:4.3 Api ca nāmarūpapaccayā viññāṇan”ti.
sn12.67:5.1 “Idāneva kho mayaṁ āyasmato sāriputtassa bhāsitaṁ evaṁ ājānāma:
sn12.67:5.2 ‘na khvāvuso koṭṭhika, sayaṅkataṁ nāmarūpaṁ, na paraṅkataṁ nāmarūpaṁ, na sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca nāmarūpaṁ, nāpi asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ nāmarūpaṁ.
sn12.67:5.3 Api ca viññāṇapaccayā nāmarūpan’ti.
sn12.67:6.1 Idāneva ca pana mayaṁ āyasmato sāriputtassa bhāsitaṁ evaṁ ājānāma:
sn12.67:6.2 ‘na khvāvuso koṭṭhika, sayaṅkataṁ viññāṇaṁ, na paraṅkataṁ viññāṇaṁ, na sayaṅkatañca paraṅkatañca viññāṇaṁ, nāpi asayaṅkāraṁ aparaṅkāraṁ adhiccasamuppannaṁ viññāṇaṁ.
sn12.67:6.3 Api ca nāmarūpapaccayā viññāṇan’ti.
sn12.67:7.1 Yathā kathaṁ panāvuso sāriputta, imassa bhāsitassa attho daṭṭhabbo”ti?
sn12.67:7.2 “Tenahāvuso, upamaṁ te karissāmi.
sn12.67:7.3 Upamāyapidhekacce viññū purisā bhāsitassa atthaṁ jānanti.
sn12.67:7.4 Seyyathāpi, āvuso, dve naḷakalāpiyo aññamaññaṁ nissāya tiṭṭheyyuṁ.
sn12.67:7.5 Evameva kho, āvuso, nāmarūpapaccayā viññāṇaṁ;
sn12.67:7.6 viññāṇapaccayā nāmarūpaṁ;
sn12.67:7.7 nāmarūpapaccayā saḷāyatanaṁ;
sn12.67:7.8 saḷāyatanapaccayā phasso …pe…
sn12.67:7.9 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.
sn12.67:7.10 Tāsañce, āvuso, naḷakalāpīnaṁ ekaṁ ākaḍḍheyya, ekā papateyya;
sn12.67:7.11 aparañce ākaḍḍheyya, aparā papateyya.
sn12.67:7.12 Evameva kho, āvuso, nāmarūpanirodhā viññāṇanirodho;
sn12.67:7.13 viññāṇanirodhā nāmarūpanirodho;
sn12.67:7.14 nāmarūpanirodhā saḷāyatananirodho;
sn12.67:7.15 saḷāyatananirodhā phassanirodho …pe…
sn12.67:7.16 evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa nirodho hotī”ti.
sn12.67:8.1 “Acchariyaṁ, āvuso sāriputta;
sn12.67:8.2 abbhutaṁ, āvuso sāriputta.
sn12.67:8.3 Yāvasubhāsitañcidaṁ āyasmatā sāriputtena.
sn12.67:8.4 Idañca pana mayaṁ āyasmato sāriputtassa bhāsitaṁ imehi chattiṁsāya vatthūhi anumodāma:
sn12.67:9.1 ‘Jarāmaraṇassa ce, āvuso, bhikkhu nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya dhammaṁ deseti, dhammakathiko bhikkhūti alaṁvacanāya.
sn12.67:9.2 Jarāmaraṇassa ce, āvuso, bhikkhu nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya paṭipanno hoti, dhammānudhammappaṭipanno bhikkhūti alaṁvacanāya.
sn12.67:9.3 Jarāmaraṇassa ce, āvuso, bhikkhu nibbidā virāgā nirodhā anupādā vimutto hoti, diṭṭhadhammanibbānappatto bhikkhūti alaṁvacanāya.
sn12.67:9.4 Jātiyā ce …
sn12.67:9.5 bhavassa ce …
sn12.67:9.6 upādānassa ce …
sn12.67:9.7 taṇhāya ce …
sn12.67:9.8 vedanāya ce …
sn12.67:9.9 phassassa ce …
sn12.67:9.10 saḷāyatanassa ce …
sn12.67:9.11 nāmarūpassa ce …
sn12.67:9.12 viññāṇassa ce …
sn12.67:9.13 saṅkhārānañce …
sn12.67:9.14 avijjāya ce, āvuso, bhikkhu nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya dhammaṁ deseti, dhammakathiko bhikkhūti alaṁvacanāya.
sn12.67:9.15 Avijjāya ce, āvuso, bhikkhu nibbidāya virāgāya nirodhāya paṭipanno hoti, dhammānudhammappaṭipanno bhikkhūti alaṁvacanāya.
sn12.67:9.16 Avijjāya ce, āvuso, bhikkhu nibbidā virāgā nirodhā anupādā vimutto hoti, diṭṭhadhammanibbānappatto bhikkhūti alaṁvacanāyā’”ti.
sn12.67:9.17 Sattamaṁ. "

sn12.68:1.1 Ekaṁ samayaṁ āyasmā ca musilo āyasmā ca paviṭṭho āyasmā ca nārado āyasmā ca ānando kosambiyaṁ viharanti ghositārāme.

sn12.68:1.3 “aññatreva, āvuso musila, saddhāya aññatra ruciyā aññatra anussavā aññatra ākāraparivitakkā aññatra diṭṭhinijjhānakkhantiyā atthāyasmato musilassa paccattameva ñāṇaṁ:
sn12.68:1.4 ‘jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇan’”ti?
sn12.68:1.5 “Aññatreva, āvuso paviṭṭha, saddhāya aññatra ruciyā aññatra anussavā aññatra ākāraparivitakkā aññatra diṭṭhinijjhānakkhantiyā ahametaṁ jānāmi ahametaṁ passāmi:

sn12.68:2.4 taṇhāpaccayā upādānanti …
sn12.68:2.5 vedanāpaccayā taṇhāti …

sn12.68:2.10 saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇanti …
sn12.68:2.11 avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā’”ti?
sn12.68:2.12 “Aññatreva, āvuso paviṭṭha, saddhāya aññatra ruciyā aññatra anussavā aññatra ākāraparivitakkā aññatra diṭṭhinijjhānakkhantiyā ahametaṁ jānāmi ahametaṁ passāmi:
sn12.68:2.13 ‘avijjāpaccayā saṅkhārā’”ti.

sn12.68:3.3 “Aññatreva, āvuso paviṭṭha, saddhāya aññatra ruciyā aññatra anussavā aññatra ākāraparivitakkā aññatra diṭṭhinijjhānakkhantiyā ahametaṁ jānāmi ahametaṁ passāmi:
sn12.68:3.4 ‘jātinirodhā jarāmaraṇanirodho’”ti.
sn12.68:4.1 “Aññatreva, āvuso musila, saddhāya aññatra ruciyā aññatra anussavā aññatra ākāraparivitakkā aññatra diṭṭhinijjhānakkhantiyā atthāyasmato musilassa paccattameva ñāṇaṁ:

sn12.68:4.3 upādānanirodhā bhavanirodhoti …
sn12.68:4.4 taṇhānirodhā upādānanirodhoti …

sn12.68:12.4 ‘bhavanirodho nibbānan’”ti.
sn12.68:13.1 “Tenahāyasmā nārado arahaṁ khīṇāsavo”ti?
sn12.68:13.2 “‘Bhavanirodho nibbānan’ti kho me, āvuso, yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṁ, na camhi arahaṁ khīṇāsavo.
sn12.68:13.3 Seyyathāpi, āvuso, kantāramagge udapāno, tatra nevassa rajju na udakavārako.
sn12.68:13.4 Atha puriso āgaccheyya ghammābhitatto ghammapareto kilanto tasito pipāsito, so taṁ udapānaṁ olokeyya.
sn12.68:13.5 Tassa ‘udakan’ti hi kho ñāṇaṁ assa, na ca kāyena phusitvā vihareyya.
sn12.68:13.6 Evameva kho, āvuso, ‘bhavanirodho nibbānan’ti yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṁ, na camhi arahaṁ khīṇāsavo”ti.
sn12.68:14.1 Evaṁ vutte, āyasmā ānando āyasmantaṁ paviṭṭhaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.68:14.2 “evaṁvādī tvaṁ, āvuso paviṭṭha, āyasmantaṁ nāradaṁ kiṁ vadesī”ti?
sn12.68:14.3 “Evaṁvādāhaṁ, āvuso ānanda, āyasmantaṁ nāradaṁ na kiñci vadāmi aññatra kalyāṇā aññatra kusalā”ti.
sn12.68:14.4 Aṭṭhamaṁ. "
sn12.69:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.69
sn12.69:0.2 7. Mahāvagga
sn12.69:0.3 Upayantisutta
sn12.69:1.1 Evaṁ me sutaṁ—
sn12.69:1.2 ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.
sn12.69:1.3 Tatra kho …pe…
sn12.69:1.4 “mahāsamuddo, bhikkhave, upayanto mahānadiyo upayāpeti, mahānadiyo upayantiyo kunnadiyo upayāpenti, kunnadiyo upayantiyo mahāsobbhe upayāpenti, mahāsobbhā upayantā kusobbhe upayāpenti.
sn12.69:1.5 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, avijjā upayantī saṅkhāre upayāpeti, saṅkhārā upayantā viññāṇaṁ upayāpenti, viññāṇaṁ upayantaṁ nāmarūpaṁ upayāpeti, nāmarūpaṁ upayantaṁ saḷāyatanaṁ upayāpeti, saḷāyatanaṁ upayantaṁ phassaṁ upayāpeti, phasso upayanto vedanaṁ upayāpeti, vedanā upayantī taṇhaṁ upayāpeti, taṇhā upayantī upādānaṁ upayāpeti, upādānaṁ upayantaṁ bhavaṁ upayāpeti, bhavo upayanto jātiṁ upayāpeti, jāti upayantī jarāmaraṇaṁ upayāpeti.
sn12.69:2.1 Mahāsamuddo, bhikkhave, apayanto mahānadiyo apayāpeti, mahānadiyo apayantiyo kunnadiyo apayāpenti, kunnadiyo apayantiyo mahāsobbhe apayāpenti, mahāsobbhā apayantā kusobbhe apayāpenti.
sn12.69:2.2 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, avijjā apayantī saṅkhāre apayāpeti, saṅkhārā apayantā viññāṇaṁ apayāpenti, viññāṇaṁ apayantaṁ nāmarūpaṁ apayāpeti, nāmarūpaṁ apayantaṁ saḷāyatanaṁ apayāpeti, saḷāyatanaṁ apayantaṁ phassaṁ apayāpeti, phasso apayanto vedanaṁ apayāpeti, vedanā apayantī taṇhaṁ apayāpeti, taṇhā apayantī upādānaṁ apayāpeti, upādānaṁ apayantaṁ bhavaṁ apayāpeti, bhavo apayanto jātiṁ apayāpeti, jāti apayantī jarāmaraṇaṁ apayāpetī”ti.
sn12.69:2.3 Navamaṁ. "
sn12.70:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.70
sn12.70:0.2 7. Mahāvagga
sn12.70:0.3 Susimaparibbājakasutta
sn12.70:1.1 Evaṁ me sutaṁ—
sn12.70:1.2 ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe.
sn12.70:1.3 Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā sakkato hoti garukato mānito pūjito apacito lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātasenāsanagilānappaccayabhesajjaparikkhārānaṁ.
sn12.70:1.4 Bhikkhusaṅghopi sakkato hoti garukato mānito pūjito apacito lābhī cīvarapiṇḍapātasenāsanagilānappaccayabhesajjaparikkhārānaṁ.
sn12.70:1.5 Aññatitthiyā pana paribbājakā asakkatā honti agarukatā amānitā apūjitā anapacitā, na lābhino cīvarapiṇḍapātasenāsanagilānappaccayabhesajjaparikkhārānaṁ.
sn12.70:2.1 Tena kho pana samayena susimo paribbājako rājagahe paṭivasati mahatiyā paribbājakaparisāya saddhiṁ.
sn12.70:2.2 Atha kho susimassa paribbājakassa parisā susimaṁ paribbājakaṁ etadavocuṁ:
sn12.70:2.3 “ehi tvaṁ, āvuso susima, samaṇe gotame brahmacariyaṁ cara.
sn12.70:2.4 Tvaṁ dhammaṁ pariyāpuṇitvā amhe vāceyyāsi.
sn12.70:2.5 Taṁ mayaṁ dhammaṁ pariyāpuṇitvā gihīnaṁ bhāsissāma.
sn12.70:2.6 Evaṁ mayampi sakkatā bhavissāma garukatā mānitā pūjitā apacitā lābhino cīvarapiṇḍapātasenāsanagilānappaccayabhesajjaparikkhārānan”ti.
sn12.70:2.7 “Evamāvuso”ti kho susimo paribbājako sakāya parisāya paṭissuṇitvā yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmatā ānandena saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn12.70:2.8 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho susimo paribbājako āyasmantaṁ ānandaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.70:2.9 “icchāmahaṁ, āvuso ānanda, imasmiṁ dhammavinaye brahmacariyaṁ caritun”ti.
sn12.70:3.1 Atha kho āyasmā ānando susimaṁ paribbājakaṁ ādāya yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā ānando bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.70:3.2 “ayaṁ, bhante, susimo paribbājako evamāha:
sn12.70:3.3 ‘icchāmahaṁ, āvuso ānanda, imasmiṁ dhammavinaye brahmacariyaṁ caritun’”ti.
sn12.70:3.4 “Tenahānanda, susimaṁ pabbājethā”ti.
sn12.70:3.5 Alattha kho susimo paribbājako bhagavato santike pabbajjaṁ, alattha upasampadaṁ.
sn12.70:4.1 Tena kho pana samayena sambahulehi bhikkhūhi bhagavato santike aññā byākatā hoti:
sn12.70:4.2 “khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyāti pajānāmā”ti.
sn12.70:4.3 Assosi kho āyasmā susimo:
sn12.70:4.4 “sambahulehi kira bhikkhūhi bhagavato santike aññā byākatā:
sn12.70:4.5 ‘khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānāmā”ti.
sn12.70:4.6 Atha kho āyasmā susimo yena te bhikkhū tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā tehi bhikkhūhi saddhiṁ sammodi.
sn12.70:4.7 Sammodanīyaṁ kathaṁ sāraṇīyaṁ vītisāretvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi. Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā susimo te bhikkhū etadavoca:
sn12.70:4.8 “saccaṁ kirāyasmantehi bhagavato santike aññā byākatā:
sn12.70:4.9 ‘khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānāmā”ti?
sn12.70:4.10 “Evamāvuso”ti.
sn12.70:5.1 “Api pana tumhe āyasmanto evaṁ jānantā evaṁ passantā anekavihitaṁ iddhividhaṁ paccanubhotha—ekopi hutvā bahudhā hotha, bahudhāpi hutvā eko hotha; āvibhāvaṁ, tirobhāvaṁ, tirokuṭṭaṁ tiropākāraṁ tiropabbataṁ asajjamānā gacchatha, seyyathāpi ākāse; pathaviyāpi ummujjanimujjaṁ karotha, seyyathāpi udake; udakepi abhijjamāne gacchatha, seyyathāpi pathaviyaṁ; ākāsepi pallaṅkena kamatha, seyyathāpi pakkhī sakuṇo; imepi candimasūriye evaṁmahiddhike evaṁmahānubhāve pāṇinā parimasatha parimajjatha, yāva brahmalokāpi kāyena vasaṁ vattethā”ti?
sn12.70:5.2 “No hetaṁ, āvuso”.
sn12.70:6.1 “Api pana tumhe āyasmanto evaṁ jānantā evaṁ passantā dibbāya sotadhātuyā visuddhāya atikkantamānusikāya ubho sadde suṇātha dibbe ca mānuse ca ye dūre santike cā”ti?
sn12.70:6.2 “No hetaṁ, āvuso”.
sn12.70:7.1 “Api pana tumhe āyasmanto evaṁ jānantā evaṁ passantā parasattānaṁ parapuggalānaṁ cetasā ceto paricca pajānātha—
sn12.70:7.2 sarāgaṁ vā cittaṁ sarāgaṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.3 vītarāgaṁ vā cittaṁ vītarāgaṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.4 sadosaṁ vā cittaṁ sadosaṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.5 vītadosaṁ vā cittaṁ vītadosaṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.6 samohaṁ vā cittaṁ samohaṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.7 vītamohaṁ vā cittaṁ vītamohaṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.8 saṅkhittaṁ vā cittaṁ saṅkhittaṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.9 vikkhittaṁ vā cittaṁ vikkhittaṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.10 mahaggataṁ vā cittaṁ mahaggataṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.11 amahaggataṁ vā cittaṁ amahaggataṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.12 sauttaraṁ vā cittaṁ sauttaraṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.13 anuttaraṁ vā cittaṁ anuttaraṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.14 samāhitaṁ vā cittaṁ samāhitaṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.15 asamāhitaṁ vā cittaṁ asamāhitaṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.16 vimuttaṁ vā cittaṁ vimuttaṁ cittanti pajānātha;
sn12.70:7.17 avimuttaṁ vā cittaṁ avimuttaṁ cittanti pajānāthā”ti?
sn12.70:7.18 “No hetaṁ, āvuso”.
sn12.70:8.1 “Api pana tumhe āyasmanto evaṁ jānantā evaṁ passantā anekavihitaṁ pubbenivāsaṁ anussaratha, seyyathidaṁ—ekampi jātiṁ dvepi jātiyo tissopi jātiyo catassopi jātiyo pañcapi jātiyo dasapi jātiyo vīsampi jātiyo tiṁsampi jātiyo cattārīsampi jātiyo paññāsampi jātiyo jātisatampi jātisahassampi jātisatasahassampi, anekepi saṁvaṭṭakappe anekepi vivaṭṭakappe anekepi saṁvaṭṭavivaṭṭakappe: ‘amutrāsiṁ evaṁnāmo evaṅgotto evaṁvaṇṇo evamāhāro evaṁsukhadukkhapaṭisaṁvedī evamāyupariyanto, so tato cuto amutra udapādiṁ; tatrāpāsiṁ evaṁnāmo evaṅgotto evaṁvaṇṇo evamāhāro evaṁsukhadukkhapaṭisaṁvedī evamāyupariyanto, so tato cuto idhūpapanno’ti. Iti sākāraṁ sauddesaṁ anekavihitaṁ pubbenivāsaṁ anussarathā”ti?
sn12.70:8.2 “No hetaṁ, āvuso”.
sn12.70:9.1 “Api pana tumhe āyasmanto evaṁ jānantā evaṁ passantā dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena satte passatha cavamāne upapajjamāne hīne paṇīte suvaṇṇe dubbaṇṇe, sugate duggate yathākammūpage satte pajānātha: ‘ime vata bhonto sattā kāyaduccaritena samannāgatā vacīduccaritena samannāgatā manoduccaritena samannāgatā, ariyānaṁ upavādakā micchādiṭṭhikā micchādiṭṭhikammasamādānā, te kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā apāyaṁ duggatiṁ vinipātaṁ nirayaṁ upapannā; ime vā pana bhonto sattā kāyasucaritena samannāgatā vacīsucaritena samannāgatā manosucaritena samannāgatā, ariyānaṁ anupavādakā sammādiṭṭhikā sammādiṭṭhikammasamādānā te kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā sugatiṁ saggaṁ lokaṁ upapannā’ti, iti dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena satte passatha cavamāne upapajjamāne hīne paṇīte suvaṇṇe dubbaṇṇe, sugate duggate yathākammūpage satte pajānāthā”ti?
sn12.70:9.2 “No hetaṁ, āvuso”.
sn12.70:10.1 “Api pana tumhe āyasmanto evaṁ jānantā evaṁ passantā ye te santā vimokkhā atikkamma rūpe āruppā, te kāyena phusitvā viharathā”ti?
sn12.70:10.2 “No hetaṁ, āvuso”.
sn12.70:11.1 “Ettha dāni āyasmanto idañca veyyākaraṇaṁ imesañca dhammānaṁ asamāpatti; idaṁ no, āvuso, kathan”ti?
sn12.70:11.2 “Paññāvimuttā kho mayaṁ, āvuso susimā”ti.
sn12.70:12.1 “Na khvāhaṁ imassa āyasmantānaṁ saṅkhittena bhāsitassa vitthārena atthaṁ ājānāmi.
sn12.70:12.2 Sādhu me āyasmanto tathā bhāsantu yathāhaṁ imassa āyasmantānaṁ saṅkhittena bhāsitassa vitthārena atthaṁ ājāneyyan”ti.
sn12.70:12.3 “Ājāneyyāsi vā tvaṁ, āvuso susima, na vā tvaṁ ājāneyyāsi atha kho paññāvimuttā mayan”ti.
sn12.70:13.1 Atha kho āyasmā susimo uṭṭhāyāsanā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṁ abhivādetvā ekamantaṁ nisīdi.
sn12.70:13.2 Ekamantaṁ nisinno kho āyasmā susimo yāvatako tehi bhikkhūhi saddhiṁ ahosi kathāsallāpo taṁ sabbaṁ bhagavato ārocesi.
sn12.70:13.3 “Pubbe kho, susima, dhammaṭṭhitiñāṇaṁ, pacchā nibbāne ñāṇan”ti.
sn12.70:14.1 “Na khvāhaṁ, bhante, imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena bhāsitassa vitthārena atthaṁ ājānāmi.
sn12.70:14.2 Sādhu me, bhante, bhagavā tathā bhāsatu yathāhaṁ imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena bhāsitassa vitthārena atthaṁ ājāneyyan”ti.
sn12.70:14.3 “Ājāneyyāsi vā tvaṁ, susima, na vā tvaṁ ājāneyyāsi, atha kho dhammaṭṭhitiñāṇaṁ pubbe, pacchā nibbāne ñāṇaṁ.
sn12.70:15.1 Taṁ kiṁ maññasi, susima,
sn12.70:15.2 rūpaṁ niccaṁ vā aniccaṁ vā”ti?

sn12.70:15.5 “Dukkhaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.70:15.6 “Yaṁ panāniccaṁ dukkhaṁ vipariṇāmadhammaṁ, kallaṁ nu taṁ samanupassituṁ:

sn12.70:16.1 “Tasmātiha, susima, yaṁ kiñci rūpaṁ atītānāgatapaccuppannaṁ ajjhattaṁ vā bahiddhā vā oḷārikaṁ vā sukhumaṁ vā hīnaṁ vā paṇītaṁ vā yaṁ dūre santike vā, sabbaṁ rūpaṁ netaṁ mama nesohamasmi na meso attāti; evametaṁ yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya daṭṭhabbaṁ.
sn12.70:16.2 Yā kāci vedanā atītānāgatapaccuppannā ajjhattaṁ vā bahiddhā vā oḷārikā vā sukhumā vā hīnā vā paṇītā vā yā dūre santike vā, sabbā vedanā netaṁ mama nesohamasmi na meso attāti; evametaṁ yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya daṭṭhabbaṁ.
sn12.70:16.3 Yā kāci saññā …pe…

sn12.70:16.5 Yaṁ kiñci viññāṇaṁ atītānāgatapaccuppannaṁ ajjhattaṁ vā bahiddhā vā oḷārikaṁ vā sukhumaṁ vā hīnaṁ vā paṇītaṁ vā yaṁ dūre santike vā, sabbaṁ viññāṇaṁ netaṁ mama nesohamasmi na meso attāti; evametaṁ yathābhūtaṁ sammappaññāya daṭṭhabbaṁ.
sn12.70:17.1 Evaṁ passaṁ, susima, sutavā ariyasāvako rūpasmimpi nibbindati, vedanāyapi nibbindati, saññāyapi nibbindati, saṅkhāresupi nibbindati, viññāṇasmimpi nibbindati.
sn12.70:17.2 Nibbindaṁ virajjati, virāgā vimuccati, vimuttasmiṁ vimuttamiti ñāṇaṁ hoti.
sn12.70:17.3 ‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṁ brahmacariyaṁ, kataṁ karaṇīyaṁ, nāparaṁ itthattāyā’ti pajānāti.
sn12.70:18.1 ‘Jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇan’ti, susima, passasī”ti?

sn12.70:20.1 “Api pana tvaṁ, susima, evaṁ jānanto evaṁ passanto anekavihitaṁ iddhividhaṁ paccanubhosi—ekopi hutvā bahudhā hosi, bahudhāpi hutvā eko hosi; āvibhāvaṁ, tirobhāvaṁ, tirokuṭṭaṁ tiropākāraṁ tiropabbataṁ asajjamāno gacchasi, seyyathāpi ākāse; pathaviyāpi ummujjanimujjaṁ karosi, seyyathāpi udake; udakepi abhijjamāno gacchasi, seyyathāpi pathaviyaṁ; ākāsepi pallaṅkena kamasi, seyyathāpi pakkhī sakuṇo; imepi candimasūriye evaṁmahiddhike evaṁmahānubhāve pāṇinā parimasasi parimajjasi, yāva brahmalokāpi kāyena vasaṁ vattesī”ti?
sn12.70:20.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.70:21.1 “Api pana tvaṁ, susima, evaṁ jānanto evaṁ passanto dibbāya sotadhātuyā visuddhāya atikkantamānusikāya ubho sadde suṇasi dibbe ca mānuse ca ye dūre santike cā”ti?
sn12.70:21.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.

sn12.70:23.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.70:24.1 “Api pana tvaṁ, susima, evaṁ jānanto evaṁ passanto dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena satte passasi cavamāne …pe… yathākammūpage satte pajānāsī”ti?
sn12.70:24.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.70:25.1 “Api pana tvaṁ, susima, evaṁ jānanto evaṁ passanto ye te santā vimokkhā atikkamma rūpe āruppā, te kāyena phusitvā viharasī”ti?
sn12.70:25.2 “No hetaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.70:26.1 “Ettha dāni, susima, idañca veyyākaraṇaṁ imesañca dhammānaṁ asamāpatti, idaṁ no, susima, kathan”ti?
sn12.70:27.1 Atha kho āyasmā susimo bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipatitvā bhagavantaṁ etadavoca:
sn12.70:27.2 “accayo maṁ, bhante, accagamā yathābālaṁ yathāmūḷhaṁ yathāakusalaṁ, yvāhaṁ evaṁ svākkhāte dhammavinaye dhammatthenako pabbajito.
sn12.70:27.3 Tassa me, bhante, bhagavā accayaṁ accayato paṭiggaṇhātu āyatiṁ saṁvarāyā”ti.
sn12.70:28.1 “Taggha tvaṁ, susima, accayo accagamā yathābālaṁ yathāmūḷhaṁ yathāakusalaṁ, yo tvaṁ evaṁ svākkhāte dhammavinaye dhammatthenako pabbajito.
sn12.70:28.2 Seyyathāpi, susima, coraṁ āgucāriṁ gahetvā rañño dasseyyuṁ:
sn12.70:28.3 ‘ayaṁ te, deva, coro āgucārī, imassa yaṁ icchasi taṁ daṇḍaṁ paṇehī’ti.
sn12.70:28.4 Tamenaṁ rājā evaṁ vadeyya:
sn12.70:28.5 ‘gacchatha, bho, imaṁ purisaṁ daḷhāya rajjuyā pacchābāhaṁ gāḷhabandhanaṁ bandhitvā khuramuṇḍaṁ karitvā kharassarena paṇavena rathiyāya rathiyaṁ siṅghāṭakena siṅghāṭakaṁ parinetvā dakkhiṇena dvārena nikkhāmetvā dakkhiṇato nagarassa sīsaṁ chindathā’ti.
sn12.70:28.6 Tamenaṁ rañño purisā daḷhāya rajjuyā pacchābāhaṁ gāḷhabandhanaṁ bandhitvā khuramuṇḍaṁ karitvā kharassarena paṇavena rathiyāya rathiyaṁ siṅghāṭakena siṅghāṭakaṁ parinetvā dakkhiṇena dvārena nikkhāmetvā dakkhiṇato nagarassa sīsaṁ chindeyyuṁ.
sn12.70:28.7 Taṁ kiṁ maññasi, susima,
sn12.70:28.8 api nu so puriso tatonidānaṁ dukkhaṁ domanassaṁ paṭisaṁvediyethā”ti?
sn12.70:28.9 “Evaṁ, bhante”.
sn12.70:29.1 “Yaṁ kho so, susima, puriso tatonidānaṁ dukkhaṁ domanassaṁ paṭisaṁvediyetha.
sn12.70:29.2 Yā evaṁ svākkhāte dhammavinaye dhammatthenakassa pabbajjā, ayaṁ tato dukkhavipākatarā ca kaṭukavipākatarā ca, api ca vinipātāya saṁvattati.
sn12.70:29.3 Yato ca kho tvaṁ, susima, accayaṁ accayato disvā yathādhammaṁ paṭikarosi taṁ te mayaṁ paṭiggaṇhāma.
sn12.70:29.4 Vuddhi hesā, susima, ariyassa vinaye yo accayaṁ accayato disvā yathādhammaṁ paṭikaroti, āyatiñca saṁvaraṁ āpajjatī”ti.
sn12.70:29.5 Dasamaṁ.
sn12.70:29.6 Mahāvaggo sattamo.

sn12.70:30.4 sammasaṁ naḷakalāpiyaṁ;

sn12.71:0.2 8. Samaṇabrāhmaṇavagga
sn12.71:0.3 Jarāmaraṇasutta
sn12.71:1.1 Evaṁ me sutaṁ—
sn12.71:1.2 ekaṁ samayaṁ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.
sn12.71:1.3 Tatra kho bhagavā …pe…
sn12.71:1.4 “ye hi keci, bhikkhave, samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā jarāmaraṇaṁ nappajānanti, jarāmaraṇasamudayaṁ nappajānanti, jarāmaraṇanirodhaṁ nappajānanti, jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ nappajānanti,
sn12.71:1.5 na me te, bhikkhave, samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samaṇesu vā samaṇasammatā brāhmaṇesu vā brāhmaṇasammatā, na ca pana te āyasmanto sāmaññatthaṁ vā brahmaññatthaṁ vā diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharanti.
sn12.71:2.1 Ye ca kho keci, bhikkhave, samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā jarāmaraṇaṁ pajānanti …pe… paṭipadaṁ pajānanti,
sn12.71:2.2 te kho me, bhikkhave, samaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā samaṇesu ceva samaṇasammatā brāhmaṇesu ca brāhmaṇasammatā, te ca panāyasmanto sāmaññatthañca brahmaññatthañca diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharantī”ti.
sn12.71:2.3 (Suttanto eko.)
sn12.71:2.4 Paṭhamaṁ. "

sn12.72-81:12.4 Aṭṭhamo samaṇabrāhmaṇoti. "
sn12.82:0.1 Saṁyutta Nikāya 12.82
sn12.82:0.2 9. Antarapeyyāla
sn12.82:0.3 Satthusutta
sn12.82:1.1 Sāvatthiyaṁ viharati.
sn12.82:1.2 “Jarāmaraṇaṁ, bhikkhave, ajānatā apassatā yathābhūtaṁ jarāmaraṇe yathābhūtaṁ ñāṇāya satthā pariyesitabbo;
sn12.82:1.3 jarāmaraṇasamudayaṁ ajānatā apassatā yathābhūtaṁ jarāmaraṇasamudaye yathābhūtaṁ ñāṇāya satthā pariyesitabbo;
sn12.82:1.4 jarāmaraṇanirodhaṁ ajānatā apassatā yathābhūtaṁ jarāmaraṇanirodhe yathābhūtaṁ ñāṇāya satthā pariyesitabbo;
sn12.82:1.5 jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ ajānatā apassatā yathābhūtaṁ jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya yathābhūtaṁ ñāṇāya satthā pariyesitabbo”ti.
sn12.82:1.6 (Suttanto eko.)
sn12.82:1.7 Paṭhamaṁ.
sn12.82:1.8 (Sabbesaṁ peyyālo evaṁ vitthāretabbo.) "

sn12.203-213:2.0 Tassuddānaṁ
sn12.203-213:2.1 Satthā sikkhā ca yogo ca,
sn12.203-213:2.2 chando ussoḷhipañcamī;

sn12.203-213:3.2 suttā dvattiṁsa satāni;

sn12.203-213:3.4 peyyālaantaramhi yeti.
